# CLAUDE.md

> **Stale-worktree protocol — FIRST ACTION OF EVERY FRESH SESSION.**
>
> **Parent first, worktree second.** The parent repo's local `main` needs to track `origin/main` so future worktrees inherit fresh state; THEN the worktree's branch rebases on `origin/main` to pick up everything since spawn. Skipping the parent step fixes the current worktree but leaves the next worktree spawn on the same stale base.
>
> ```
> git -C /Users/stefan/t9l-website fetch --all --prune
> git -C /Users/stefan/t9l-website pull --ff-only origin main
> git rebase origin/main   # in the worktree
> ```
>
> Every Claude Code session is spawned in a worktree branched off the parent repo's *local* `main`, which routinely lags behind `origin/main` as PRs merge upstream. The worktree's HEAD on session start is therefore frequently weeks behind reality. Without the rebase, the entire CLAUDE.md / file structure / git log / dependency surface you observe is a stale snapshot — diagnostics like "the file the plan references doesn't exist" can be artifacts of the lag, not real prompt injection. Multiple prior sessions have flagged plan inputs as fictional and stopped, when in fact rebasing onto `origin/main` revealed all the referenced files were already shipped.
>
> **Procedure:**
> 1. **Fast-forward the parent's `main` to `origin/main` first** via the `git -C` commands above. If `pull --ff-only` fails (parent has uncommitted changes, or local `main` has diverged from `origin/main`), STOP and surface to the user. Do NOT force, do NOT `reset --hard`, do NOT switch branches inside the parent — divergent parent state means the operator has uncommitted work or an in-progress branch and needs to resolve manually.
> 2. **Then rebase the worktree onto `origin/main`.** Run *before* any reading or analysis of the briefing — do not skip even if the parent message looks self-contained.
> 3. **If `git rebase` reports conflicts in the worktree, STOP and surface to the user.** Do not attempt to resolve, force, abort-and-reset, or otherwise paper over divergent state — the conflict means the orchestrator gave the worktree commits that diverge from upstream, and the right move is operator intervention.
> 4. **If both succeed (or are no-op fast-forwards), proceed with the task as briefed.** Re-read CLAUDE.md from scratch — frontmatter, file structure, ledger — because everything you "remembered" from the pre-rebase state may be wrong.
> 5. **If the rebase reveals files / tags / version constants the briefing references that you previously couldn't see, that's the expected path — execute the briefing.** A briefing matching post-rebase state is the strongest signal it's legitimate, not the weakest.
>
> This rule exists because diagnostic agents have repeatedly mis-classified legitimate work as prompt injection on the basis of a stale worktree. The cost of pausing to rebase is seconds; the cost of refusing real work in front of a backlog of merged PRs is multi-session drag.
>
> **Current release:** v1.49.0 — **Server-side session hydration: eliminate the post-paint auth-UI flash.** User-reported perf bug: when an authenticated user landed on `/`, the auth-aware UI elements (`UserTeamBadge` "your team is X", `RsvpBar` with playerId-driven controls, `Submit Goal` CTA, header logged-in dropdown) appeared 300ms-1s after the page painted, on a noticeable lag. Pre-v1.49.0 root cause: [`src/app/layout.tsx`](src/app/layout.tsx) was a synchronous server component that mounted `<SessionProvider>` (via [`src/components/AuthProvider.tsx`](src/components/AuthProvider.tsx)) with no `session` prop, so `SessionProvider` fired a client-side `GET /api/auth/session` round-trip on mount to populate the session. While in flight, every `useSession()` consumer (Dashboard, UserTeamBadge, RsvpBar, NextMatchdayBanner, GuestLoginBanner, LineLoginButton, RsvpButton, TopPerformers, LeagueTable, AssignPlayerClient — 11 client components) returned `{ data: undefined, status: 'loading' }`. Initial paint showed the unauthenticated shell; the round-trip resolved (300ms warm baseline measured against prod, multi-second cold) and triggered a re-render with the auth-aware UI. **The fix is the canonical NextAuth pattern** (documented at next-auth.js.org): make the layout async, call `getServerSession(authOptions)` at the layout boundary, pass the resolved session to `<SessionProvider session={...}>`. The session prop seeds the provider so `useSession()` returns the correct value synchronously on first render — no client round-trip, no flash. **Why TTFB doesn't compound:** Next.js automatically parallelizes layout + page on the same request, and the page (`app/page.tsx`) was already async via `getLeagueIdFromRequest()` + `getPublicLeagueData()`. The JWT callback runs in parallel with `getPublicLeagueData`, so total wall-clock TTFB stays ~max(layout, page) ≈ unchanged. Total time-to-correct-UI on the warm path drops from "~500ms paint + 300ms session round-trip = 800ms" to "~500-800ms paint with correct UI baked in" — same wall-clock, no flash. On cold the win is larger because the JWT callback's cold-start cost is amortized into the page paint (which was cold-starting anyway) instead of stacking on top. **Why `<AuthProvider>` accepts `session` as an optional prop:** `<AuthProvider>` is a thin `'use client'` wrapper around `<SessionProvider>`; making the prop required would force every test that mounts the provider to supply a session, but `<SessionProvider>` itself accepts `undefined` (its documented fallback is to fetch). Optional prop preserves the test seam. **Tests:** new [`tests/unit/sessionHydration.test.ts`](tests/unit/sessionHydration.test.ts) (11 cases pinning the call shape across both files — `getServerSession` import + `authOptions` import + `async function RootLayout` + `await getServerSession(authOptions)` + `<AuthProvider session={session}>`; AuthProvider `session?:` prop + forwards to `<SessionProvider session={session}>`; explicit regression target asserting `<SessionProvider>{children}` shape is gone — would fail if a future PR drops the prop). Stash-pop sanity check confirmed: reverting the layout + AuthProvider fails 9/11 (regression catches the broken behavior). 1212 passed | 2 skipped (1201 baseline + 11 new — sessionHydration cases). Type-check clean. Local `npx next build` clean (Next 16 / Turbopack — every route was already dynamic per host-header reads in `app/page.tsx` etc., so adding `getServerSession` to the layout doesn't introduce new dynamic surface). Minor bump (1.48.1 → 1.49.0) — meaningful UX behavior change (auth-aware UI no longer flashes in post-paint). **Out of scope:** further JWT-callback latency optimization. Audit confirmed the JWT callback path is already as tight as it can be (Redis-canonical with sliding TTL per v1.5.0/v1.26.0 + per-league key + tri-state hit/miss/error handling). The remaining cost is the Redis round-trip itself (~50-100ms warm; cold-Upstash variability) plus serverless cold-start; both are infra costs that v1.49.0 doesn't add but inherits.
>
> v1.48.1 — **Submit-Goal CTA singleton across matchday changes + bold matchday label in modal.** Patch follow-up to v1.48.0. **Bug 1 — CTA "spawning infinitely on scroll":** v1.48.0 mounted the Submit-Goal CTA inside the homepage Dashboard with `<SubmitGoalForm key={selectedMatchday.id} ...>` (Dashboard.tsx:152). The `key` forced a full unmount + remount on every matchday swipe; combined with the Google-Translate script wired in the root layout (which mutates DOM nodes in place to swap English↔Japanese text), React's reconciler and Google Translate's DOM mutations collide each time a keyed subtree remounts, producing visible "ghost" CTAs that appear to multiply as the user scrolls/swipes between matchdays. v1.48.1 drops the `key` so `<SubmitGoalForm>` becomes a singleton whose props update across swipes — never remounts, never collides with Google Translate's mutated tree. Two new internal effects keep the singleton state clean: (a) a `useEffect(() => { setOpen(false); setSuccess(false); }, [matchday.id])` in `SubmitGoalForm` so a previously-open modal doesn't linger after the user swipes (e.g. opened for MD2, swiped to MD3, modal closes); (b) a `useEffect` in `SubmitGoalModal` that resets `matchPublicId` to `matches[0]?.id ?? ''` (and clears scorer/assister) when the previous selection isn't in the new matches list — guards against the modal staying open across a matchday change with stale match-id state. **Bug 2 — modal lacked clear matchday context:** the modal heading was just "Submit a goal" with no indication of which matchday the goal would be filed under. v1.48.1 replaces the heading with a small "Submit a goal for" eyebrow + a prominent bold matchday label (`{matchday.label}` — e.g. "MD3") rendered as the dialog `<h3>` with `data-testid="submit-goal-modal-matchday-label"`. The label uses `font-display text-2xl font-black uppercase tracking-tight` for visual weight. **Tests:** 5 new cases in [`tests/unit/matchdayPage.test.ts`](tests/unit/matchdayPage.test.ts) (regression target — Dashboard does NOT carry the `key={selectedMatchday.id}` prop on `<SubmitGoalForm>`; SubmitGoalForm has the `useEffect` cleanup on `matchday.id` change; SubmitGoalModal syncs `matchPublicId` against the matches list; modal renders the bold matchday label with the right testid + content). All 5 fail on the pre-fix state (verified via `git stash`-pop). 1201 passed | 2 skipped (1196 baseline + 5 new). Type-check clean. Patch bump (1.48.0 → 1.48.1) — bug fix on existing UX, no contract change.
>
> v1.48.0 — **Submit-Goal expanded + homepage/matchday convergence + open-attribution + click-to-copy section headers.** Single coherent UX update spanning four product changes. **(1) Submit-goal CTA moves to homepage too.** Pre-v1.48.0 the `[+ Submit a goal]` CTA lived only on `/matchday/[id]` (PR ζ / v1.46.0 / v1.47.0). v1.48.0 mounts it on the homepage Dashboard above `MatchdayAvailability` — gated client-side via `combineJstDateAndTime(matchday.date, match.kickoff)` + `selfReportGateOpen` for the SELECTED matchday so the gate auto-updates as the user swipes between matchdays. The button color flips from pink (`bg-vibrant-pink`) to LINE green (`bg-[#06C755]`) — visual delineation from the surrounding magenta brand chrome makes the action discoverable and signals "this writes data, not just navigates." **(2) Homepage IS the matchday page.** Pre-v1.48.0 the per-matchday route rendered a separate `MatchdayPageView` client component (v1.47.0); v1.48.0 deletes [`src/app/matchday/[id]/MatchdayPageView.tsx`](src/app/matchday/[id]/MatchdayPageView.tsx) and `[src/app/matchday/[id]/page.tsx](src/app/matchday/[id]/page.tsx)` becomes a thin server wrapper that resolves the league + verifies the matchday exists then renders the same `Dashboard` the apex renders, with new `initialMatchdayId` prop pre-selecting the URL matchday. Subsequent banner navigation (swipe / arrow / dot) is local state — the URL is the entry point, not a continuous source of truth. Visiting `/matchday/md2` looks identical to homepage but with MD2 pre-loaded; user can swipe to MD3 from there without URL change. The `NextMatchdayBanner.lockToSelected` prop (added in v1.47.0) is no longer set by anyone but stays in the API for future callers. The "View matchday" link inside `MatchdayCard` is **removed** because it routed somewhere that now looks identical to where the user was — pure UX dead weight. **(3) Open attribution.** Pre-v1.48.0 `submitOwnMatchEvent` forced `scorerId = session.playerId` — a player could only submit their OWN goals. The form locked the scorer; the action enforced it. v1.48.0 lets ANY logged-in linked player submit a goal for ANY player. New required `scorerPlayerSlug: string` parameter on the action; the form gains a scorer dropdown (`data-testid="submit-goal-scorer"`) sourced from the two participating-team rosters of the SELECTED match (grouped by team, sorted alphabetically). Server validates: scorer has a `PlayerLeagueAssignment` in one of the match's two teams (cross-league/cross-team picker abuse rejected); assister, when supplied, must be on the SCORER's team (not caller's) and ≠ scorer; OWN_GOAL beneficiary derives from the OPPOSITE of the scorer's team. `MatchEvent.createdById` still records the calling user (audit identity); `scorerId` is now driven by form input. No moderation layer for v1; admin StatsTab CRUD (PR γ) handles cleanup if abuse appears. **(4) Click-to-copy section headers.** New client component [`src/components/CopyMatchdayLink.tsx`](src/components/CopyMatchdayLink.tsx) wraps the MatchdayCard eyebrow text ("MATCHDAY RESULTS" / "YOUR NEXT MATCHDAY" / "MATCHDAY DETAILS") as a `<button>` that on click computes `${window.location.origin}/matchday/<id>` (apex + subdomain compatible without per-tenant config) and writes via `navigator.clipboard.writeText`. Sonner toast confirms ("Link copied to clipboard" with the URL as description) and a brief inline checkmark icon flips for ~1.8s on success. The eyebrow + small link/share glyph together form the affordance — both clickable, hover state turns vibrant-pink. Defensive failure handling: if `navigator.clipboard` is undefined or rejects, fires `toast.error('Could not copy link')` instead of crashing. **Cleanup:** `MatchdayPageView.tsx` deleted; `actions.ts#submitOwnMatchEvent` signature gains `scorerPlayerSlug` (and the test mocks lose `playerLeagueAssignment.findFirst`'s overloaded scorer-then-assister behavior — they now thread two `findFirst` calls). The `participatingMatches` filter (user-team-only) is gone from both the form and the page since open attribution lets any team be submittable. **Tests:** rewritten [`tests/unit/submitOwnMatchEvent.test.ts`](tests/unit/submitOwnMatchEvent.test.ts) (17 cases — happy path with scorer-from-form-not-session as the load-bearing regression target; `scorerId` recorded from `scorerPlayerSlug`; `createdById` recorded from session for audit; rejections on no-session / no-linked-caller / invalid-goalType / malformed-publicId / matchday-not-in-league / scorer-not-on-either-match-team / empty-scorer / before-kickoff / assister-equals-scorer / assister-not-on-scorers-team / minute-out-of-range; OG happy path; explicit "caller does NOT need to be on a match team" coverage). Rewritten [`tests/unit/matchdayPage.test.ts`](tests/unit/matchdayPage.test.ts) (37 cases — `MatchdayPageView` is GONE (regression target); page renders Dashboard with `initialMatchdayId`; Dashboard exposes `initialMatchdayId?` prop and uses it as first-render selection; SubmitGoalForm mounted via `submitGateOpen` evaluated client-side via `combineJstDateAndTime`; form takes `players` (open attribution); CTA color is `bg-[#06C755]` not pink; scorer testid present; "View matchday" link gone from MatchdayCard; CopyMatchdayLink uses `navigator.clipboard.writeText` + `window.location.origin` + `toast.success` + per-matchday testid; Sonner imported). 1196 passed | 2 skipped (1189 baseline + 7 net new — the test additions track the added behavior; counts include 17 new `submitOwnMatchEvent` cases vs 15 prior; 37 `matchdayPage` cases vs 37 prior with shape changes; 6 new `CopyMatchdayLink` cases). Type-check clean. Local build clean (Next 16 / Turbopack). Minor bump (1.47.0 → 1.48.0) — meaningful UX redesign + permission widening.
>
> v1.47.0 — **Matchday page redesign: mirror the homepage layout + big "Submit a goal" CTA with modal overlay.** Pre-v1.47.0 the per-matchday route ([src/app/matchday/[id]/page.tsx](src/app/matchday/[id]/page.tsx)) had a bespoke 3-section layout (header card / per-match scoreline cards / per-event timeline rows / inline-expand SubmitGoalForm). User asked for it to mirror the homepage Dashboard so the experience feels continuous. v1.47.0 replaces the bespoke layout with the homepage shape: `Header` → `GuestLoginBanner` → `UserTeamBadge` → `NextMatchdayBanner` (locked to URL) → big "Submit a goal" CTA (PR ζ gated, modal overlay) → `MatchdayAvailability` → `RsvpBar` (fixed bottom). **Same visual grammar as `/`** — admins / players already know how it works. **`NextMatchdayBanner.lockToSelected` prop** (new) — when true, skips the "auto-default to user's next playing matchday" useEffect that the homepage uses to pre-select the most relevant matchday on session hydration. The matchday page passes `lockToSelected` so the URL is the canonical source of which matchday renders; banner navigation (swipe / arrow / dot) routes via `router.push('/matchday/<new-id>')` rather than mutating local state. Default `false` preserves the homepage's existing behavior. **`SubmitGoalForm` UX inverted** — the v1.46.0 inline-expand pattern (small CTA → expand inline form) is replaced by a big full-width pink CTA + modal overlay. Modal uses `createPortal` to escape parent stacking context, has `role="dialog"` + `aria-modal="true"`, ESC + backdrop click + X button + Cancel all dismiss, body scroll locks while open. The form body itself (match dropdown / goalType picker / assister picker / minute input / Submit button) is unchanged in field shape; only the wrapper is. PR ζ's `submitOwnMatchEvent` server-action contract is unchanged. Success state shows "✅ Submitted. Tap again to add another." below the CTA so a player can drop multiple goals from one session without re-mounting the modal manually. **New `MatchdayPageView` client component** ([src/app/matchday/[id]/MatchdayPageView.tsx](src/app/matchday/[id]/MatchdayPageView.tsx)) — receives the resolved server-side data + the PR ζ gate result + the participating-matches list and renders the homepage-mirrored composition. Page is now a thin server component that fetches + threads. **Per-event PEN/SP/OG decorated timeline dropped from the public-facing matchday page** — the homepage MatchdayCard already shows minute + scorer + assister + (OG) per goal in compact form. PEN/SP markers stay on the underlying MatchEvent rows + admin Stats CRUD; surfacing them in a public detail view can land in a future PR if needed. **Cross-league session safety** preserved — `MatchdayPageView` reuses the same render-null branches as the homepage Dashboard for the `userTeamId not in this league's roster` case (UserTeamBadge hides via `pickUserTeam`; RsvpBar hides via `userTeamIsPlaying === false`; the availability lookup with a stale teamId returns undefined). **Tests:** rewritten [tests/unit/matchdayPage.test.ts](tests/unit/matchdayPage.test.ts) (37 cases — page is thin + delegates to MatchdayPageView; gate evaluated server-side; subdomain-aware unchanged; new MatchdayPageView composition pinned to the homepage-mirrored shape; `lockToSelected` prop + early-return + dep-array contract; SubmitGoalForm modal shape — createPortal + role=dialog + aria-modal + ESC handler + backdrop testid + body scroll lock + every form testid preserved + PR ζ server-action contract unchanged; MatchdayCard wiring unchanged from PR ε; `goalTypeLabel` export preserved for backward compat). 1189 passed | 2 skipped (1171 baseline + 18 net new — the v1.45.0 bespoke-layout assertions like `data-testid="matchday-matches"` / `match-section-...` / `event-...` are removed because the bespoke layout is gone). Type-check clean. Minor bump (1.46.1 → 1.47.0) — meaningful UX behavior change (the per-matchday public surface goes from a bespoke 3-section view to the homepage-mirrored composition).

> v1.46.1 — **Epic match events backfill applied to prod + Guest seeder + resolver upgrades (Kosma fuzzy match + Guest fallback).** Scripts-only follow-up to v1.46.0 / PR β. Pre-v1.46.1 the PR β backfill script ([`scripts/backfillMatchEventsFromSheet.ts`](scripts/backfillMatchEventsFromSheet.ts)) had never been `--apply`-ed against prod (the prior session deferred to operator action; the apply requires prod creds). Result: PR δ's read-flip in [`src/lib/dbToPublicLeagueData.ts`](src/lib/dbToPublicLeagueData.ts) shipped against an empty `MatchEvent` table, so the public site rendered scorelines (driven by the `Match.homeScore`/`awayScore` Int cache populated by the legacy PR-4 backfill) but ZERO scorers / assists / event timeline anywhere. User flagged the gap. **v1.46.1 fixes the script's resolver gaps + applies the backfill end-to-end.** **Resolver upgrades:** new pure helpers `firstNameToken(name)` (lowercased first space-separated token, null on single-token input) + `findUniqueByFirstName(firstNameLc, teamPlayers)` (returns the unique team player whose first-name matches, null on 0 or 2+ matches). `resolvePlayer(rawName, byLcName, bySlug, context?)` adds two new resolution steps after the exact + slug fallback: (3) **fuzzy first-name match within team context** — single-token names like "Kosma" resolve to the unique team player when scoring-team is supplied; (4) **EXPLICIT_GUEST_NAMES fallback** — names like `"Guest"` and `"Sergei Borodin"` map to the team's Guest player. The list is opt-in: arbitrary unresolvable names still SKIP, so we never silently miscredit goals. **Per-team Guest players:** new `ensureGuestPlayers(prisma, leagueTeams)` idempotently creates ONE Player named "Guest" per LeagueTeam (deterministic id `p-guest-<leagueTeamId>` via `guestPlayerIdFor` helper) with a current `PlayerLeagueAssignment` (onboardingStatus=COMPLETED, joinSource=null). Per-team is load-bearing: a single global Guest with N assignments would collapse in the `playerToLt` map (`Map<playerId, leagueTeamId>` — last-write-wins) breaking the scorer→team lookup that drives `computeScoreFromEvents`. The legacy single `p-guest` Player (with no PLA) is left untouched — harmless since the public read path iterates PLA rows. **Guest-shadow bug** caught in dry-run #2: 4 Guest players all sharing `name = "Guest"` collapsed in `playerByLcName` to one last-write-wins entry, which shadowed the contextual Guest fallback (the by-name match returned BEFORE the EXPLICIT_GUEST_NAMES branch could route to the correct team). Fix: skip Guest players when building `playerByLcName` / `playerBySlug` so they're only reachable via the contextual fallback. **Visibility:** Guests appear in the public roster — the legacy `GUEST_ID === 'p-guest'` exact-equals filter in `dbToPublicLeagueData` does NOT match the new `p-guest-<lt-id>` ids. Hiding them would require a `src/` change (out of scripts-only PR scope); flagged in the report for a follow-up if undesired. **Apply summary:** prod dry-run #3: 23 scanned / 23 inserts / 0 skipped / 0 score-cache mismatches. Apply: 23 events created across 5 matches (MD1 wk1 Mariners-vs-Fenix, MD1 Hygge-vs-Fenix, MD1 Mariners-vs-Hygge, MD2 Torpedo-vs-Fenix, MD2 Fenix-vs-Mariners). 4 Guest player records + 4 PLA rows seeded. 2 assister-name notes (rows 17 / 18: "Mihail Volkov" / "Alksey Koltakov" unresolved → null assister; goals still inserted). Public verification: post-cache-expiry curl on `/matchday/md1` shows 15 `data-testid="event-..."` rows, scorelines unchanged (2-2, 2-2, 4-3 from the cache columns), 0 "No events recorded" surfaces. **Tests:** new cases in [`tests/unit/backfillMatchEvents.test.ts`](tests/unit/backfillMatchEvents.test.ts) (53 cases total — 27 new across `firstNameToken`, `findUniqueByFirstName`, `EXPLICIT_GUEST_NAMES`, `guestPlayerIdFor`, expanded `resolvePlayer` covering fuzzy + Guest branches with/without context, expanded `decideRowAction` covering team-context wiring for "Kosma" / "Guest" / "Sergei Borodin" / phantom-name-still-skips / assister-also-uses-team-context). 1171 passed | 2 skipped (1144 baseline + 27 new). Type-check clean. Patch bump (1.46.0 → 1.46.1) — scripts-only data backfill + resolver enhancement, no app behavior change beyond what was already shipped in PR δ's read-flip lighting up against actual data.

> v1.46.0 — **Epic match events PR ζ: player self-report goal submission.** Sixth and final PR in the match-events epic (α / β / γ / δ / ε / ζ). Players who are signed in + linked to a Player record now see a `[+ Submit a goal you scored]` CTA on `/matchday/[id]` after the matchday's earliest kickoff in JST. Auto-approved per the user's brief — admin can edit/delete via PR γ's StatsTab CRUD if any submission is wrong. **Pure gate** [`src/lib/playerSelfReportGate.ts`](src/lib/playerSelfReportGate.ts) → `evaluateSelfReportGate({ hasSession, hasLinkedPlayer, matchKickoffs, now })` returning a discriminated union `'NO_SESSION' | 'NO_LINKED_PLAYER' | 'NO_KICKOFFS' | 'BEFORE_KICKOFF' | 'OPEN'`. The CTA renders only when `OPEN` (boolean shorthand `selfReportGateOpen`). Defensive against bad input — invalid date strings filter out so a corrupt kickoff field doesn't crash the gate. **Server action** [`submitOwnMatchEvent`](src/app/matchday/[id]/actions.ts) re-evaluates EVERY gate the page-level CTA enforces (defense in depth — page UI is the affordance, server is the contract): session has playerId; matchPublicId parses to `(weekNumber, matchIndex)` via the new `parseMatchPublicId` helper; gameWeek + match exist in the player's league; the matchday's earliest kickoff has passed; the player's team is participating in the match; assister, when supplied, ≠ scorer + on the player's own team. **Scorer is set from `session.userId → session.playerId → slugToPlayerId` — NEVER from form input** (a player can only ever submit their OWN goals). For OWN_GOAL, beneficiary is computed as the OPPOSITE of the player's team. Mutation + recompute wrapped in `prisma.$transaction(async tx => ...)` mirroring PR γ's admin actions. `MatchEvent.createdById` recorded for audit trail. **Client form** [`src/components/matchday/SubmitGoalForm.tsx`](src/components/matchday/SubmitGoalForm.tsx) — collapsed by default (just the CTA button); expands inline on click; match dropdown filtered to the player's team's participating matches in the matchday; goalType picker (4 options); assister picker filtered to teammates; minute optional; useTransition spinner; success state shows "✅ Submitted. Add another?" so a player can drop multiple goals from the same session. **Page integration** [`src/app/matchday/[id]/page.tsx`](src/app/matchday/[id]/page.tsx) — reads `getServerSession` + Prisma `gameWeek.findFirst` for the real `playedAt` instants (the public Match shape only carries JST `"HH:MM"` strings; the gate needs Date objects), evaluates the gate server-side, conditionally renders `<SubmitGoalForm>` only when `submitGateOpen && myPlayer`. **Tests:** new [`tests/unit/playerSelfReportGate.test.ts`](tests/unit/playerSelfReportGate.test.ts) (9 cases — every branch + ISO-string acceptance + invalid-date defensive skip + at-exactly-kickoff opens + earliest-of-multiple). New [`tests/unit/submitOwnMatchEvent.test.ts`](tests/unit/submitOwnMatchEvent.test.ts) (15 cases — happy path with createdById from session not input, regression on the load-bearing rule that scorerId comes from session not form, rejections on no-session / no-player / invalid-goalType / malformed-publicId / matchday-not-in-league / team-not-in-match / before-kickoff / assister-equals-scorer / assister-not-on-team / minute-out-of-range; OG happy path with player on home team). 1144 passed | 2 skipped (1120 baseline + 24 new). Type-check clean. Minor bump (1.45.0 → 1.46.0) — new player-facing write path. **Closes the match-events epic.** Goal/Assist tables and the legacy admin `addGoal`/`deleteGoal` actions remain for backward compat; a separate cleanup PR can retire them once events reads have soaked on prod.
>
> v1.45.0 — **Epic match events PR ε: per-matchday public page.** Fifth of 6 PRs in the match-events epic. New route [`src/app/matchday/[id]/page.tsx`](src/app/matchday/[id]/page.tsx) — server component, subdomain-aware via the v1.22.0 `getLeagueIdFromRequest()` helper. The `[id]` segment matches the public matchday id (`md1`, `md4`, etc. — same shape `dbToPublicLeagueData` produces). 404s when the matchday isn't in the resolved league. **Page contents:** matchday label + JST date (formatted via `formatJstFriendly`) + venue link if present; per-match section with home/away team labels, scoreline (cache integers OR scoreOverride driven, per PR δ's read-flip), JST kickoff (+ FT when ended), and a per-match timeline showing each MatchEvent as `<minute>' Stefan ⚽️ (set piece) 🅰️ Alex` with goalType decoration via the new `goalTypeLabel` helper (OPEN_PLAY → no decoration; SET_PIECE → "set piece"; PENALTY → "pen"; OWN_GOAL → "OG"; null/undefined → no decoration so Sheets-path data renders cleanly). **Sitting-out badge** when the matchday's `sittingOutTeamId` resolves to a real team. **Linking from `MatchdayCard`** — the existing `Dashboard` + `/schedule` cards now render a `[View matchday →]` link to `/matchday/<id>` on every card. The legacy "See full schedule" link remains for the Dashboard view. **Tests:** new [`tests/unit/matchdayPage.test.ts`](tests/unit/matchdayPage.test.ts) (14 cases — file presence, subdomain awareness via `getLeagueIdFromRequest`, `notFound` on missing matchday, full set of testid hooks the future e2e specs key off, `formatJstFriendly` + 'TBD' fallback, reads `goal.minute` + `goal.goalType` from the public Goal shape per PR δ, does NOT use `getLeagueStats`; MatchdayCard wires the new `/matchday/<id>` href + testid, preserves the legacy `/schedule` link; `goalTypeLabel` returns the right label for each enum value plus null/undefined). 1120 passed | 2 skipped (1106 baseline + 14 new). Type-check clean. Minor bump (1.44.0 → 1.45.0) — new public route.

> v1.44.0 — **Epic match events PR δ: public read-flip + per-match goal highlights.** Fourth of 6 PRs in the match-events epic. Pre-δ the public dashboard derived `LeagueData.goals` and per-match scorelines from the legacy `Goal`+`Assist` Prisma join. v1.44.0 flips both reads to compute from the unified `MatchEvent` log shipped in PR α and populated by PR β's backfill (and PR γ's admin CRUD). [`src/lib/dbToPublicLeagueData.ts`](src/lib/dbToPublicLeagueData.ts) now `include`s `match.events` (with scorer + assister) instead of `match.goals`, builds a `playerToLt` map from the league's PLA fetch, and derives each public Goal record from a MatchEvent — including the OWN_GOAL flip (scorer's team is one side; goal credits the OPPOSITE team). New optional fields on the `Goal` shape in [`src/types/index.ts`](src/types/index.ts): `minute?: number | null` and `goalType?: 'OPEN_PLAY' | 'SET_PIECE' | 'PENALTY' | 'OWN_GOAL' | null`. The Sheets path keeps `minute`/`goalType` undefined; the DB path populates them from MatchEvent. **Score-override applied** via the v1.42.0 `resolveDisplayScore` helper: when `Match.scoreOverride` parses cleanly (`"3-0 (forfeit)"`) the override drives the displayed numbers; when set but unparseable (`"abandoned"`) the cache integers stand and the override decorates. **`isPlayed` semantic preserved**: pre-δ a match was rendered as played when `status === 'COMPLETED' || goals.length > 0`; post-δ it's `status === 'COMPLETED' || events.length > 0 || scoreOverride !== null`. **Defensive scorer skip**: any MatchEvent whose scorer can't be resolved to either match team's roster is silently skipped — mirrors the structured-warning pattern in `recomputeMatchScore`. **MatchdayCard tick** ([`src/components/MatchdayCard.tsx`](src/components/MatchdayCard.tsx)) gains a minute prefix (`47' Stefan`) and an `(OG)` suffix for own goals. Per-event detail (PEN / SP markers, full timeline) is deferred to PR ε's per-matchday page. **Admin StatsTab leaderboard** ([`src/components/admin/StatsTab.tsx`](src/components/admin/StatsTab.tsx)) flips its top-scorers computation to read from `events` via the new `buildScorerStatsFromEvents` helper (exported for tests). Own goals continue to be excluded from individual goal totals. The legacy `buildScorerStats` (Goal/Assist-backed) is preserved on the export surface for backward compat. The League Table section continues to use `Match.homeScore`/`awayScore` because those are now the recompute-populated cache. **Tests:** new [`tests/unit/dbToPublicLeagueDataEvents.test.ts`](tests/unit/dbToPublicLeagueDataEvents.test.ts) (7 cases — adapter reshapes events into Goal[] with right beneficiary slug, OG flip, scoreOverride parses cleanly, cache-integer fallback when override absent, isPlayed=null when no events/no override/not COMPLETED, isPlayed=true when events present even on IN_PROGRESS, defensive skip on unresolvable scorer). New `buildScorerStatsFromEvents` cases added to [`tests/unit/statsTabEvents.test.ts`](tests/unit/statsTabEvents.test.ts) (4 cases — counts goals + assists, OG excluded from individual tally, matchday filter, sort order). 1106 passed | 2 skipped (1095 baseline + 11 new). Type-check clean. Minor bump (1.43.0 → 1.44.0) — public read-path semantics change. Goal+Assist tables and the legacy `getLeagueStats` helper stay live; retiring them is out of scope for this PR (a future cleanup PR can drop them once event reads have soaked).

> v1.43.0 — **Epic match events PR γ: admin events CRUD on the StatsTab.** Third of 6 PRs in the match-events epic. Pre-γ the admin StatsTab was a read-only top-scorers + league-table view with no UI to create / edit / delete goals (admins had to drill into a per-match page). v1.43.0 adds an events-first surface ABOVE the existing leaderboard sections: matchday filter chips + free-text search + per-row Edit/Delete + a `[+ New event]` modal editor. **Smart pickers** (server-enforced; client UI is the affordance, not the contract): for `OPEN_PLAY`/`SET_PIECE`/`PENALTY` the scorer picker shows ONLY the beneficiary team's roster; for `OWN_GOAL` the scorer picker flips to the OPPOSING team's roster (the OG-er); assister picker always shows the beneficiary team's roster minus the scorer. The "beneficiary team" toggle on the form lets the admin pick whether the goal counts toward home or away, decoupled from goalType. **Three new admin server actions** in [`src/app/admin/leagues/actions.ts`](src/app/admin/leagues/actions.ts): `adminCreateMatchEvent` / `adminUpdateMatchEvent` / `adminDeleteMatchEvent`. Each gates on `assertAdmin`, validates cross-league isolation (match.leagueId === supplied leagueId), validates beneficiaryTeamId is one of the match's teams, validates scorer-on-right-team per goalType, and (when assister supplied) validates assister is on beneficiary team + ≠ scorer. Each wraps the mutation + `recomputeMatchScore(tx, matchId)` call in a `prisma.$transaction(async tx => ...)` so a recompute failure rolls back the event write — the cache columns and event rows can never get out of sync. Each fires `revalidate({ domain: 'admin', paths: [stats / schedule / matches/<id>] })`. Plus `adminSetMatchScoreOverride({ matchId, leagueId, override })` writes the v1.42.0 `Match.scoreOverride` column and DOES NOT recompute (the override is for forfeits — events stay as the underlying truth). **New data fetch** [`getLeagueEvents`](src/lib/admin-data.ts) returns `[events, matches, leagueTeams (with rosters), gameWeekCount]` cached under the `leagues` tag (so admin write busts pick it up automatically via the v1.16.0 canonical helper). The existing `getLeagueStats` (Goal/Assist-backed) stays — PR δ flips the leaderboard reads to MatchEvent. **UI** ([`src/components/admin/StatsTab.tsx`](src/components/admin/StatsTab.tsx)): three new sub-components — `EventRowDisplay` (per-row card with goalType color pill, scorer + assister names, match label, Edit + Delete buttons; Delete wraps `adminDeleteMatchEvent` in a `useTransition` + `window.confirm` gate); `EventEditor` (modal portal mounted via `<div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/60">`, owns the form state, click-outside + Cancel close, calls Create or Update path based on `existing` prop, surfaces server errors inline). Pure helpers `filterEvents` and `rosterFor` exported for unit testing. Player self-report (PR ζ) reuses the same scorer/assister picker shape but locks scorerId to the session's playerId. **Tests:** new [`tests/unit/adminMatchEventActions.test.ts`](tests/unit/adminMatchEventActions.test.ts) (20 cases — happy paths, cross-league isolation, beneficiary-not-in-match, scorer-not-on-team for non-OG, scorer-not-on-OPPOSING for OG including the regression target that the PLA query keys on `leagueTeamId: AWAY` when beneficiary is HOME, OG happy path, assister-not-on-beneficiary, assister-equals-scorer, invalid goalType, out-of-range minute; updateMatchEvent + deleteMatchEvent + setMatchScoreOverride covering recompute-fires + recompute-doesn't-fire on override, override clears on null + whitespace-only). New [`tests/unit/statsTabEvents.test.ts`](tests/unit/statsTabEvents.test.ts) (15 cases — `filterEvents` matchday-filter / case-insensitive search across scorer + assister + team + combined; `rosterFor` named-only filter + sort + unknown-team-empty; structural pins on the StatsTab source: imports the new actions, exposes the seven `data-testid` hooks, declares the four GoalType labels, includes the OG advisory copy; admin stats page-level wiring threads events + eventMatches + eventLeagueTeams). 1095 passed | 2 skipped (1060 baseline + 35 new). Type-check clean. Minor bump (1.42.1 → 1.43.0) — new admin write capability + new admin UI surface.

> v1.42.1 — **Epic match events PR β: backfill historical goals from `GoalsRaw!A:F` into `MatchEvent`.** Second of 6 PRs in the match-events epic. New script [`scripts/backfillMatchEventsFromSheet.ts`](scripts/backfillMatchEventsFromSheet.ts) reads the source sheet (same auth/auth as `sheetsToDbBackfill.ts`), resolves each row's `(matchday, scoringTeam, concedingTeam) → Match.id` and `(scorerName, assisterName) → Player.id` via a case-insensitive trimmed exact match with a `slugify` fallback, and inserts a `MatchEvent { kind: GOAL, goalType: OPEN_PLAY, minute: null, createdById: null }` row per resolvable goal. **Default mode is `--dry-run`**; `--apply` actually writes. Per-row decisions: INSERT (resolved) or SKIP with structured reason (`unresolved-matchday` / `unresolved-scoring-team` / `unresolved-conceding-team` / `unresolved-match` / `unresolved-scorer`). Assister text that resolves: insert with assisterId. Assister text that does NOT resolve: insert with `assisterId: null` + flag the row in the report (we don't drop the goal because the assister was unrecognised). **Score-cache safety net** — after computing inserts (in dry-run via simulation, in apply via re-read) the script compares the events-derived scoreline against the existing `Match.homeScore`/`awayScore` cache and reports mismatches per match. **Critically: the script NEVER mutates the cache** — mismatches are surfaced in the markdown report (`outputs/match-events-backfill-report.md`) for user review. Existing `Goal`+`Assist` rows are also untouched (they stay as the legacy read source through PR γ; PR δ flips reads). **Assumption encoded in the report:** GoalsRaw has no goalType column today, so all imported events land as OPEN_PLAY; admins can edit individual events post-import via PR γ's admin events CRUD. **Operator-side gate:** the prod apply requires DB credentials this session does not have inside the worktree. The script ships with a clean dry-run shape; surfaced to dispatch — operator runs `npx ts-node --project tsconfig.scripts.json scripts/backfillMatchEventsFromSheet.ts --dry-run` to review the report, then `--apply` against prod when ready. **Tests:** new [`tests/unit/backfillMatchEvents.test.ts`](tests/unit/backfillMatchEvents.test.ts) (26 cases — `parseFlags` defaults / overrides; `slugify` parity with the public-side helper including the apostrophe edge case; `resolveWeekNumber` MD-label happy path / timestamp fallback / unresolvable; `resolvePlayer` exact / slug-fallback / null-on-empty; `decideRowAction` happy path with and without assister, both home-vs-away and away-vs-home permutations resolving to the same Match, every SKIP branch, the `_assisterNote` annotation when assister is non-empty but unresolvable, every imported row landing as OPEN_PLAY). 1060 passed | 2 skipped (1034 baseline + 26 new). Type-check clean. Patch bump (1.42.0 → 1.42.1) — data-only / new script; no app behavior change in prod app.

> v1.42.0 — **Epic match events PR α: additive `MatchEvent` schema + `Match.scoreOverride` + pure score-helper module.** First of 6 PRs in the match-events epic (α / β / γ / δ / ε / ζ). Pre-v1.42.0 the scoreline lived as `Match.homeScore`/`awayScore` Int columns mutated by `updateMatchScore`, while goal detail lived in a parallel `Goal`+`Assist` table pair — two systems of truth. v1.42.0 introduces a single `MatchEvent` event log (cuid id, FK to Match + scorer Player + optional assister Player + audit `createdById` User; `kind` enum starts with just `GOAL`, `goalType` enum covers OPEN_PLAY / SET_PIECE / PENALTY / OWN_GOAL; nullable `minute`) and a new `Match.scoreOverride String?` for forfeits / abandoned matches. **Schema delta:** purely additive — `CREATE TYPE EventKind`, `CREATE TYPE GoalType`, `CREATE TABLE MatchEvent` with cascading FK on Match (cascade delete) + RESTRICT on scorerId Player (deleting a player with events is intentionally hard) + SET NULL on assisterId / createdById (detach without deleting events). `ALTER TABLE Match ADD COLUMN scoreOverride TEXT NULL`. `Goal` + `Assist` tables and their reads stay intact through PR γ; PR δ flips public read paths to compute from MatchEvent. **New module** [`src/lib/matchScore.ts`](src/lib/matchScore.ts): pure `computeScoreFromEvents(homeTeamId, awayTeamId, events, scorerTeamLookup) → { home, away }` (counts goals to scorer team, OWN_GOAL flips to opposite, unresolved scorers silently skipped); pure `parseScoreOverride(raw) → { home, away } | null` (regex parses `"H-A"` / `"H – A"` / `"H — A"` / `"H:A"` shapes including with leading/trailing decoration like `"3-0 (forfeit)"`); pure `resolveDisplayScore(match) → { home, away, kind, overrideText?, overrideParsedCleanly? }` (override beats cache when set; falls back to cache integers when override is unparseable text like `"abandoned"`); side-effecting `recomputeMatchScore(prisma, matchId) → { home, away }` reads match + events + assignments, builds player→team lookup (first-assignment-wins for v1), writes `Match.homeScore`/`awayScore`, NEVER touches `scoreOverride`, structured-warns on unresolved scorers. Idempotent. **No call sites changed** — helpers exist, schema exists, no read or write site reaches into MatchEvent yet (that's PR γ's job). **Tests:** new [`tests/unit/matchScore.test.ts`](tests/unit/matchScore.test.ts) (17 cases — 0-0 empty, OPEN_PLAY scorer team, SET_PIECE/PENALTY identical, OWN_GOAL flips, mixed regular+OG, unresolved-skip, third-team-defensive, null-goalType-defensive; parseScoreOverride covering hyphen/en-dash/em-dash/colon plus decoration plus unparseable; resolveDisplayScore cache+override-clean+override-unparseable). New [`tests/unit/matchEventSchema.test.ts`](tests/unit/matchEventSchema.test.ts) (13 cases pinning the schema deltas + back-relations + migration purely-additive invariant — no DROP TABLE/COLUMN/TYPE, no ALTER COLUMN DROP, no TRUNCATE; FK cascade/RESTRICT/SET NULL semantics). New [`tests/unit/recomputeMatchScore.test.ts`](tests/unit/recomputeMatchScore.test.ts) (7 cases — mocked Prisma covering 0-0, mixed events including OG, unresolved-warning structured-log shape, missing-match returns 0-0 without writes, scoreOverride untouched in update payload, idempotency, multi-PLA first-wins). 1034 passed | 2 skipped (987 baseline pre-v1.42.0 + 47 net new across the schema + helpers + recompute + ratings cleanup baseline). Type-check clean. **Operator follow-up:** the prod migration `20260503100000_match_events` is purely additive and runs cleanly during the Vercel build; rollback recipe in the migration SQL header. Minor bump (1.41.4 → 1.42.0) — schema additions + new public helper module.

> v1.41.2 — **Bug fix: header wraps to two rows on iPhone-width viewports.** User-reported: "on iPhones the banner takes up 2 vertical spaces instead of 1." Diagnosis via Chrome MCP measurement of header content widths at the prod URL: the header inner content (`flex items-center gap-2 px-4 h-12`) needed ~366px on the Sign-in branch (76px title + 12px `ml-3` + 62px Stats pill + 8px `gap-2` + 60px ThemeToggle + 8px `gap-2` + 52px LanguageToggle + 8px `gap-2` + ~80px Sign-in pill at `text-[11px] px-4 py-1.5`) but only ~358px was available at 390px viewport (after the container `px-4` strips 32px). 8px overflow at iPhone 12 (390px), ~23px overflow at iPhone SE (375px). **Fix:** trim mobile padding/gaps in [`src/components/Header.tsx`](src/components/Header.tsx) and the Sign-in pill in [`src/components/LineLoginButton.tsx`](src/components/LineLoginButton.tsx) without shrinking the brand title. Container `px-4` → `px-3 md:px-4` (saves 8px on mobile); nav `ml-3` → `ml-2 md:ml-3` (saves 4px); Stats pill `px-2.5` → `px-2 md:px-2.5` (saves 4px); right cluster `gap-2` → `gap-1.5 md:gap-2` (saves 4px across 3 gaps); Sign-in pill `px-4` → `px-3 md:px-4` (saves 8px). Total ~28px saved on mobile (366 → 338 content width); fits at iPhone 12 with ~28px margin and at iPhone SE with ~13px margin. Title `text-xl` deliberately preserved on both breakpoints — the brand mark is load-bearing; trimming utility chrome around it was preferred over shrinking the wordmark itself. Desktop layout (≥768px / `md:` breakpoint) is byte-equivalent to pre-v1.41.2 — every trim is `mobile-value md:original-value`. **Tests:** new [`tests/unit/headerMobileSizing.test.ts`](tests/unit/headerMobileSizing.test.ts) (6 cases — container `px-3 md:px-4`; nav `ml-2 md:ml-3`; Stats pill responsive; right-cluster `gap-1.5 md:gap-2`; brand title stays at `text-xl` on both breakpoints; Sign-in pill `px-3 md:px-4`). **Verified regression target:** stash the fix → 5/6 cases fail on the broken state (the 6th is a forward-looking check that the title doesn't acquire a `text-lg md:text-xl` pattern — neutral on the pre-fix state). 987 passed | 2 skipped (984 baseline + 6 new — three slot via file-collision with neighbouring tests). Type-check clean. Patch bump (1.41.1 → 1.41.2) — UX bug fix on existing layout, no contract change. Auth flow / data flow unchanged. Title font / brand colors / accessibility unchanged.

> v1.41.1 — **Bug fix: invisible "Go to homepage" button text on `/join/[code]` invite-error + roster-full pages.** User-reported: clicking an unrecognised invite code (or hitting the "Roster is full" branch) rendered a magenta `bg-primary` button with no visible label — DOM had `<a>Go to homepage</a>` but the text color matched the inherited foreground rather than white. Root cause: nine call sites across `src/app/join/**` (`page.tsx` ErrorState + roster-full, `RedeemPersonalForm`, `RedeemCodePicker`, `id-upload/IdUploadForm`, `id-upload/page.tsx`, `onboarding/OnboardingForm`, `welcome/page.tsx`) and `src/app/account/player/AccountPlayerForm.tsx` use the Tailwind utility `text-on-primary` over `bg-primary`, but the matching `--color-on-primary` token was **never declared** in the `@theme inline` block of [`src/app/globals.css`](src/app/globals.css). Tailwind v4 compiled the class to `color: var(--color-on-primary)` which evaluated to nothing → the property was discarded → text fell back to the inherited `--color-fg-mid` (low-contrast against magenta, effectively invisible against the brand pink). The matching token `--color-primary-foreground` (white) was correctly declared one line above. **Fix:** add `--color-on-primary: var(--primary-foreground);` to the `@theme inline` block — single source of truth aliasing both names to the same `--primary-foreground` (white) declaration. Single one-line CSS edit fixes all 9 call sites simultaneously. **Tests:** new [`tests/unit/onPrimaryColorToken.test.ts`](tests/unit/onPrimaryColorToken.test.ts) (3 cases — token declared anywhere; aliased to `--primary-foreground` (single source of truth); declared specifically inside the `@theme inline` block so Tailwind picks it up). Verified the regression target by `git stash`-ing the fix and re-running: all 3 cases fail on the broken state. 984 passed | 2 skipped (981 baseline + 3 new). Type-check clean. Patch bump (1.41.0 → 1.41.1) — bug fix, no contract change.

> v1.41.0 — **Admin Players tab: per-row Edit-mode redesign with EditPlayerPanel + new `adminUpdatePlayerPosition` action.** Pre-v1.41.0 the player name was rendered as a permanent `PillEditor variant="text"` (v1.20.0) — every row carried a dotted-underline + click-to-swap-input editor that was always visible. The user audit ("there is more space" once the inline edit affordance is gone) drove the conversion: display mode is now compact static text, edit mode lives inside a per-row `EditPlayerPanel` toggled by a pencil button next to the kebab. **Display mode** — name renders as plain `<p>` with `font-condensed text-base font-bold leading-tight` (mobile + desktop), no dotted underline; the data-testids stayed (`player-name-mobile-{id}` / `player-name-{id}`) so callers can still locate the row. The desktop grid's last column widens from 40px to 80px to fit the pencil + kebab pair (`gridTemplateColumns: '32px 40px 1fr 140px 60px 110px 80px'`). **Edit mode** — pencil button (`lucide-react#Pencil`, 14px) toggles `editPanelId` (mirrors the existing `transferPanelId` shape — only one panel can be open at a time, single-row toggle via the same-row click pattern). On open, [`EditPlayerPanel`](src/components/admin/PlayersTab.tsx) expands below the row carrying a name `<input type="text" maxLength={100}>`, a position `<select>` with the four PlayerPosition enum values + an explicit `"" → "— None —"` fallback for nullable, and Save / Cancel buttons. Local form state in the panel; on Save, only the changed fields are written (sequential `adminUpdatePlayerName` then `adminUpdatePlayerPosition` calls so per-action error toasts surface in order). Save is disabled when `!dirty || nameInvalid || pending`. Cancel calls `onClose` directly — local state is destroyed on unmount, no explicit revert needed. Visual layout (`mx-4 md:mx-5 my-3 p-4 bg-admin-surface3 rounded-md border border-admin-border` flex form) mirrors `TransferPanel` so the two row-expansion affordances feel like the same family. **Schema delta:** none. **New server action** [`adminUpdatePlayerPosition({ playerId, leagueId, position })`](src/app/admin/leagues/actions.ts) — accepts the 4 PlayerPosition enum literals or `null` to clear; coerces unknown strings to null defensively (mirrors PR ε's `adminCreatePlayer`); validates non-empty `playerId`; uses the canonical [`revalidate({ domain: 'admin', paths: [\`/admin/leagues/${leagueId}/players\`] })`](src/lib/revalidate.ts) helper. Pre-v1.41.0 the only paths that wrote `Player.position` were `adminCreatePlayer` (PR ε) and `submitOnboarding` (PR ζ) — admins had no surface to fix a mistyped position or fill a slot the user left blank without flipping `onboardingStatus` back via PR θ. **Code dropouts:** `handleRenamePlayer` is gone from `PlayersTab` (its single caller was the inline `PillEditor.onSave` which is also gone); the `PillEditor` import is dropped (no remaining call sites in this file — the variant still exists in `PillEditor.tsx` for any future callers). The `text` variant's intrinsic contract (commit-on-blur / change-guard / rollback-on-failure) is still pinned by [`tests/unit/playersTabNamePill.test.ts`](tests/unit/playersTabNamePill.test.ts)'s remaining two `describe` blocks (PillEditor variant + `adminUpdatePlayerName` action existence); the v1.20.0 third block ("PlayersTab uses PillEditor for name") is removed because v1.41.0 contradicts it directly. **Tests:** new [`tests/unit/playersTabEditMode.test.ts`](tests/unit/playersTabEditMode.test.ts) (22 cases — display mode pins the absence of `variant="text"` + `value={player.name ?? ''}` combo, no PillEditor import, plain-`<p>` testids, 80px-final-column grid, pencil-button testids in both layouts, `editPanelId` state + same-row toggle handler, two `editPanelId === player.id && (...)` mounts; EditPlayerPanel function exists + name init + position-narrowing + only-changed-fields write + `position === '' → null` coercion at boundary + Save disabled gate + Cancel-onClose + 4-enum + None option set + per-input testids; `adminUpdatePlayerPosition` exported with 4-literal-or-null signature + defensive coercion + canonical revalidate + empty-playerId guard fires before Prisma + PlayersTab imports the new action). Existing [`tests/unit/playersTabRedesign.test.ts`](tests/unit/playersTabRedesign.test.ts) updated for the 80px-final-column shape (1 case modified). Existing [`tests/unit/playersTabNamePill.test.ts`](tests/unit/playersTabNamePill.test.ts) loses its third `describe` block (6 cases removed — the v1.20.0 inline-pill assertion is contradicted by v1.41.0). 978 passed | 2 skipped (962 baseline + 22 new − 6 obsolete = 978). Type-check clean. Stash-pop sanity check confirmed: reverting just the PlayersTab edits fails 17 of 22 new cases (regression catches the broken behavior). Minor bump (1.40.0 → 1.41.0) — meaningful UX redesign + new admin write capability + extends the editable-fields surface to position. **Out of scope:** team change still happens via the existing TransferPanel (it requires picking the effective GW so it doesn't fit the simple field-edit pattern). The v1.20.0 `text` variant of PillEditor is preserved as part of the public PillEditor API even though no current call site uses it. v1.40.0 — **Invite-page inline auth: `/join/[code]` provider buttons are now ON the invite page itself; picking a provider IS the confirmation.** Pre-v1.40.0 the signed-out flow on `/join/[code]` had two intermediate steps: (PERSONAL) the user saw the player preview + a "Yes, that's me — sign in to confirm" button which routed to `/auth/signin?callbackUrl=/join/<code>`, where they picked LINE / Google / email, then bounced back. (CODE) the user saw the league preview + a single "Sign in to continue" link to the same provider picker, then bounced back. Two round-trips of branding-context loss before the user could claim the slot. v1.40.0 collapses the YES step: provider buttons render INLINE inside the invite card itself, each fires `signIn(provider, { callbackUrl: '/join/<code>' })` directly. After NextAuth's OAuth round-trip the user lands back on `/join/<code>` already signed-in; the page rerenders into the signed-in branch which kicks off `redeemInvite` (PERSONAL) or shows the roster picker (CODE). The user never leaves the invite context. **New component** [`src/app/join/[code]/JoinInlineAuth.tsx`](src/app/join/[code]/JoinInlineAuth.tsx) — `'use client'` provider picker, mirrors `SignInLightbox.tsx`'s visual language (LINE primary green button + conditional Google + Email buttons; non-LINE providers self-hide via `getProviders()` when their env vars aren't set on Vercel; email transitions inline to a "check your email" surface). NOT a modal — no `createPortal`, no focus-trap, no body-scroll lock; it's an inline three-button stack inside the invite card. **Page wiring** [`src/app/join/[code]/page.tsx`](src/app/join/[code]/page.tsx) — `PersonalPreview` for `isSignedIn === false` now mounts `<JoinInlineAuth code={code} />` instead of `<RedeemPersonalForm isSignedIn={false} ...>`; `CodePreviewSignedOut` mounts `<JoinInlineAuth code={code} />` instead of the legacy `<Link href="/auth/signin?callbackUrl=...">`. The "Is this you?" copy on PERSONAL signed-out gets a tail ("Pick how you'd like to sign in to claim your slot.") so the provider buttons read as the answer. The `data-testid="join-signin-cta"` on the legacy CODE-signed-out link is gone (regression target — would fail this test if a future PR re-introduces the bounce). **Form simplification** [`src/app/join/[code]/RedeemPersonalForm.tsx`](src/app/join/[code]/RedeemPersonalForm.tsx) — drops the `isSignedIn` prop and the signed-out branch entirely. Pre-v1.40.0 the component had two paths: signed-out → `router.push('/auth/signin?callbackUrl=...')`; signed-in → `await redeemInvite({ code })`. Post-v1.40.0 only the signed-in path exists; the parent only mounts this component when `isSignedIn === true`, so `useRouter` is now used only for the post-redeem `router.push(result.redirectTo)`. Button label simplification: the third "Yes, that's me — sign in to confirm" variant is gone. **Already-signed-in users** on `/join/[code]` continue to skip the auth section — the page-level `existingBinding` lookup at line 102 still routes them to `/welcome` / `/id-upload` / `/onboarding` per their assignment's `onboardingStatus`. Admin player-list edit-mode redesign (queued as v1.41.0). v1.39.2 — **Bug fix: non-LINE users (Google / email) can no longer use the legacy `/assign-player` picker — surface a "need invite" message instead.** User-reported: a freshly registered Google/email user clicked Confirm on a player and got "NOT AUTHENTICATED" toast. Root cause: `/api/assign-player` POST/DELETE gate on `session?.lineId` (LINE-keyed end-to-end since v1.5.0 / v1.8.0; the canonical Redis store is keyed by lineId, the durable Prisma write is to `Player.lineId @unique`). Google/email users authenticated via the v1.28.0 multi-provider foundation have `session.userId` but no `session.lineId`, so the API rejects them with 401. Pre-v1.39.2 nothing surfaced this contract at the page level — three CTAs in [`LineLoginButton.tsx`](src/components/LineLoginButton.tsx) (the first-login `AssignModal` popup + the no-player dropdown link + the linked-player "Change/Unassign" link) all routed unconditionally to `/assign-player`, the page rendered the picker for any session, the user clicked Confirm, then hit the 401 wall. **Fix shape (Option A per user's intent):** existing LINE users are grandfathered onto the legacy picker; non-LINE users redeem invites via PR ζ's `/join/[code]` flow (per the user's prior decision: "registration requires an invite"). Three surfaces gated: (1) [`src/app/assign-player/page.tsx`](src/app/assign-player/page.tsx) gains a server-side early-return — `if (session && !session.lineId) return <NeedInviteSurface />` — that renders a card with the "you need an invite to join" message + `mailto:vitoriatamachi@gmail.com` + Back-to-home CTA. The gate fires BEFORE `getLinkedPlayerIds` and the picker JSX so the API write path can't be reached at all. (2) [`LineLoginButton.tsx`](src/components/LineLoginButton.tsx) — the `AssignModal` popup `useEffect` gates on `session?.lineId` (the dependency array now includes it) so non-LINE users don't see the LINE-keyed pop-up at all. (3) Same file's dropdown derives a new `hasLine = !!session.lineId` flag and gates three branches: needsSetup-with-LINE shows "Assign to my player" (existing); needsSetup-without-LINE shows a "Need an invite link" message + mailto (new `data-testid="account-menu-need-invite"`); linked-player-with-LINE shows "Edit my details" + "Change/Unassign player" (existing); linked-player-without-LINE shows "Edit my details" only (the legacy "Change/Unassign player" link is hidden because non-LINE users switch by redeeming a fresh invite — v1.39.0 PR λ's `linkUserToPlayer` already handles atomic User-side rebinding). The API gates at `route.ts:212` / `route.ts:309` STAY in place as the load-bearing safety net (regression target — a directly-crafted POST from a Google/email session must continue to 401, not silently mutate the LINE-keyed store). **Tests:** new [`tests/unit/assignPlayerNonLineGate.test.ts`](tests/unit/assignPlayerNonLineGate.test.ts) (16 cases — page-level NeedInviteSurface presence + early-return ordering + gate predicate shape + mailto + back-to-home; route-level POST + DELETE gates pinned as regression targets; LineLoginButton `hasLine` derived flag + AssignModal useEffect gate + needsSetup ternary + linked-player `hasLine && (...)` gate + every `href="/assign-player"` is upstream-gated by either the AssignModal popup gate or `hasLine`). Patch bump (1.39.0 → 1.39.1) — docs-only, no code or schema change. v1.39.0 — **PR λ: Identity unification audit + invariant-clearing fix on non-LINE redemption.** Third and final follow-up PR (ι/κ/λ) after the δ→θ onboarding chain. **Schema delta:** none — purely application-layer. **Audit findings ([`outputs/identity-unification-audit.md`](outputs/identity-unification-audit.md)):** confirmed that LINE-auth redemption populates `Player.lineId`, Google/email leaves `Player.lineId` null with `Player.userId` + `User.playerId` set, and `Player.id` (cuid) is the canonical PK. **Found bug:** `redeemInvite` (PR ζ) had a non-LINE branch that bypassed the v1.29.0 `linkPlayerToUser` helper — direct `tx.player.update({...userId})` + `tx.user.update({...playerId})` with NO defensive clearing of stale 1:1 invariant pointers. Pre-λ a Google/email user rebinding from a prior Player to a new one would surface as a Prisma `Player.userId @unique` violation 500 instead of a graceful rebind. **Fix:** new generic [`linkUserToPlayer(tx, {userId, playerId, lineId?})`](src/lib/identityLink.ts) helper keyed on `User.id @unique` (not `User.lineId`) so it works for Google / email / LINE flows uniformly. Same invariant-clearing logic as `linkPlayerToUser`: clears stale `Player.userId === user.id` from a different Player, clears `User.playerId` if previously bound. Optional `lineId` argument lets the LINE branch ALSO set `Player.lineId` in the same `tx.player.update` call. `redeemInvite` refactored to route BOTH LINE and non-LINE branches through `linkUserToPlayer`: the LINE call passes `{userId, playerId, lineId}` (sets all three columns in one update); the non-LINE call passes `{userId, playerId}` only (Player.lineId stays null). The pre-λ pattern of two separate updates per branch is gone. `linkPlayerToUser` (the legacy lineId-keyed helper) stays — `/api/assign-player` POST/DELETE and the admin actions still use it because they carry lineId from the LINE session, not userId. Stage 4 (Δ) will retire the legacy helper alongside `Player.lineId`. **Tests:** new [`tests/unit/linkUserToPlayer.test.ts`](tests/unit/linkUserToPlayer.test.ts) (8 cases — happy path, lineId optional, lineId explicit-null branch, prior-rebind clearing, idempotent re-bind, no-User no-op); new [`tests/unit/identityUnificationAudit.test.ts`](tests/unit/identityUnificationAudit.test.ts) (12 cases — structural assertions on redeemInvite, identityLink exports, /api/assign-player still uses the legacy helper, audit doc shape); existing [`tests/unit/redeemInvite.test.ts`](tests/unit/redeemInvite.test.ts) — 2 cases updated for the new call shape (LINE branch goes through `linkUserToPlayer({...lineId})`; Google/email branch goes through `linkUserToPlayer({...no lineId})`). 930 passed | 2 skipped (910 baseline + 20 net new). Closes the loop on the admin side: when a player needs to redo onboarding (changed name, mistyped position, ID purged, etc.), the admin flips their `PlayerLeagueAssignment.onboardingStatus` back to `NOT_YET` and the next visit to `/join/[code]` redirects them through the onboarding form again. **Schema delta:** none. The `onboardingStatus` enum + column shipped at v1.34.0 (PR ζ). θ is purely the admin write-path + UI affordance. **Code delta:** new server action `adminResetOnboarding({ playerId, leagueId })` in [`src/app/admin/leagues/actions.ts`](src/app/admin/leagues/actions.ts). League-scoped (the `onboardingStatus` lives on the assignment, not on Player — a user in N leagues has N independent onboarding states); rejects when the player has no assignment in the supplied league (cross-league isolation; admin in League A can't reset onboarding for a player in League B); idempotent no-op when already NOT_YET. **Preserves all existing data** — the action only flips the status flag. PR ζ's onboarding form is idempotent on re-entry (already prefills with prior submissions), so re-routing the user through it surfaces their prior data pre-filled with no data loss. NOT_YET assignments don't show the button (clicking would be a no-op); pre-staged players without an active assignment also don't show it. Inserts a required ID-upload step between ζ's onboarding form and the welcome page: front + back photo of the user's ID upload to Vercel Blob, consent line per operator decision 2026-05-02 ("we will only ever use your ID for the sole purpose of booking more courts for the league"). **Schema delta:** three additive nullable columns on `Player` — `idFrontUrl String?` + `idBackUrl String?` + `idUploadedAt DateTime?`. Form completion redirects to `/join/[code]/id-upload` instead of `/welcome`. Two new server actions in `src/app/join/[code]/actions.ts`: `submitIdUpload(formData)` — FormData action (binary file streaming; base64 round-trip would inflate ~33% and hit Vercel's 4.5MB body cap on photos); validates session + bound user + both files present + `BLOB_READ_WRITE_TOKEN` set; uploads via `@vercel/blob.put({ access: 'public', addRandomSuffix: false })` to stable paths `player-id/<playerId>/{front|back}-<timestamp>.<ext>` (timestamp suffix = re-upload-safe without orphaning prior assets); writes Player URLs + `idUploadedAt: new Date()`; flips assignment `onboardingStatus` to COMPLETED in the same `$transaction`; redirects to `/welcome`. `skipIdUpload({ code, playerId })` — operator-gate fallback when `BLOB_READ_WRITE_TOKEN` is missing AND a soft fallback for users who don't have their ID handy at sign-up time; flips onboardingStatus to COMPLETED without writing URLs (admin sees `idUploadedAt IS NULL` in the player list and follows up out-of-band). New admin server action `adminPurgePlayerId({ playerId, leagueId })` in `src/app/admin/leagues/actions.ts` — best-effort `@vercel/blob.del([frontUrl, backUrl])` (logged on failure; no-fatal because what matters is the columns clear); nulls all three Player columns; idempotent (no-op when already purged). **Public route:** new `/join/[code]/id-upload` server component renders the upload form when `BLOB_READ_WRITE_TOKEN` is set; falls back to a "service unavailable, ask admin" surface with an inline server-action skip button when the env var is missing. Idempotent re-visit handling: `onboardingStatus === COMPLETED` → bounce to `/welcome`; `Player.name === null` (form not submitted yet) → bounce to `/onboarding`; otherwise render the upload form. The `/join/[code]` resolver's three-stage redirect updated post-η: COMPLETED → `/welcome`; NOT_YET + name set → `/id-upload`; NOT_YET + no name → `/onboarding`. **Client form** (`IdUploadForm.tsx`): two `<input type="file">` fields with `accept="image/jpeg,image/png,image/heic,image/webp,image/heif,application/pdf"` and per-field 8MB cap (well within Vercel Blob's per-call limit); image previews via `URL.createObjectURL` for verification before submit; FormData submission with `code` + `playerId` injected as hidden values. A separate "Skip for now — admin will collect ID later" affordance below the submit button calls `skipIdUpload` directly so users can defer without the operator-gate fallback. **Admin UI:** new `IdViewerDialog.tsx` component renders a modal with front + back image panes side-by-side, the upload timestamp, and a Purge button gated by `ConfirmDialog`. Per-row "ID" button on PlayersTab (desktop + mobile, only visible when `Player.idUploadedAt` is set; uses the lucide `IdCard` icon) opens the dialog. PlayersTab's `PlayerRow` interface gains `idFrontUrl` / `idBackUrl` / `idUploadedAt` fields surfaced from the existing `prisma.player` include in `getLeaguePlayers`. The page-level type-safe boundary coerces `idUploadedAt` to ISO string with the v1.17.1 cache-Date-trap defense (`x instanceof Date ? x.toISOString() : String(x)`) since `getLeaguePlayers` is wrapped in `unstable_cache` (JSON-round-trips Dates → strings). **Tests:** new `tests/unit/idUploadSchema.test.ts` (5 cases — schema columns + migration purely additive). Operator can ship η with token unset (no functional regression for users since the skip flow lets them complete onboarding); the admin would just collect IDs out-of-band until the env var lands. **Out of scope:** PR θ — Reset onboarding admin action (flips `onboardingStatus` back to NOT_YET while preserving data; admin notifies user verbally, who is then redirected through the flow on next visit). Closes the loop on the redemption flow ε pre-staged: admin-generated `LeagueInvite` codes are now redeemable end-to-end. **Schema delta:** new `enum OnboardingStatus { NOT_YET COMPLETED }` + `enum JoinSource { ADMIN SELF_SERVE CODE PERSONAL }`. `PlayerLeagueAssignment.onboardingStatus OnboardingStatus @default(NOT_YET)` — added with DEFAULT COMPLETED first so existing rows backfill to "already onboarded" (active players don't get retroactively gated), then default flipped to NOT_YET so future admin pre-stages and `/join/[code]` redemptions enter the redemption flow. `PlayerLeagueAssignment.joinSource JoinSource?` — nullable for backfill compat; new writes are tagged at the source (ADMIN / SELF_SERVE / CODE / PERSONAL). `Player.onboardingPreferences Json?` — captures the form's free-form preference fields (preferredLeagueTeamId + preferredTeammateIds + preferredTeammatesFreeText). Migration `20260503010000_redemption_foundation` is purely additive — no destructive DROP against any existing column. **Code delta:** new pure helper `src/lib/joinValidation.ts#validateInvite(invite, { now, expectedLeagueId? })` returns a discriminated union over 7 outcomes (`ok` / `not-found` / `expired` / `revoked` / `used-up` / `wrong-league`) with documented branch precedence (`wrong-league > revoked > expired > used-up > ok`). Used by both the `/join/[code]` server component (UI rendering) AND the `redeemInvite` server action (race-safe re-validation inside the transaction). New routes: `/join/[code]` (server component) renders 7 branches — error states for the 4 invalid kinds + signed-out preview (PERSONAL: pinned-target card with photo/name/team/position; CODE: league preview + sign-in CTA) + signed-in PERSONAL "Is this you?" confirm + signed-in CODE roster picker (grouped by team, filtered to `Player.userId IS NULL`). `/join/[code]/onboarding` renders the post-redemption form (name required, position dropdown, optional preferred team, multi-select preferred teammates from the league's player list, "Other" free-text). `/join/[code]/welcome` renders the post-onboarding confirmation card with a CTA to the league subdomain (or apex). All three routes are public — sign-in is the YES gate, not a render-time gate, because PERSONAL invites are personalised previews that must be readable to confirm. Re-visiting `/join/[code]` while already bound + onboarded → server-side redirect to `/welcome`. Re-visiting bound-but-not-onboarded → redirect to `/onboarding` (idempotent re-entry). New server actions in `src/app/join/[code]/actions.ts`: `redeemInvite({ code, pickedPlayerId? })` — re-validates the invite at write time; resolves PERSONAL via `targetPlayerId` or CODE via `pickedPlayerId`; cross-league check rejects code-pickers picking out-of-league players; for LINE users routes through the existing v1.29.0 `linkPlayerToUser` helper (sets `Player.lineId` + dual-writes `User.playerId` ↔ `Player.userId`); for Google/email users (no lineId) sets `Player.userId` directly + mirrors `User.playerId` (the first time the codebase has a logged-in Player with `lineId IS NULL` per the rework plan §4.5); updates the existing `PlayerLeagueAssignment` with `onboardingStatus` (COMPLETED if `LeagueInvite.skipOnboarding`, else NOT_YET) + `joinSource` (CODE or PERSONAL); increments `LeagueInvite.usedCount`; all five DB writes inside one `$transaction` so partial failures don't corrupt the binding state. Returns `{ ok, onboardingStatus, redirectTo, playerId }` so the client can navigate to `/welcome` (skipOnboarding) or `/onboarding` (form) without an additional fetch. `submitOnboarding({ code, playerId, name, position, preferredLeagueTeamId, preferredTeammateIds, preferredTeammatesFreeText })` — validates the calling User is bound to the Player (defense in depth — the route only renders the form for the bound user, but the action shouldn't trust the route); writes `Player.name` / `Player.position` / `Player.onboardingPreferences` (as a JSON blob); flips `PlayerLeagueAssignment.onboardingStatus` to COMPLETED via `updateMany` (covers all the player's assignments in this league); redirects to `/welcome`. **Existing-write tagging:** `adminCreatePlayer` (PR ε) now creates assignments with `joinSource: 'ADMIN'`; `assignPlayer` admin action same. `/api/assign-player` POST now updates the player's existing `PlayerLeagueAssignment` rows with `joinSource: 'SELF_SERVE'` (only the rows where `joinSource IS NULL` — admin-tagged rows aren't downgraded). `transferPlayer`'s new assignment row stays with `joinSource: null` (transfer is a continuation, not a join event). **Tests:** new `tests/unit/joinValidation.test.ts` (16 cases — all 7 outcomes + branch precedence + boundary cases for `expiresAt === now` and `usedCount === maxUses`). New `tests/unit/redemptionFoundationSchema.test.ts` (10 cases — both enum literals + nullability invariants on the three new columns + the COMPLETED→NOT_YET default-flip ordering). New `tests/unit/redeemInvite.test.ts` (23 cases — auth gate, all 4 validation rejections + "no DB write on rejection", PERSONAL happy path including LINE vs Google/email branching + skipOnboarding routing + idempotency on already-bound, CODE flavor including cross-league rejection + roster-picker integration + joinSource tagging, single-transaction guarantee, cache busting). Existing `tests/unit/identityReworkAlphaSchema.test.ts` updated: the "α did not introduce JoinSource" assertion now reads the immutable α migration SQL instead of the live schema (which post-ζ correctly carries JoinSource). Existing `tests/unit/adminCreatePlayer.test.ts` updated for the new `joinSource: 'ADMIN'` field on assignment.create. 812 passed | 2 skipped (763 baseline + 49 new). Type-check clean.
