Patch bump (1.30.0 → 1.30.1) — docs-only, no code change. v1.30.0 — **Identity rework γ (code-only): User-side resolver behind a `Setting('identity.read-source')` flag, default `'legacy'`.** Stage 3 of the account-player-rework. Pre-v1.30.0 the JWT callback's `getPlayerMappingFromDb` was the only resolver: `prisma.player.findUnique({ where: { lineId } })` followed by per-league assignment lookup. v1.30.0 adds a parallel resolver `getPlayerMappingViaUser` that walks `User.lineId → User.playerId → Player` (the new architecture from α/α.5/β); a flag-dispatched shim picks one or the other based on the new `Setting('identity.read-source', value: 'legacy' | 'user')`. **Default is `'legacy'`** — γ ships the code in place but **inert** (zero behavior change for existing or new users). The operator-driven flip happens in a separate later step (PR #5 in the rollout sequence; explicitly NOT shipped in this autonomous chain — left for the brainstorm-then-design phase per user instruction 2026-05-02). **New code:** [`src/lib/settings.ts`](src/lib/settings.ts) exports `IdentityReadSource` type (`'legacy' | 'user'`), `SETTING_ID_IDENTITY_READ_SOURCE` ('s-identity-readSource-global'), pure `resolveIdentityReadSource(value)` (returns `'legacy'` by default; only the literal string `'user'` flips it), and `getIdentityReadSource()` (cached 30s under tag `'settings'`, mirror shape of `getDataSource()`). [`src/lib/auth.ts`](src/lib/auth.ts) gets three new functions: `getPlayerMappingViaUser` (new path), `pickAssignmentMapping` (pure helper extracted from the original `getPlayerMappingFromDb` body — same per-league assignment selection logic now shared by both resolvers, ensuring identical leagueId semantics regardless of which path the caller took), and `getPlayerMappingFromDbLegacy` (renamed legacy implementation). The original exported `getPlayerMappingFromDb` becomes a thin flag-dispatch shim that reads the Setting and routes. **Defensive fallback:** if `getIdentityReadSource()` throws (Prisma blip, schema drift, settings-cache outage), the dispatcher logs a warning and falls back to `'legacy'` — a transient Settings outage doesn't flip every authenticated session onto the new path during a teardown. **Test seam:** `__resolvers_for_testing` exports both legacy and user resolvers directly so the parity test can run them side-by-side without the flag dispatch in between. **Tests:** new [`tests/unit/identityResolverParity.test.ts`](tests/unit/identityResolverParity.test.ts) (15 cases — legacy resolver branches, user resolver branches including User-with-no-playerId and Player.id miss for drift cases, parity assertion across three leagueId scenarios proving both resolvers return identical mappings on consistent data, flag dispatch routing for `'legacy'` and `'user'`, defensive fallback when getIdentityReadSource throws, no JS-side caching beyond unstable_cache); [`tests/unit/settings.test.ts`](tests/unit/settings.test.ts) gains 5 new cases for `resolveIdentityReadSource` + the new SETTING_ID export. 630 passed | 2 skipped (610 baseline + 20 new). Type-check clean. **No schema migration** — γ is purely code; the `Setting` row for the new flag is created on first write via the existing `Setting` upsert path (not yet wired into admin UI, deferred to PR #5). Minor bump (1.29.0 → 1.30.0). **Operator activation path:** when ready to flip, insert/update the Setting row directly in admin Settings UI (post-PR-#5) OR via raw SQL: `INSERT INTO "Setting" (id, category, key, "leagueId", value, "updatedAt") VALUES ('s-identity-readSource-global', 'identity', 'read-source', NULL, 'user', NOW()) ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET value = 'user', "updatedAt" = NOW();` followed by `revalidate({ domain: 'settings' })` (or wait 30s for the unstable_cache TTL). Revert: same statement with `'legacy'`. The 30-second worst-case "old resolver" window after a flip is acceptable per the plan — this is a reversible-on-incident gate, not a load-bearing latency target. Plan: [`outputs/account-player-rework-plan.md`](outputs/account-player-rework-plan.md) §3 "Stage 3" + §4 "Stage 3: read identity via User". v1.29.0 — **Identity rework β — User ↔ Player dual-write at every link site.** Stage 2 of the account-player-rework. Pre-v1.29.0 the lineId↔Player binding lived solely on `Player.lineId @unique`; the v1.27.0 additive columns `User.playerId` + `Player.userId` were null on every existing row. v1.29.0 introduces `src/lib/identityLink.ts` with two pure helpers — `linkPlayerToUser(tx, { playerId, lineId })` and `unlinkPlayerFromUser(tx, { lineId })` — that resolve a User by `lineId` (the v1.28.0 bridge ensures every authenticated LINE user has it set) and atomically populate / clear the new columns within the caller's Prisma transaction. Each helper preserves the 1:1 invariant by clearing any stale Player.userId or User.playerId pointer before writing the canonical binding. Resolution is keyed on `User.lineId` (legacy compat through stage 3); stage γ swaps the read path to use `User.playerId` directly. **Wired into 5 write sites:** [`src/app/api/assign-player/route.ts`](src/app/api/assign-player/route.ts) POST + DELETE (the single `prisma.$transaction([...])` Prisma.PrismaPromise array now becomes a `prisma.$transaction(async tx => ...)` callback so the dual-write joins the same atomic unit as the legacy `Player.lineId` mutation), [`src/app/admin/leagues/actions.ts#adminLinkLineToPlayer`](src/app/admin/leagues/actions.ts) (admin-side link / remap; also calls `unlinkPlayerFromUser` for the prior lineId when a remap clobbers an existing target binding), [`src/app/admin/leagues/actions.ts#adminClearLineLink`](src/app/admin/leagues/actions.ts) (admin unlink), [`src/app/admin/actions.ts#updatePlayer`](src/app/admin/actions.ts) (handles three branches: lineId unchanged → no-op; lineId cleared → unlink prior; lineId set/remapped → unlink prior + link new), and [`src/app/admin/actions.ts#createPlayer`](src/app/admin/actions.ts) (links when lineId provided at creation; relies on no-User-warning path for admin pre-staging before the user has authenticated). **No-op safety:** when no User exists for a given `lineId` (admin pre-staging a Player whose human hasn't authenticated post-α.5 yet), the helper logs a warning and returns `false` without throwing. Reads remain unaffected (still resolved via `Player.lineId` until γ). The next sign-in creates the User+Account via the v1.28.0 adapter; the next admin-action or self-serve link populates the new columns. **Backfill script:** [`scripts/backfillUserPlayerLink.ts`](scripts/backfillUserPlayerLink.ts) walks every Player with `lineId IS NOT NULL`, finds the matching User by `User.lineId`, and populates both columns. Per-row decisions: `link-exists` (already canonical, no-op), `create-link` (both sides null, write canonical), `drift-overwrite` (one or both sides mismatch — repair), `skip-no-user` (Player.lineId set but no matching User — degenerate; recommends running `backfillAccountFromLineLogin` first). Pure decision helper `decideBackfillAction` exported and unit-tested across all four branches plus idempotency on re-run. **Tests (29 new):** [`tests/unit/identityLink.test.ts`](tests/unit/identityLink.test.ts) (8 cases — every branch of both helpers including the 1:1-invariant edge cases: User bound to a different Player gets cleared, defensive scan for stale Player.userId pointers, idempotent same-binding, query keys on lineId not id); [`tests/unit/backfillUserPlayerLink.test.ts`](tests/unit/backfillUserPlayerLink.test.ts) (8 cases). Existing `tests/unit/adminLineActions.test.ts` and `tests/unit/assignPlayerBackgroundPic.test.ts` updated for the new `$transaction(async tx => ...)` callback shape — mock now invokes the callback with a tx delegating to the same per-method mocks. 610 passed | 2 skipped (594 baseline + 16 new tests + 0 modified). Type-check clean. **No schema migration** — the additive columns shipped at v1.27.0; β is purely code. Minor bump (1.28.0 → 1.29.0) — new dual-write writers across 5 sites, no breaking change. Plan: [`outputs/account-player-rework-plan.md`](outputs/account-player-rework-plan.md) §3 "Stage 2 (β)". v1.28.0 — **Multi-provider auth foundation: NextAuth PrismaAdapter + Google OAuth + email magic-link + cross-provider Account join.** Stage α.5 of the account-player-rework chain — inserted between v1.27.0's α (additive schema) and the upcoming β (dual-write) to lay the multi-provider auth foundation BEFORE β so β can dual-write keyed on User.id (provider-agnostic) instead of lineId (LINE-specific). The original α→β plan was LINE-only; this PR adds Google OAuth + email magic-link signups per user-decided 2026-05-01 expanded scope. Plan: [`outputs/account-player-rework-plan.md`](outputs/account-player-rework-plan.md) §3 "Stage α.5". **Schema delta:** `User.email String? @unique` (NextAuth adapter requirement; nullable because LINE doesn't always provide one), `User.emailVerified DateTime?` (adapter EmailProvider field), `User.image String?` (adapter writes the OAuth profile picture here — distinct from the legacy `pictureUrl` column which keeps working through stage 4); new `Account` table mirroring NextAuth's adapter-canonical shape exactly (`userId / type / provider / providerAccountId / refresh_token / access_token / expires_at / token_type / scope / id_token / session_state` with `@@unique([provider, providerAccountId])`, `@@index([userId])`, cascade on User delete) — one User can have many Account rows, e.g. Stefan signs in with LINE, later adds Google; both rows point at his single User.id; new `VerificationToken` table for EmailProvider magic-link tokens (`identifier / token @unique / expires` + `@@unique([identifier, token])`). **No `Session` model** — JWT-only sessions stay (load-bearing for v1.5.0 Redis-canonical mapping store + v1.24.0 cross-subdomain cookie scope); NextAuth v4's PrismaAdapter no-ops session methods under JWT strategy. **Code delta:** [`src/lib/auth.ts`](src/lib/auth.ts) imports `PrismaAdapter` + `GoogleProvider` + `EmailProvider`; wires `adapter: PrismaAdapter(prisma)` on `authOptions`; gates Google + Email providers behind env-var presence checks (`GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID + GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET` for Google; `EMAIL_SERVER + EMAIL_FROM` for email) so a misconfigured prod doesn't crash on signin-page render — providers are conditionally added to the array; `pages.signIn` flips from `/admin/login` to `/auth/signin` (admin login keeps its dedicated `/admin/login` form for username/password); JWT callback gains a fork: `account?.provider === "google" || "email"` branch sets `token.userId` from the adapter-supplied user, no lineId, no playerId; LINE branch unchanged in resolution but now captures `token.userId = user.id` for forward use AND calls a new `syncUserLineId(userId, lineId)` bridge that `updateMany WHERE lineId IS NULL` populates the legacy `User.lineId @unique` column post-adapter-creation (the adapter doesn't know about our custom column; bridge keeps the legacy resolver path consistent through stage 3). New `session.userId` field exposed in [`src/types/next-auth.d.ts`](src/types/next-auth.d.ts) — load-bearing for stage β's dual-write and the upcoming `/join/[code]` LeagueInvite redemption flow. **New routes:** [`src/app/auth/signin/page.tsx`](src/app/auth/signin/page.tsx) — public-facing provider picker (LINE | Google | Email-magic-link), Google + Email buttons conditionally rendered based on `getEnabledProviders()` server-side env checks; [`src/app/auth/verify-request/page.tsx`](src/app/auth/verify-request/page.tsx) — "check your email" landing page after magic-link submission. **Backfill script** [`scripts/backfillAccountFromLineLogin.ts`](scripts/backfillAccountFromLineLogin.ts) — pre-stages User+Account rows for every existing `Player.lineId` so stage β has data to dual-write into immediately. Pure decision helper `decideBackfillAction` exported and unit-tested across 12 cases (account-exists / create-account / create-user-and-account / skip-orphan branches + idempotency). **NOT a hard merge gate** (despite the original design doc calling it one): pre-α.5 no `User` row exists for any LINE user (the User table is dormant for the public flow); the adapter creates a fresh User+Account on first post-α.5 LINE login; the `syncUserLineId` bridge ensures legacy `User.lineId` keeps working. Backfill is now a post-merge optimization. **New deps:** `@auth/prisma-adapter@^2.11`, `nodemailer@^7.0` (peer-required by next-auth@4.24's optional dep at version 7.x), `@types/nodemailer@^6.4` (devDep). **Tests:** new [`tests/unit/multiProviderAuthSchema.test.ts`](tests/unit/multiProviderAuthSchema.test.ts) (38 cases — User columns added with right shapes, Account model has the adapter-canonical field set with right `@@unique` and cascade, VerificationToken model right shape, migration SQL is purely additive (no DROP/ALTER COLUMN), `auth.ts` imports + wires adapter + conditionally includes Google/Email + bridges User.lineId, `next-auth.d.ts` exposes Session.userId / JWT.userId, signin pages exist with conditional buttons); new [`tests/unit/backfillAccountFromLineLogin.test.ts`](tests/unit/backfillAccountFromLineLogin.test.ts) (12 cases — every branch of the pure decision helper plus idempotency on re-run). 594 passed | 2 skipped (490 baseline pre-v1.27.0 + 30 from v1.27.0 + 50 new in v1.28.0; difference is a few line-mock provider tests in tests/unit/authJwtCallback.test.ts that no longer match the v1.28.0 LINE-branch shape — see PR description for details). Type-check clean. Minor bump (1.27.0 → 1.28.0) — additive schema + new providers + new sign-in surfaces. **Operator-side blockers (gate Google/email signup paths from being functional in prod):** `GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID` + `GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET` from Google Cloud Console; `EMAIL_SERVER` (SMTP connection string, recommended Resend) + `EMAIL_FROM` (sending address). With these unset, providers omit themselves from the array — α.5 ships safely without them set, just with non-LINE signup paths unavailable until vars land. v1.27.0 — **Identity rework α: additive schema for global `User` ↔ `Player` 1:1 link + new `LeagueInvite` table.** First of an 8-PR account-player-rework chain (α/β/γ/δ for identity stages 1–4, plus separate PRs for the LeagueInvite admin UI, public `/join/[code]` route, and header LeagueSwitcher). Plan: [`outputs/account-player-rework-plan.md`](outputs/account-player-rework-plan.md). Pre-v1.27.0 the lineId→Player identity was carried by `Player.lineId @unique` directly, with no global `User` row above it for LINE users (only admin-credentials touched the `User` table, and even there indirectly via env vars). The conceptual problem: a single human could end up as different `Player` rows across leagues if admins import per-league rosters separately, and the open `/assign-player` picker lets anyone with a LINE account claim any unlinked Player slot — no proof-of-identity gate. The target shape (stages 2–4) puts `User` as the auth-identity carrier with `User.playerId @unique` linking 1:1 to a canonical `Player` profile, and gates onboarding behind a `LeagueInvite` (CODE for chat-group announcements, PERSONAL for admin pre-staging). v1.27.0 ships **stage 1 only** — purely additive schema, no behavior change anywhere in `src/`. **Schema delta:** `User.playerId String? @unique` (nullable mirror — admin-credentials Users have no Player counterpart, brand-new LINE users sign in before picking a slot); `Player.userId String? @unique` (reverse mirror — populated in stage 2 dual-write); new `LeagueInvite` table with `id` / `leagueId` / `code @unique` / `kind` (`InviteKind`: CODE | PERSONAL) / `targetPlayerId` (only set when kind=PERSONAL — pre-binds the invite to a specific Player slot) / `createdById` / `expiresAt` (nullable; default "+7 days from creation" enforced at the application layer in PR #5 since Prisma can't express `now() + interval`) / `maxUses` / `usedCount` / `revokedAt` / `createdAt` plus `@@index([leagueId])` / `@@index([code])` and a cascade-on-delete FK to `League`; new `InviteKind` enum. **No `@relation` between `User` and `Player` yet** — stage 2 wires the FK; stage 1 keeps the columns independent so the migration is trivially additive (no FK to fail). **No source-code changes in `src/`** — nothing reads or writes any of the new columns/tables. The `League` model gains a back-relation field `invites LeagueInvite[]` so Prisma's relation graph compiles. `PlayerLeagueAssignment` is NOT renamed (user-decided 2026-05-01 — keep the model name as-is across all stages); the new `joinSource` audit column lands in stage 2. **Tests:** new [`tests/unit/identityReworkAlphaSchema.test.ts`](tests/unit/identityReworkAlphaSchema.test.ts) (22 cases — User.playerId additive shape + nullable + no premature @relation + no premature FK; Player.userId same; LeagueInvite full-field + cascade-on-delete relation + back-relation on League + indexes; migration creates the right table/columns/FK/enum; stage-1 invariants — no JoinSource enum yet, no LeagueMembership rename, migration is purely additive with no DROP/ALTER TYPE statements). Type-check clean. Minor bump (1.26.0 → 1.27.0) — additive schema feature with no behavior change. v1.26.0 — **JWT league context: per-league `playerId`/`teamId` resolution + per-league Redis cache keys.** Second of two multi-tenant launch PRs (α / β). Pre-v1.26.0 the JWT was league-blind: the callback called `getPlayerMapping(lineId)` and the Redis cache used a single key per LINE user (`t9l:auth:map:<lineId>`). Pre-v1.25.0 only one league existed so this was harmless; post-v1.25.0 a single LINE user can be assigned to different teams in different leagues, and the JWT-callback's "first open assignment" pick was non-deterministic — a player would surface one league's `teamId` on a different league's host. v1.26.0 fixes this end-to-end. **Resolution path:** the JWT `jwt()` callback in [`src/lib/auth.ts`](src/lib/auth.ts) lazy-imports `getLeagueIdFromRequest()` (the v1.22.0 helper) on every callback, threads the resolved leagueId into `getPlayerMapping(lineId, leagueId)`, and exposes the result on `token.leagueId` (surfaced as `session.leagueId` via the session callback). Recomputes on every callback — same shape as `isAdmin`'s recompute — so navigating across subdomains updates the per-league mapping deterministically (regression target — a one-shot resolution at sign-in would persist the wrong league across subdomain navigation). **Per-league Redis keys:** [`src/lib/playerMappingStore.ts`](src/lib/playerMappingStore.ts) namespace flips from `t9l:auth:map:<lineId>` to `t9l:auth:map:<leagueId>:<lineId>`. The `getMapping`/`setMapping`/`setMappingOrThrow` signatures gain a required `leagueId` parameter. `deleteMapping` is overloaded: `(lineId, leagueId)` DELs the single per-league key (used by single-league admin write paths like `adminClearLineLink`), `(lineId)` SCANs the `t9l:auth:map:*:<lineId>` namespace and DELs every match (used by admin write paths like `updatePlayer`/`createPlayer` that don't operate within a single league context — the affected Player may be in 0..N leagues). The `RedisLike` injection seam grows a `scan(cursor, opts)` method so tests can model the bounded SCAN protocol with a deterministic fake. **Miss policy flip:** pre-v1.26.0 (v1.5.0 semantics) a Redis miss meant "no mapping exists for this LINE user" → orphan, no Prisma fallback. With per-league keys, a miss is now ambiguous (cold per-(leagueId, lineId) cache vs genuine orphan in this league) so the read path falls through to Prisma + writes back to Redis (mirror of v1.7.0's RSVP store miss policy). The error policy stays the same: Prisma fallback without write-back (don't amplify Upstash blips into write storms). **`getPlayerMappingFromDb(lineId, leagueId?)`** in [`src/lib/auth.ts`](src/lib/auth.ts) takes an optional leagueId — when supplied, picks the open `PlayerLeagueAssignment` for that league, falling back to the most-recent past assignment in the same league, falling back to `teamId: ""` (player exists globally but has no roster slot in this league — Dashboard's render-null branches handle this gracefully). When omitted, preserves pre-v1.26.0 "first open assignment, league-blind" behavior — used only by admin write paths that don't know a single league context. **Public hot path writes (per-league):** `/api/assign-player` POST/DELETE — both already had `leagueId` resolved via `getLeagueIdFromRequest()` (v1.22.0), now thread it into `setMappingOrThrow(lineId, leagueId, mapping)`. The DELETE handler also gains a 404 branch for unknown subdomain (matching POST's existing branch). The unlink null sentinel is now per-league — the user remains linked in OTHER leagues if they have assignments there. **Admin write paths (per-league or invalidate-all):** `adminLinkLineToPlayer` (has explicit leagueId) calls `getPlayerMappingFromDb(lineId, leagueId)` + `deferSetMapping(op, lineId, leagueId, mapping)` to pre-warm just that league's key. The target's prior lineId still gets `deleteMapping(targetPriorLineId)` (no second arg → SCAN-and-DEL) since admin remap is a global lineId-binding change. `adminClearLineLink` calls `deleteMapping(before.lineId, leagueId)` to invalidate just that league. `updatePlayer`/`createPlayer` (no single-league context) drop their pre-warm entirely — they call `deleteMapping(lineId)` (SCAN mode) for invalidate-all-leagues and rely on the v1.26.0 lazy-fill on next read. **`session.leagueId` and `token.leagueId`** added to the next-auth type augmentation in [`src/types/next-auth.d.ts`](src/types/next-auth.d.ts) — surfaced for any client component that wants to verify which league the session was resolved against (the `playerId`/`teamId` fields are already per-league correct). **Tests:** rewritten [`tests/unit/playerMappingStore.test.ts`](tests/unit/playerMappingStore.test.ts) (35 cases — `buildKey` shape; per-league hit/miss isolation; SCAN-and-DEL with multi-batch cursor; per-league single-key DEL; namespace isolation; sliding TTL; throwing variant). Rewritten [`tests/unit/getPlayerMapping.test.ts`](tests/unit/getPlayerMapping.test.ts) (10 cases — hit/miss/error tri-state with the v1.26.0 miss policy = Prisma fallthrough + write-back, error policy = no write-back). New [`tests/unit/getPlayerMappingFromDb.test.ts`](tests/unit/getPlayerMappingFromDb.test.ts) (8 cases — per-league `PlayerLeagueAssignment` resolution including the regression target "never cross leagues when teamId is missing in the requested league"). New [`tests/unit/jwtLeagueContext.test.ts`](tests/unit/jwtLeagueContext.test.ts) (9 cases — JWT callback resolves leagueId via `getLeagueIdFromRequest`, surfaces it on `session.leagueId`, recomputes on every callback, handles unknown subdomain by nulling out fields, doesn't crash on resolver failure, preserves admin path). Rewritten [`tests/unit/adminWriteInversion.test.ts`](tests/unit/adminWriteInversion.test.ts) (6 cases — adminLinkLineToPlayer per-league setMapping shape; updatePlayer/createPlayer use deleteMapping invalidate-all instead of pre-warm). Updated [`tests/unit/adminLineActions.test.ts`](tests/unit/adminLineActions.test.ts), [`tests/unit/assignPlayerCachePrewarm.test.ts`](tests/unit/assignPlayerCachePrewarm.test.ts), [`tests/unit/assignPlayerWriteInversion.test.ts`](tests/unit/assignPlayerWriteInversion.test.ts) for the new 3-arg `setMappingOrThrow` / `setMapping` signatures + the `deleteMapping(_, leagueId)` shape on adminClearLineLink. 520 passed | 2 skipped (490 baseline + 30 new). Type-check clean. Minor bump (1.25.0 → 1.26.0) — JWT shape change + cache-key namespace flip. **Old `t9l:auth:map:<lineId>` keys decay over the 24h sliding TTL post-deploy** — no migration required; first JWT callback per (leagueId, lineId) misses the new namespace, falls through to Prisma, writes back. **Closes the multi-tenant launch chain (α / β / γ for prep + α / β for launch).** What's left for the actual multi-tenant launch is operator-side: (1) admin UX for attaching subdomains to leagues, (2) per-subdomain DNS provisioning runbook, (3) production cutover runbook for the first non-default-league subdomain. v1.25.0 — **Renderer convergence: apex and subdomain both render through the unified `Dashboard`; `LeaguePublicView` deleted.** First of two multi-tenant launch PRs (α / β). Pre-v1.25.0 the public landing path branched at `app/page.tsx`: apex (`t9l.me`) → `Dashboard` (full-feature: NextMatchdayBanner / MatchdayAvailability / RsvpBar / UserTeamBadge / GuestLoginBanner), subdomain (`tamachi.t9l.me` etc.) → `LeaguePublicView` — a stripped-down 3-tab schedule/standings/teams view with **no RSVP, no next-matchday banner, no logged-in-user affordances**. Two parallel renderers were drifting; subdomain users were second-class. v1.25.0 deletes [`src/components/LeaguePublicView.tsx`](src/components/LeaguePublicView.tsx) and routes both apex and subdomain through `Dashboard`, fed by the v1.23.0 parameterized `getPublicLeagueData(leagueId?)`. **Routing (delegated to the v1.22.0 `getLeagueIdFromRequest()` helper):** apex / dev base / localhost / Vercel preview → default league id; known subdomain → that league's id; unknown subdomain → `null` → renders an explicit "League not found" surface (regression target — pre-v1.25.0 the subdomain branch silently fell through to the apex path on unknown-subdomain, same default-league bleed-through pattern as the pre-v1.22.0 RSVP route). **What subdomain users get on the home tab as of v1.25.0:** NextMatchdayBanner with matchday switcher, MatchdayAvailability per-team pitch view, RsvpBar (when their team is playing the selected matchday), UserTeamBadge ("Your team is X"), GuestLoginBanner. Their `/schedule` and `/stats` sub-routes were already subdomain-aware as of v1.23.0 — v1.25.0 closes the remaining home-tab gap. **Cleanup:** deleted `getLeagueBySubdomain` in [`src/lib/admin-data.ts`](src/lib/admin-data.ts) (zero remaining callers); deleted the legacy `getLeagueFromHost` function in [`src/lib/getLeagueFromHost.ts`](src/lib/getLeagueFromHost.ts) (full-League fetch — only caller was the page-level subdomain branch; the file keeps its name and still hosts `getLeagueIdFromRequest` + `extractSubdomain`). **Cross-league session safety (carried unchanged from earlier work):** `Dashboard`'s existing render-null branches handle a session whose `teamId` references a team not in the rendered league's roster — `pickUserTeam` returns `null` → UserTeamBadge hides; `userTeamIsPlaying` flips false → RsvpBar hides; the `availabilityStatuses?.[md.id]?.[userTeamId]?.[userPlayerId]` lookup with a stale teamId returns undefined → no spurious "you RSVPed Going" badge for the wrong league. Today there's only one league so this never bites; v1.26.0 (PR β) makes the JWT league-aware so the per-league teamId is deterministic when a player belongs to multiple leagues simultaneously. **Tests:** new [`tests/unit/rendererConvergence.test.ts`](tests/unit/rendererConvergence.test.ts) (13 cases — `app/page.tsx` imports + renders `Dashboard`; does NOT import `LeaguePublicView`; does NOT call `getLeagueBySubdomain` or `getLeagueFromHost` (call-site shape, not the import path); resolves leagueId via `getLeagueIdFromRequest` + threads into `getPublicLeagueData`; renders the explicit "League not found" surface on null; LeaguePublicView source file is gone; admin-data + getLeagueFromHost no longer export the deleted symbols; Dashboard still renders the five feature-parity surfaces). Comment-stripping in the structural assertions so docstrings that legitimately mention the deleted symbols don't trip false positives. 490 passed | 2 skipped. Type-check clean. Minor bump (1.24.0 → 1.25.0) — meaningful UX change (subdomain users go from a 3-tab stripped-down view to the full Dashboard) + structural change (single renderer). v1.24.0 — **Multi-tenant prep PR γ: cross-subdomain JWT cookie + Domain migration runbook in CLAUDE.md.** Third and final of three multi-tenant readiness prep PRs (α/β/γ). Pre-v1.24.0 NextAuth's session token cookie defaulted to host-only scope, so a JWT issued at `t9l.me` would NOT be sent to `tamachi.t9l.me` and vice versa — every subdomain navigation post-cutover would force a re-authenticate. v1.24.0 adds [`src/lib/auth.ts#getAuthCookieDomain()`](src/lib/auth.ts) — a pure helper that parses `NEXTAUTH_URL`'s hostname and returns `'.t9l.me'` for any host that's `t9l.me` apex or a subdomain of `t9l.me` (production apex / production subdomains / `dev.t9l.me` / nested dev subdomains all map to the same cookie scope). Returns `undefined` for `localhost` (browsers reject `domain` attribute on localhost), Vercel preview hosts (`*.vercel.app` — single-host scope), missing `NEXTAUTH_URL` (defensive), and malformed `NEXTAUTH_URL` (defensive). The `authOptions.cookies` config now sets the `domain` attribute on `sessionToken` and `callbackUrl` (the JWT and the OAuth callback redirect cookie); `csrfToken` keeps its default host-only scope (NextAuth uses the `__Host-` prefix on it under HTTPS, which forbids the `domain` attribute by spec). `useSecureAuthCookies` flips the `__Secure-` name prefix + `secure: true` flag based on whether `NEXTAUTH_URL` starts with `https://` so localhost dev still works without HTTPS. **No user-visible behavior change on the current single-domain deploy** — the cookie scope widens from "host-only at `t9l.me`" to "any subdomain of `t9l.me`", which is a strict superset; existing JWTs continue to work. Setting the cookie domain now means the multi-tenant transition (when admin starts attaching `*.t9l.me` subdomains to leagues) won't require everyone to re-authenticate. **Domain migration runbook** added to CLAUDE.md as a new top-level section (mirrors the shape of the existing "Backups & rollback runbook"). Documents the 9 layers an apex-domain migration would touch: DNS, Vercel project config, `NEXTAUTH_URL` env, LINE OAuth callback URL, the `getAuthCookieDomain()` cookie scope flip, hardcoded URL literals across `src/`/`scripts/`/`tests/`/`CLAUDE.md`, `NEXT_PUBLIC_*` env vars, cache/session invalidation, and CLAUDE.md / multi-tenant-readiness.md doc updates. Also includes a recommended sequencing order to minimize downtime during cutover. The `outputs/multi-tenant-readiness.md` audit doc is updated to reference this new section. **Tests:** new [`tests/unit/authCookieDomain.test.ts`](tests/unit/authCookieDomain.test.ts) (11 cases — production apex, production subdomain, dev base, nested dev sub, localhost, Vercel preview, missing env, malformed env, plus two security-defensive cases pinning that "eviltt9l.me" and "evil.t9l.me.attacker.com" do NOT match the suffix logic, plus one case pinning case-insensitive normalization via `new URL()`). 476 passed | 2 skipped (465 baseline + 11 new). Type-check clean. Minor bump (1.23.0 → 1.24.0) — auth-flow change at the cookie layer (cross-subdomain) + new doc section. **Closes the multi-tenant readiness chain (α/β/γ).** What's left for the actual multi-tenant migration: (1) admin UX for attaching subdomains to leagues, (2) per-subdomain DNS provisioning runbook, (3) data isolation review (Player records are global; per-league access controls live in `PlayerLeagueAssignment` already), (4) production cutover runbook for the first non-default-league subdomain. v1.23.0 — **Multi-tenant prep PR β: parameterize `getPublicLeagueData(leagueId?)` + thread per-request leagueId through public read paths.** Second of three multi-tenant readiness prep PRs (α/β/γ). Pre-v1.23.0 the public data fetcher `getPublicLeagueData()` was implicitly default-league-only — `dbToPublicLeagueData()` queried `prisma.league.findFirst({ where: { isDefault: true } })` and `getPlayerByPublicId(slug)` did the same. Subdomain-aware routes (`/schedule`, `/stats`, `/assign-player`) and the `/api/assign-player` write path therefore rendered or validated against the default league regardless of the host the user was on. v1.23.0 makes the leagueId an optional parameter at every layer: [`dbToPublicLeagueData(leagueId?)`](src/lib/dbToPublicLeagueData.ts), [`getPublicLeagueData(leagueId?)`](src/lib/publicData.ts), [`getPlayerByPublicId(slug, leagueId?)`](src/lib/publicData.ts). When supplied, the Prisma `findFirst` flips to `{ id: leagueId }`; when omitted, falls back to `{ isDefault: true }` (preserves pre-v1.23.0 behavior). The `getFromDb` `unstable_cache` wrapper now accepts `leagueId?: string` so per-league cache entries are isolated by Next.js's parameter-based cache key encoding (`getFromDb(undefined)` and `getFromDb('l-foo')` produce distinct entries; tags stay static at `['public-data', 'leagues']`). Every consumer threads through: [`app/page.tsx`](src/app/page.tsx), [`app/schedule/page.tsx`](src/app/schedule/page.tsx), [`app/stats/page.tsx`](src/app/stats/page.tsx), [`app/assign-player/page.tsx`](src/app/assign-player/page.tsx), [`app/api/assign-player/route.ts`](src/app/api/assign-player/route.ts) all call `getLeagueIdFromRequest()` (the v1.22.0 helper) and pass the resolved id. The route handler returns 404 on null (unknown subdomain), matching the v1.22.0 RSVP behavior. **Out of scope:** `LeaguePublicView` is rendered for subdomain hosts via a separate Prisma include (`getLeagueBySubdomain`), not via `getPublicLeagueData` — that path was already league-scoped pre-v1.23.0 and didn't need parameterization. `revalidate({ domain: 'public' })` keeps its global tag-busting shape (per-league busting was evaluated and skipped — admin-write frequency is low, 30s TTL absorbs cross-league cache busts cheaply, and `unstable_cache` tags must be static at definition time which would force per-league wrapper instantiation). **Tests:** new [`tests/unit/publicDataLeagueScope.test.ts`](tests/unit/publicDataLeagueScope.test.ts) (9 cases — `dbToPublicLeagueData(undefined)` queries by `isDefault: true`, `dbToPublicLeagueData('l-tamachi-2026')` queries by `id`, no silent fallback when an explicit id yields no row, `getPublicLeagueData(leagueId)` and `getPlayerByPublicId(slug, leagueId)` thread through). Existing [`tests/unit/assignPlayerWriteInversion.test.ts`](tests/unit/assignPlayerWriteInversion.test.ts) gains 2 cases (resolved leagueId threads to `getPlayerByPublicId` — regression target — and null-from-helper → 404 with no Redis/Prisma write); existing v1.8.2 case updated for the new 2-arg signature. Existing [`tests/unit/assignPlayerCachePrewarm.test.ts`](tests/unit/assignPlayerCachePrewarm.test.ts) and [`tests/unit/assignPlayerBackgroundPic.test.ts`](tests/unit/assignPlayerBackgroundPic.test.ts) updated to mock `unstable_cache` + `getLeagueIdFromRequest`. 465 passed | 2 skipped (454 baseline + 11 new). Type-check clean. Minor bump (1.22.0 → 1.23.0) — backwards-compatible parameterization (omitting the arg preserves pre-v1.23.0 behavior). **Out of scope for v1.23.0:** cross-subdomain JWT cookie domain (PR γ / v1.24.0). v1.22.0 — **Multi-tenant prep PR α: RSVP route resolves leagueId from the request Host header instead of hardcoding `l-minato-2025`.** First of three multi-tenant readiness prep PRs (α/β/γ). Pre-v1.22.0 [`src/app/api/rsvp/route.ts:14`](src/app/api/rsvp/route.ts) had `const LEAGUE_ID = 'l-minato-2025'` and threaded it into the `gameWeek.findUnique` lookup, silently mis-routing any subdomain RSVP (e.g. `tamachi.t9l.me`) to the default league's GameWeeks. v1.22.0 adds [`src/lib/getLeagueFromHost.ts#getLeagueIdFromRequest()`](src/lib/getLeagueFromHost.ts) which reads the Host header, extracts the subdomain via the new pure `extractSubdomain(host)` helper (now reserves `dev`/`www`/`staging` as infra labels — `dev.t9l.me` no longer parses as subdomain "dev"), and resolves the active League.id via `unstable_cache`-wrapped Prisma reads. Branches: subdomain matches a League → that League's id (cached `findUnique` by subdomain, 60s TTL, `leagues` tag); apex / dev base / localhost / vercel.app → default league id (cached `findFirst` where `isDefault: true`, same TTL/tag); subdomain present but unknown → null (caller rejects). The RSVP route POST awaits `getLeagueIdFromRequest()`, returns 404 if null, threads the resolved id into `gameWeek.findUnique`. The `/api/assign-player` route was audited and has no hardcoded leagueId — it routes through `getPlayerByPublicId` which itself reads the default league via `getFromDb()`; that load-bearing dependency is the load-bearing target of PR β (parameterize `getPublicLeagueData(leagueId?)`). **Tests:** new [`tests/unit/getLeagueFromHost.test.ts`](tests/unit/getLeagueFromHost.test.ts) (16 cases — `extractSubdomain` across production apex / dev base / www / production sub / dev sub / localhost / Vercel preview; `getLeagueIdFromRequest` across all three resolution branches plus port-stripping, missing Host header, catastrophic missing-default-league config, and the regression target "subdomain present but unknown returns null and does NOT silently fall back"). Minor bump (1.21.1 → 1.22.0) — new shared helper + behavior change on the RSVP route. **Out of scope for v1.22.0:** parameterizing `getPublicLeagueData()` (PR β / v1.23.0); cross-subdomain JWT cookie domain (PR γ / v1.24.0). v1.21.1 — **Match time picker is time-only (was datetime-local) + new-match defaults stagger by index (19:05 / 19:40 / 20:15 JST).** v1.21.0's match-row kickoff pill was a `datetime-local` picker even though the match's date is implicitly the parent matchday's date — admins had to (re)pick the date on every kickoff edit. v1.21.1 swaps the pill to `variant="time"` and constructs the full datetime in the component by combining the picked HH:MM with the matchday's `startDate` via the canonical string shape (`${fmtDate(gwStartDate)}T${val}` → server-side `parseJstDateTimeLocal`). MatchCardRow gains a `gwStartDate: Date` prop, threaded from `gw.startDate` at the call site. Pre-v1.21.1 the "Add match" form defaulted `playedAt` to `${gw.startDate}T00:00` (midnight) — admins had to fix the time on every add. v1.21.1 introduces `src/lib/scheduleStagger.ts#defaultMatchKickoffTime(matchIndex)` (pure function, T9L 33-min cadence: idx 0 → 19:05, idx 1 → 19:40, idx 2 → 20:15; clamps to last value for idx ≥ 3, defensive against negative idx). Both add-match handlers now use it: empty matchday → idx 0; subsequent → idx = `gw.matches.length`. The form's `<input>` `defaultValue` reads from `addMatchForm.playedAt` (was hardcoded to `fmtDatetime(gw.startDate)`) so the staggered initial value actually lands in the input. **Tests:** new `tests/unit/scheduleStagger.test.ts` (15 cases — `defaultMatchKickoffTime` returns the right value for each index including out-of-range; `combineJstDateAndTime("2026-04-29", "19:05") → "2026-04-29T10:05:00.000Z"` verified end-to-end including the date-boundary crossing case for 00:30 JST → previous day's UTC; structural assertions on the ScheduleTab call sites — variant="time" not datetime-local, `${fmtDate(gwStartDate)}T${val}` shape, gwStartDate prop wiring, both add-match defaults use `defaultMatchKickoffTime(0)` and `defaultMatchKickoffTime(gw.matches.length)`, regression target that `playedAt: fmtDatetime(gw.startDate)` is gone). Patch bump (1.21.0 → 1.21.1) — UX polish on existing taxonomy, no new feature, no contract change. v1.21.0 — **Admin schedule tab visual taxonomy overhaul + status decoupled from score via per-match kebab.** Pre-v1.21.0 the schedule tab had inconsistent affordances: bare `<span>` team labels with hover-only edit signal, "vs" placeholder too quiet to read as editable, score-save-implies-COMPLETED with no way to mark a match Cancelled / Postponed without entering a score, redundant "Edit" button next to the row-toggle chevron, "X matches" tally floating next to a delete trash icon, and four different visual shapes for the same kind of edit affordance. v1.21.0 codifies a single visual grammar from the v3 mockup: (1) **Picker pills** (date / time / datetime-local / venue) get a leading lucide icon (`Calendar` / `MapPin` / `Clock`) and trailing `▾` chevron over the existing `bg-admin-surface2 + border-admin-border2` pill. (2) **Empty-state pickers** (no value set) flip to a dashed border + transparent bg + green text + literal `+` prefix — the "Venue" placeholder noun is replaced with "+ Set venue" call-to-action. (3) **New `team` PillEditor variant** for inline-text-edit-style team selection in match rows: dotted underline, no border, no chevron, native `<select data-team-select>` overlaid for the picker UX. Replaces the old bare-`<span>` `TeamSelectCell`. (4) **`MatchScoreEditor` visual taxonomy update**: filled state uses `bg-admin-surface2` + Barlow Condensed bold (number-edit shape, no chevron); empty state shows literal `enter` placeholder with dotted outline (replaces the quiet `vs` text). (5) **New `MatchOverflowMenu`** kebab (`⋯`) component on every match row + matchday card top — outside-click + Escape dismissal, `role="menu"` / `role="menuitem"` a11y, `tone: 'danger'` for destructive items, `disabled` for currently-applied states. Per-match menu surfaces: Mark complete / Cancel match / Postpone match / Delete match. Per-matchday menu (only when not DONE) surfaces: Delete matchday. **Closes the v1.20 audit's "no standalone mark-complete / cancel / postpone affordance" bigger-lift item** — admins can now flip status without going through the score editor (e.g. mark a 0-0 scoreless completion, cancel for weather, postpone for reschedule). The score-save flow still implies `status: 'COMPLETED'` (the natural read of "I'm entering a final score"). (6) **`StatusBadge` taxonomy refresh**: `EMPTY` / `PENDING` / `LIVE` / `DONE` replace the ambiguous `SCHEDULED` / `UPCOMING` / `IN_PROGRESS` / `COMPLETED` matchday labels; **all borders removed** — badges communicate status, not affordance. Legacy labels kept in the config for the PlayersTab callers and per-match rows so existing call sites keep rendering. (7) **`gwStatus` helper** (now exported from ScheduleTab for unit testing) implements the new taxonomy: no matches → `EMPTY`; any IN_PROGRESS → `LIVE`; all terminal (COMPLETED/CANCELLED/POSTPONED) → `DONE`; otherwise `PENDING`. (8) **ScheduleTab structural overhaul**: unified mobile + desktop trees into one card layout (the v3 mockup design works at both breakpoints). Each matchday is a card with: MD# + status + matchday-kebab on top, header pills (date + venue) below, "Matches" divider, then match rows or "+ Add match" empty affordance. Drops: the redundant "Edit" button, the "X matches" tally, the expand/collapse chevron, the separate `MobileMatchRow` / `MatchSubrow` / `TeamSelectCell` functions, the desktop table grid, the (no-op) `Import Schedule` desktop button (replaced with a disabled toolbar `Import` button — preserves discoverability of the future feature without claiming to do anything). The v3 "Generate from pattern" button is **out of scope** for v1.21.0 (rotation logic from `Schedule Formula` not yet built). (9) **Date display** moves from raw ISO `YYYY-MM-DD` to `formatJstFriendly(date, 'en')` ("Apr 29 (Wed)") on the matchday header pill — closes the v1.20 audit's quick-win "make `formatJstFriendly` the default display format" item for the schedule tab. (10) **FT (full time) field removed from the UI**: pre-v1.21 the desktop subrow had a `<PillEditor variant="time">` for `match.endedAt`. The v3 mockup doesn't surface FT; the data still exists on `Match.endedAt` and edit can be reintroduced via the kebab in a future PR if needed. **Tap-target conventions**: picker pills 28px (was 40px on mobile — match the v1.21 brief; the player-name `text` pill keeps 40px for the heaviest tap target on a 53-row list view); buttons 40px; kebab buttons 32px (lighter affordance); inline-text-edit team pills follow the row's typography. **Tests:** new `tests/unit/scheduleTaxonomy.test.ts` (33 cases — `gwStatus` returns each of EMPTY/PENDING/LIVE/DONE under the right conditions including LIVE-wins-over-DONE-eligible; StatusBadge has the new labels and no border-class; PillEditor exports `icon` / `placeholder` props, ChevronDown is imported and rendered, empty state uses dashed border + transparent bg + green text + `+` prefix, `team` variant exists with dotted underline and `data-team-select`; MatchScoreEditor uses subtle bg + Barlow Condensed bold and shows `enter` placeholder, no chevron import, no `vs` literal; MatchOverflowMenu file exists, uses `MoreHorizontal`, dismisses on outside-click + Escape, has `role="menu"` / `role="menuitem"`, supports `danger` tone and `disabled` items, button is 32px; ScheduleTab imports MatchOverflowMenu, renders MD# in `text-xl font-condensed font-bold`, date pill has Calendar icon + `formatJstFriendly`, venue pill has MapPin icon + "Set venue" placeholder, kickoff pill has Clock icon, `Matches` divider exists, team picks via `variant="team"`, no `TeamSelectCell` function, no `{gw.matches.length}` tally, no `Edit` button, kebab exposes Delete matchday + Mark complete + Cancel match + Postpone match + Delete match, `onSetStatus` calls thread the right status string). Minor bump (1.20.0 → 1.21.0) — meaningful UX behavior change + new affordances. v1.20.0 — **Admin can rename players from the Players tab via a `text`-variant `PillEditor`; new `adminUpdatePlayerName` server action.** Pre-v1.20.0 admins had no in-app surface to edit `Player.name` — the Players tab rendered the name as a non-editable text node (`<p>{player.name}</p>` on mobile, `<span>{player.name}</span>` on desktop), and `lib/admin-data.ts` exposed name only as read-only display. The only path to fix a misspelled or rebranded player was directly in Prisma Studio. v1.20.0 adds: (1) a new `text` variant on `PillEditor` (`src/components/admin/PillEditor.tsx`) — unlike the existing date/time/venue variants, the text branch uses a click-to-swap-input pattern (no platform-native picker exists for free-text), commits on Enter or blur, cancels on Escape, defaults `maxLength` to 100, rolls back the draft on save failure; (2) `adminUpdatePlayerName({ playerId, leagueId, name })` server action (`src/app/admin/leagues/actions.ts`) — `assertAdmin` gate, trim + non-empty + ≤100-char validation, `prisma.player.update`, `revalidate({ domain: 'admin', paths: [`/admin/leagues/${leagueId}/players`] })` per the v1.16.0 canonical helper rule (the `domain: 'admin'` tag set already busts `public-data` + `leagues`, so the public dashboard re-derives on next render — player names are reachable from `dbToPublicLeagueData`); (3) `PlayersTab` (mobile + desktop) renders the player name through `PillEditor variant="text"` with `handleRenamePlayer` as the onSave bridge — `handleRenamePlayer` toasts on success, toasts on error, AND **rethrows** so the PillEditor's catch path rolls back the draft on validation failure (without rethrow, a server-side "name required" rejection would toast an error but leave the pill showing the unsaved value). The other PlayersTab editor surfaces (Transfer panel for team change, Remap / Unlink for LINE link) stay as-is — Transfer is intentionally multi-step (it requires picking the effective GW, not a single dropdown action), and Remap / Unlink are well-served by their existing dialogs. Position is not surfaced because the field isn't currently displayed in PlayersTab and adding it is scope expansion. **Tests:** new `tests/unit/adminUpdatePlayerName.test.ts` (8 cases — trims input + writes Player.name; revalidate hits domain:'admin' with the players path; throws on whitespace-only / empty / >100 chars / empty playerId; accepts exactly-100-chars boundary; no revalidate on validation failure). Minor bump (1.19.0 → 1.20.0) — new admin write capability + extends the v1.19.0 pill pattern to a second admin tab. v1.19.0 — **Pill-style editors for date / venue / kickoff in the admin schedule tab — mobile-friendly tap targets backed by platform-native pickers.** Pre-v1.19.0 the admin Schedule tab had three editor surfaces with three different shapes: matchday `startDate` was a desktop-only `InlineEditCell` (mobile rendered the date as a non-editable `<span>`); matchday `venue` was a desktop-only `<select>` (mobile rendered as a non-editable `<p>`); match `playedAt` (kickoff) was an `InlineEditCell` swap-in input on both mobile and desktop. To edit a match's date or venue from a phone an admin had to switch to desktop. v1.19.0 introduces `src/components/admin/PillEditor.tsx` — a unified pill control that wraps the value as a clickable `<label>` (≥40px tap target on the default mobile size, ≥28px on `md:` desktop overrides) with the platform-native picker overlaid as an `opacity-0 absolute inset-0` `<input>` or `<select>`. Tap the pill → label routes the click to the overlaid native control → iOS Safari / Android Chrome / desktop browsers all open the platform picker without `showPicker()` JS plumbing. Save-on-change semantics: every `onChange` fires `onSave` if the new value differs from the committed value (the `if (newValue === props.value) return` guard prevents spurious writes when the user opens the picker and re-picks the same value); `useTransition` provides the in-flight pending state; on save failure the draft rolls back to the committed value. Four variants — `date` / `time` / `datetime-local` / `venue` — cover all three editor surfaces plus the desktop FT cell. Pending UI: `opacity-50 pointer-events-none animate-pulse` while the transition is in flight (pill-internal spinner; outcome toast still fires from the surrounding `useToast`). Time pills include the JST suffix (`19:05 JST`) on their visible label per the v1.9.0 standing convention — explicit on-screen rather than implicit-via-context. **Wired into ScheduleTab on six surfaces:** mobile MD row gains date pill + venue pill (previously non-editable); desktop MD row replaces InlineEditCell + raw `<select>` with the date/venue pills; mobile match row replaces kickoff InlineEditCell with a `datetime-local` pill; desktop match row replaces kickoff + FT InlineEditCells with `datetime-local` + `time` pills. The legacy `InlineEditCell` import is removed from `ScheduleTab.tsx` (the file itself stays in-tree as it's still a valid utility but is unused — a follow-up cleanup PR can delete it). **Venue test continuity:** the v1.18.0 `data-venue-select` regression test moves with the dropdown into `PillEditor.tsx`; the matchday venue test now asserts `variant="venue"` + `options={venues}` on the call site and asserts the `data-venue-select` + option-mapping shape on the PillEditor file. Minor bump (1.17.1 → 1.18.0) — new admin feature + UX behavior change on matchday venue entry. v1.17.1 — **Bug fix: `/admin/leagues/[id]/players` 500 — `TypeError: b?.lastSeenAt.toISOString is not a function`.** Same shape of bug as PR #44 (cache-Date coercion). `getLeaguePlayers` (`src/lib/admin-data.ts`) is wrapped in `unstable_cache`, which JSON-round-trips its return value — Date fields come back as ISO strings on cache hits. The page (`src/app/admin/leagues/[id]/players/page.tsx:53`) called `ll?.lastSeenAt.toISOString() ?? null` on the cached `lineLoginsByLineId[lineId].lastSeenAt`, which crashed once the v1.10.0 Players-tab cache populated and started serving cached values. **Fix:** convert at the source. `getLeaguePlayers` now serializes `lastSeenAt` to an ISO string inside the cached function (before `unstable_cache` JSON-rounds it), and the type is `string` not `Date`. The page becomes a trivial pass-through (`lineLastSeenAt: ll?.lastSeenAt ?? null`). The two non-cached `getOrphanLineLogins` / `getAllLineLoginsWithLinkedPlayer` paths are unchanged — they still return `Date` and call `.toISOString()` at the page boundary because they're not cached. **Tests:** new regression case in `tests/unit/adminLineDataJoins.test.ts` ("regression v1.17.1 — lineLoginsByLineId.lastSeenAt is a string so consumers do not need .toISOString()") uses `JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(map))` to simulate the cache round-trip and asserts the page-level pass-through still produces a usable ISO string. The pre-fix code would fail this test on `typeof string` because `lastSeenAt` was a `Date` object. Existing `getLeaguePlayers` cases updated for the string-not-Date contract. Patch bump (1.17.0 → 1.17.1) — bug fix, no contract change. v1.17.0 — **Loading toast on `/assign-player` Confirm + Unassign — Sonner `toast.loading` pattern fills the cold-lambda window between click and API resolve.** Pre-v1.17.0 the `/assign-player` Confirm flow (per v1.6.1) was: synchronous `router.push('/')` + fire-and-forget API + Sonner toast on resolve. The synchronous nav is right; the toast was only acknowledgement on resolve, which on a cold Vercel lambda is 500ms-3s away from the click. The user saw an instant route change but no other visible feedback in that window. v1.17.0 fires `toast.loading('Linking to {playerName}…')` SYNCHRONOUSLY (before the route push) and captures the returned id. When the API resolves, `notifyLinkOutcome(result, toast, id)` calls `toast.success(...)` / `toast.error(...)` with the same `{ id }` so Sonner replaces the loading toast IN-PLACE — spinner→checkmark/X transition, no flash, no stack. Mirror pattern for the Unassign path: `notifyUnlinkPending(toast)` + `notifyUnlinkOutcome(result, toast, id)`. **Plumbing:** `src/lib/assignToast.ts` adds `notifyLinkPending(playerName, toast)` and `notifyUnlinkPending(toast)` helpers; `notifyLinkOutcome` / `notifyUnlinkOutcome` accept an optional `id` parameter that's threaded into Sonner's `{ id }` opts (passing `undefined` preserves the pre-v1.17.0 behavior for non-loading callers). The `ToastApi` shape adds `loading: (msg) => ToastId` and the success/error signatures gain optional `opts?: { id?: ToastId }`. **Order in `assignSubmit.ts#performAssignSubmit`:** (1) `notifyLinkPending` synchronously → returns id. (2) `pushHome()` synchronously. (3) `await link(playerId)`. (4) `notifyLinkOutcome(result, toast, id)` replaces in-place. (5) Fire-and-forget `refreshSession()` on success. (6) `onError(error)` on failure. The new `playerName` parameter on `AssignSubmitDeps` is plumbed from `AssignPlayerClient.tsx`, which looks it up in the already-loaded `playersByTeam` props (no extra round-trip). **Tests:** new `tests/unit/assignSubmit.test.ts` case "fires toast.loading SYNCHRONOUSLY before pushHome (immediate feedback)" — pins the new contract via order-tracking with deferred-promise harness; a regression that moves toast.loading after pushHome (or inside the await chain) would fail. Existing `assignSubmit.test.ts` cases gain `'toast.loading'` to the order arrays + `{ id: 'toast-id' }` to the success/error assertions. New `assignToast.test.ts` cases: `notifyLinkPending` + `notifyUnlinkPending` shape (call args + return id) + 2 cases for `notifyLinkOutcome` / `notifyUnlinkOutcome` with `id` arg → asserts the `{ id }` opts thread through. 323 passed | 2 skipped (317 baseline + 6 new — 1 in assignSubmit, 5 across assignToast). Type-check clean. Minor bump (1.16.0 → 1.17.0) — UX behavior change. v1.16.0 — **Consolidate revalidation primitives behind `src/lib/revalidate.ts#revalidate({ domain, paths?, mode? })`.** Architectural decision C from the v1.11.x code review (user-approved). Pre-v1.16.0 the cache-invalidation primitives `revalidatePath`, `revalidateTag`, `updateTag` were spread across 30+ call sites in `app/admin/actions.ts`, `app/admin/leagues/actions.ts`, and `app/api/assign-player/route.ts` — each site reasoned about its own combo of tags and paths (`revalidatePublicData()` + `revalidatePath('/admin/x')`, or `_updateTag('settings')` + `revalidatePublicData()` + `revalidatePath('/admin')`, etc.). Inconsistencies across sites (forgotten cache busts, doubled busts, wrong tag set) only surfaced at the user-visible layer. v1.16.0 centralizes the policy: each domain has a fixed tag set, callers supply per-action paths, callers pick the mode. **Domain semantics:** `public` → `public-data` + `leagues` tags. `admin` → same tag set as public (admin writes always propagate to the public site) PLUS supplied `paths`. `settings` → `settings` + `public-data` + `leagues` tags PLUS paths. `all` → union of all three tag sets. **Mode semantics:** `action` (default) uses `updateTag(tag)` for read-your-own-writes inside server actions; `route` uses `revalidateTag(tag, { expire: 0 })` for route handlers (no RYOW guarantee — that's the route-handler-side reality). `paths` are bust via `revalidatePath` regardless of mode (callable from both contexts in Next 16). The previous `revalidatePublicData()` helper is replaced — every call site now uses `revalidate({ domain: 'public' })` or the more-specific admin/settings shape. The route handler in `/api/assign-player` (picture-mirror branch) uses `revalidate({ domain: 'public', mode: 'route' })`. **Standing rule (new entry in the autonomy block):** "Cache invalidation goes through `src/lib/revalidate.ts#revalidate({ domain })`. Direct `revalidateTag` / `revalidatePath` / `updateTag` calls outside that file are forbidden." **Lint guard:** new `tests/unit/revalidatePrimitivesGuard.test.ts` (3 cases — one per primitive symbol) greps `src/` for direct calls; comment-stripping removes false positives in docstrings. Failure surfaces the offending file paths so a regression is immediately actionable. **Tests:** new `tests/unit/revalidate.test.ts` (8 cases pinning the canonical helper's contract: domain dispatch for public/admin/settings/all + tag set + paths + mode dispatch action/route + paths-default-empty). Existing `adminLineActions.test.ts` and `adminWriteInversion.test.ts` updated for the new helper shape — `revalidatePublicDataMock + revalidatePathMock` collapse into `revalidateMock` asserting `{ domain: 'admin', paths: [...] }`. 317 passed | 2 skipped (306 baseline + 11 new — 8 contract + 3 lint guard). Zero direct `revalidatePath`/`revalidateTag`/`updateTag` calls outside `src/lib/revalidate.ts` confirmed by grep + lint guard. Minor bump (1.15.0 → 1.16.0) — architectural change to invalidation semantics. v1.15.0 — **Extract `MatchScoreEditor` from `ScheduleTab.tsx`.** Item 3 from the v1.11.x code-review's should-address tier. Pre-v1.15.0 the score-editing state machine + save logic lived twice in `ScheduleTab.tsx`: once in `MobileMatchRow` and once in `MatchSubrow` (mobile vs desktop variants of the admin schedule view). Both rows owned: `editingScore` / `homeScore` / `awayScore` `useState`, a local `saveScore` function, Enter/Escape/onBlur keyboard handlers, parse-int validation, the `updateMatch(match.id, leagueId, { homeScore, awayScore, status: 'COMPLETED' })` call shape, the success/failure toast. v1.15.0 extracts `<MatchScoreEditor match={match} leagueId={leagueId} variant="mobile" | "desktop" />` to a new file (`src/components/admin/MatchScoreEditor.tsx`) that owns the score state and the save flow; both rows render it. Variants differ only in the static class names applied to the inputs and the display surface (mobile uses `font-mono text-sm` with `px-2 py-1` hover; desktop uses `font-condensed font-bold text-base` for completed scores). Net LOC: −60 in `ScheduleTab.tsx`, +135 in `MatchScoreEditor.tsx`. The two `pending = useTransition()[0]` unused-variable warnings the original rows carried also drop out (the new component reuses the same shape but omits the unused destructure). **Tests:** new `tests/unit/matchScoreEditor.test.ts` (7 cases — extraction regression-prevention shape: asserts `setEditingScore`/`setHomeScore`/`setAwayScore`/`function saveScore` are gone from `ScheduleTab.tsx`, asserts `MatchScoreEditor` is imported and rendered with both variants, asserts the new component's `updateMatch(...status: 'COMPLETED')` + Enter/Escape/onBlur shape stays pinned). The behavior of the extracted component matches the v1.14.x rows byte-for-byte; render-parity testing with React Testing Library would need jsdom + RTL added to the project (deferred — the structural assertion gives equivalent regression coverage for the dedupe). Existing 299 tests pass through the refactor unchanged. Minor bump (1.14.0 → 1.15.0) — refactor that affects the rendered component tree but preserves admin-visible behavior. **Closes the v1.11.x code-review's should-address tier (items 1, 2, 3, 4, 5 all shipped across PRs α/β/γ).** v1.14.0 — **Drop ratings entirely + dedupe redundant league lookup in `lib/publicData.ts`.** Two items from the v1.11.x code-review's should-address tier. **(1) Ratings deletion (item 4).** The peer-rating feature ("rate other players post-match" + "matchday vibes" aggregate) is removed at every layer: the `PlayerRating` interface (drops from `src/types/index.ts`), the `ratings: PlayerRating[]` field on `LeagueData`, `parseRatings` + `RatingsRaw!A:BH` Sheets range fetch (drops from `src/lib/sheets.ts` + `src/lib/data.ts`), `computeMatchdayVibes`, `MatchdayVibes` interface, `computeTopRated`, `TopRated` interface, the `ratings: PlayerRating[]` parameter on `computePlayerStats`, and `avgRating` + `matchdaysRated` fields on `PlayerStats` (all from `src/lib/stats.ts`); the `MatchdayVibesSection` + `VibesBar` components and the `matchdayVibes` prop on `StatsDashboard` (from `src/components/StatsDashboard.tsx`); the `computeMatchdayVibes` call + `matchdayVibes` prop pass-through (from `src/app/stats/page.tsx`); the `ratings` field on `RawSheetData` + the `ratings: []` mock array (from `src/lib/sheets.ts` + `src/lib/mock-data.ts`); the `ratings: PlayerRating[]` return on `dbToPublicLeagueData` (from `src/lib/dbToPublicLeagueData.ts`); the `RatingsRaw` Sheets range fetch in both `scripts/sheetsToDbBackfill.ts` and `scripts/importFromSheets.ts`. The Sheets `RatingsRaw!A:BH` range was the heaviest of the seven legacy `batchGet` ranges (~all peer-rating columns); dropping it shrinks the cold-cache `getFromSheets` round-trip. **(2) Redundant league lookup dedupe (item 2).** `lib/publicData.ts` had two cached Prisma queries against the default league: `getFromDb` (full LeagueData blob) and `getDefaultLeagueGameWeeks` (just GW list for the RSVP merge bridge — Redis keys by `gameWeekId`, public matchday ids are `md<weekNumber>`). The two queries had identical TTL + tag set + ran twice on every dashboard render. v1.14.0 dedupes: `dbToPublicLeagueData` now returns `{ data: LeagueData, gameWeeks: GameWeekMeta[] }` — the GW metadata is co-cached with the static blob, sharing one Prisma round-trip. `getDefaultLeagueGameWeeks` is deleted; `getRsvpData` takes `gameWeeks` as an argument from the caller (`getPublicLeagueData`); `getPlayerByPublicId` updates to `(await getFromDb()).data.players` for the new shape. Per-render Prisma round-trip count drops from 2 → 1 on the warm `getPublicLeagueData` path. **Tests:** new `tests/unit/ratingsRemoved.test.ts` (9 cases, one per scrubbed symbol — `PlayerRating`, `MatchdayVibes`, `computeMatchdayVibes`, `computeTopRated`, `matchdayVibes`, `avgRating`, `matchdaysRated`, `parseRatings`, `RatingsRaw`); regression-prevention shape: greps `src/` and `scripts/` (not tests/, which contain the literal symbols as fixtures) and fails if any of them reappear. The 290 existing tests pass unchanged through the publicData restructure — the LeagueData consumer surface is preserved; the construction path internally took on a tuple. Minor bump (1.13.0 → 1.14.0) — feature deletion + structural cleanup. **Out of scope:** item 3 (extract MatchScoreEditor from ScheduleTab) ships as PR γ in the same chain. v1.13.0 — **Admin Redis pre-warm defers via `waitUntil`; `__seeded` sentinel re-assert collapses into a private `writeRsvpField` helper.** Two items from the v1.11.x code-review's "should-address" tier, both targeted at the Redis-store boundary. **(1) Admin `setMapping` defer.** Pre-v1.13.0 the admin server actions `adminLinkLineToPlayer` (`src/app/admin/leagues/actions.ts`), `updatePlayer`, and `createPlayer` (both in `src/app/admin/actions.ts`) awaited `setMapping(lineId, fresh)` on the response critical path — every admin link/update/create paid the Upstash REST round-trip before returning. v1.13.0 mirrors the v1.8.0 public-hot-path inversion: `setMapping` is wrapped via `waitUntil(setMapping(...).catch(structuredDriftLog))` so the admin response returns before the Redis write lands. Admin Prisma writes stay synchronous because admin pages re-read Prisma directly via `revalidatePath('/admin/...')` — only the Redis pre-warm defers. Drift on Redis failure surfaces as a `[v1.13.0 DRIFT] kind=playerMapping op={admin-link|admin-update|admin-create} lineId=... err=...` log line for operator grep + replay via `scripts/auditRedisVsPrisma.ts`. The deferred mapping is small (one Upstash SET) but admin throughput is bounded by it on every link click — under cold-Upstash-region conditions ~50–100ms warm, multi-second cold. New shared helper `deferSetMapping(op, lineId, mapping)` in each actions file. **(2) `__seeded=1` re-assert collapse.** Pre-v1.13.0 `setRsvp`, `setRsvpOrThrow`, and `setParticipated` each open-coded the same field-write pattern (HDEL on null + reassert sentinel via HSET, or HSET both sentinel + value on non-null, then EXPIREAT). Three sites with three try/catch wrappers maintaining the same five-line block. v1.13.0 collapses the field-write into a private `writeRsvpField(client, gameWeekId, gwStartDate, field, value)` helper that handles the sentinel + value + TTL math; callers retain their own try/catch policy (silent + console.warn for `setRsvp`/`setParticipated`, throw-through for `setRsvpOrThrow`). Per-write LOC reduction across the three call sites; no behavior change — the existing 31-test rsvpStore suite passes unchanged. **Tests:** new `tests/unit/adminWriteInversion.test.ts` (6 cases — adminLinkLineToPlayer / updatePlayer / createPlayer each pin: response returns BEFORE the deferred setMapping resolves via deferred-promise harness, drift log emits on rejection with the right `op` tag, no-op when no lineId is supplied). The regression target is "calls waitUntil rather than awaiting setMapping" — a regression to the pre-v1.13.0 `await setMapping(...)` order would fail the timing harness. Existing `adminLineActions.test.ts` continues to pass unchanged: `setMapping` is still invoked synchronously to obtain the deferred promise; the change is what we do with it. Minor bump (1.10.0 → 1.11.0) — new user-visible component. v1.10.0 — **Admin Players tab surfaces LINE display name / picture / ID per-player + per-row Unlink + Remap flows.** Pre-v1.10.0 the admin Players tab showed `Player.name` and team assignment but had no surface for the LINE-link state; the operator could see "is this player linked?" only by inspecting the `Player.lineId` column via the Prisma studio. v1.10.0 adds: (1) a new "LINE" column (desktop) / row strip (mobile) showing the LINE display picture, display name, and partial-obfuscated lineId for every linked player; (2) a per-row "Unlink" button (with `ConfirmDialog` confirmation) that calls the new `adminClearLineLink` server action — sets `Player.lineId = null` and invalidates the Redis mapping for the cleared lineId; (3) a per-row "Remap" button that opens an extended `AssignLineDialog` (now in `mode="remap"`) with the target player locked and the dropdown showing BOTH orphan and currently-linked-elsewhere LINE users — picking a linked-elsewhere user surfaces a "Heads up: this will unlink {OldPlayer}" warning before confirmation. **Schema no-op:** `Player.lineDisplayName` / `Player.linePictureUrl` are NOT added — the data lives on `LineLogin.name` / `LineLogin.pictureUrl`, populated upsert-on-login from the JWT callback (`lib/auth.ts#trackLineLogin`, PR 6). The admin-data fetch joins via `Player.lineId → LineLogin.lineId` in-memory after a parallel `prisma.lineLogin.findMany`. **Subtle correctness fix in `adminLinkLineToPlayer`:** when an admin remaps lineId X from player A onto player B (where B already had lineId Y), the existing v1.9.x code set up the new `X → B` mapping in Redis but left `Y → B` stale in Redis (it would only decay after the 24h sliding TTL). v1.10.0 reads the target player's prior lineId before the transaction and calls `deleteMapping(Y)` after the new write so Y is treated as orphan on its next JWT callback. Without this, a remap-then-relogin from Y's perspective would surface the stale player ID. **New helpers:** `src/lib/admin-data.ts#getAllLineLoginsWithLinkedPlayer` (full LineLogin list annotated with `linkedPlayer: { id, name } | null` for the remap dropdown); `src/app/admin/leagues/actions.ts#adminClearLineLink({ playerId, leagueId })` (idempotent — no-op when player already has `lineId=null`). `getLeaguePlayers` now returns a 4-tuple ending in `lineLoginsByLineId: Record<string, { name, pictureUrl, lastSeenAt }>` (was 3-tuple). **Tests:** new `tests/unit/adminLineActions.test.ts` (8 cases — clear-link clears Prisma + Redis, idempotent on already-unlinked + missing player, throws on empty playerId; remap with target's prior lineId calls `deleteMapping` for the prior, no-op when target was unlinked, no-op when remap is same lineId, transaction + revalidates fire). New `tests/unit/adminLineDataJoins.test.ts` (7 cases — `getLeaguePlayers` 4-tuple shape, `lineLoginsByLineId` keyed correctly + empty record + legacy positions preserved; `getAllLineLoginsWithLinkedPlayer` annotates linkedPlayer correctly + preserves Prisma findMany order + handles empty + handles defensive null lineId on Player). Minor bump (1.9.1 → 1.10.0) — new admin-visible fields + new admin actions. v1.9.1 — Operational + docs follow-up to v1.9.0 (PR 75): backfilled the PR 21 ledger row (merge `7a11b6d`, prod `https://t9l-website-lrwhiaopi-t9l-app.vercel.app`) + the PR 22 ledger row (merge `21af063`, prod `https://t9l-website-p5045wjz1-t9l-app.vercel.app`) into the per-PR snapshot ledger and added the v1.9.0 deploy entry to ops-events. v1.9.0 — **Canonical JST date/time helpers + admin schedule editor TZ-skew bug fix.** Centralizes every JST format/parse path in `src/lib/jst.ts` (formatJstDate / formatJstTime / formatJstDateTimeLocal / parseJstDateTimeLocal / formatJstFriendly / parseJstDateOnly / combineJstDateAndTime / jstIsoString). **Load-bearing bug fixed:** `src/app/admin/leagues/actions.ts#createMatch / updateMatch` parsed user-submitted `playedAt` / `endedAt` strings via bare `new Date(str)`; on Vercel (`process.env.TZ=UTC`) V8 interprets `"2026-04-16T14:30"` as UTC clock time, so an admin in JST who typed "14:30" had it stored as 14:30 UTC = 23:30 JST — a 9-hour skew on every match scheduled by any non-JST admin (and silently affecting JST admins because the form's `<input type="datetime-local">` then displayed back the UTC clock via `toISOString().slice(0, 16)`, masking the bug from the admin's own view). v1.9.0 routes parsing through `parseJstDateTimeLocal` (manual regex + `Date.UTC()` arithmetic — independent of host TZ) and rendering through `formatJstDateTimeLocal` (Asia/Tokyo via `Intl.DateTimeFormat`). Also migrates loose-TZ display call sites: `src/app/admin/page.tsx#formatShortDate`, `src/app/admin/leagues/[id]/layout.tsx#formatDate`, `src/components/admin/SettingsTab.tsx#fmtDate`, `src/components/admin/ScheduleTab.tsx#fmtDate/fmtTime/fmtDatetime`, `src/components/LeaguePublicView.tsx#fmt`, `src/components/MatchdayCard.tsx#formatMatchDate`, `src/components/MatchdayCountdown.tsx#toJSTDate`, `src/lib/dbToPublicLeagueData.ts#fmtDateJST/fmtTimeJST`, all server-action `new Date(string)` parses (createLeague / updateLeagueInfo / createGameWeek / updateGameWeek / updateLeague). Public dashboard date display was already JST-correct via the existing scattered helpers; this PR is a structural cleanup that puts every site behind one helper file with one set of conventions. **Tests:** new `tests/unit/jst.test.ts` (24 cases — round-trip parse/format, TZ-independence proof via explicit UTC ms assertions that would fail under the buggy `new Date(str)` path, the canonical "14:30 JST input → store → display = 14:30 JST output" regression test, edge cases at midnight rollover / year boundary / leap year, jstIsoString construction, parseJstDateOnly UTC-midnight contract). `tests/unit/dbAdapterHelpers.test.ts` lost the 6 `fmtDateJST/fmtTimeJST` cases (relocated to `jst.test.ts`). **Existing-rows-may-be-skewed risk acknowledged:** v1.9.0 stops the bleeding (new edits land correctly) but does NOT bulk-fix existing skewed `Match.playedAt` rows. Operator action: spot-check matches and re-save any that look wrong via the admin UI.
