Keep this table append-only; future PRs add a row. **Rollback target convention:** the tag in row N points to the commit *before PR (N+1) was merged* — i.e. it's where you'd reset main to undo PR (N+1).

**Neon branch hygiene rule.** Snapshots older than 5 PRs ago can be retired by the active session as needed to free Neon branch slots; the active per-PR snapshot is sufficient for forward rollback (Layer 1 git tag + Layer 2 Vercel deploy promotion still cover the older windows). Each retirement gets a one-line note in the ledger row of the snapshot being retired AND in the row of the PR that retired it.

### Operational events

One-shot ops on shared systems (Redis cleanup, Sheets edits, manual DB writes outside a migration) get a dated line here. No PR / no version bump for pure data-only events; record what was done so future sessions can audit.

## Domain migration runbook

If the apex domain ever migrates from `t9l.me` to a different domain, the following surfaces all need to be touched. Same shape as the [Backups & rollback runbook](#backups--rollback-runbook) above — each layer has a specific action; some can be done independently, others must be sequenced.

### Layer 1 — DNS

Update DNS at the domain registrar:
- Apex `A` (or `ALIAS`/`ANAME`) record pointing at Vercel (`76.76.21.21` for the IP-based config, or the canonical Vercel-managed CNAME).
- Wildcard `*.<newdomain>` `CNAME` pointing at Vercel so per-league subdomains resolve.
- Keep the old domain's DNS in place during cutover — Vercel can serve both simultaneously while traffic shifts.

### Layer 2 — Vercel project config

In the Vercel dashboard for the `t9l-website` project:
- Add the new domain (`<newdomain>`) and the wildcard (`*.<newdomain>`) under Settings → Domains.
- Verify the SSL certificate provisions for both (Let's Encrypt via Vercel auto-provisioning).
- Optionally set the new domain as the production redirect target so the old domain auto-redirects post-cutover.
- Remove the old domain only after Layer 3–8 are complete and validated.

### Layer 3 — `NEXTAUTH_URL` env var

Update on **prod AND preview** Vercel envs:
```
NEXTAUTH_URL=https://<newdomain>
```
This is the load-bearing var for [`getAuthCookieDomain()`](src/lib/auth.ts) — see Layer 5. NextAuth v4 also uses `NEXTAUTH_URL` to construct the OAuth callback URL.

Local dev (`.env.local`): leave as `http://localhost:3000` — the cookie helper falls through to host-only on localhost.

### Layer 4 — LINE OAuth callback URL

In the LINE Developer Console (channel for the T9L app):
- Add `https://<newdomain>/api/auth/callback/line` to the Callback URL allowlist.
- Keep the old `https://t9l.me/api/auth/callback/line` until Layer 8 (the cutover commit) ships and you've verified the new flow end-to-end.
- Remove the old callback URL only after the cutover is fully complete.

### Layer 5 — NextAuth cookie domain

Update [`src/lib/auth.ts#getAuthCookieDomain()`](src/lib/auth.ts) — flip the apex match from `t9l.me` to the new apex:
```diff
- if (host === "t9l.me" || host.endsWith(".t9l.me")) {
-   return ".t9l.me";
+ if (host === "<newdomain>" || host.endsWith(".<newdomain>")) {
+   return ".<newdomain>";
  }
```
Update the test in [`tests/unit/authCookieDomain.test.ts`](tests/unit/authCookieDomain.test.ts) to match. Bump `APP_VERSION`.

### Layer 6 — Hardcoded URL literals

Grep for the old domain across the entire repo:
```bash
grep -rn "t9l\.me" --include="*.ts" --include="*.tsx" --include="*.json" --include="*.md" .
```
Replace each occurrence with the new domain. Surfaces to check:
- `src/` — code (auth helpers, components that hardcode share URLs, etc.)
- `scripts/` — deploy/seed/backfill scripts
- `prisma/seed.ts` if any
- Tests (`tests/unit/**`, `tests/e2e/**`) — many tests reference `t9l.me` literally as fixtures
- `CLAUDE.md` (this file) — every occurrence of the domain name
- `README.md` (if it references the domain)
- `package.json` `homepage` / `repository` / `bugs` URLs
- `playwright.config.ts` `baseURL` default
- `next.config.{js,ts,mjs}` `images.domains` / `headers` if any

Note: `extractSubdomain` in `src/lib/getLeagueFromHost.ts` does not literally contain `t9l.me` — it's domain-agnostic and just splits on dots. But verify the `RESERVED_SUBDOMAIN_LABELS` set still applies (`dev`/`www`/`staging` are infrastructure labels that should remain reserved on any domain).

### Layer 7 — Other env vars referencing the domain

Audit for env vars that contain the old domain:
- `NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_URL` (if set — currently not used, but flag for the future)
- `NEXT_PUBLIC_BASE_URL` (same)
- Any Vercel-managed Preview-env URLs (these are auto-generated by Vercel, no action needed)
- `BLOB_READ_WRITE_TOKEN` and `KV_REST_API_URL` are domain-independent, no change needed.

### Layer 8 — Cache + session invalidation

Once the cutover code merges and prod is serving from the new domain:
- Players currently signed in via LINE OAuth will need to re-authenticate. The session JWT cookie was scoped to `.t9l.me`; on `.<newdomain>` it's a fresh cookie scope. Communicate this to operators / players ahead of the cutover.
- Optionally flush prod Upstash (`t9l:auth:map:*` namespace) — not strictly required since the mappings are domain-agnostic, but reasonable as a clean reset if the cutover is part of a broader infrastructure refresh.
- Neon `Player.lineId` rows are domain-agnostic — no action needed.
- The `googtrans` cookie (Google Translate, set by `LanguageToggle`) is host-scoped by default; users will need to re-pick their language preference on first visit to the new domain.

### Layer 9 — CLAUDE.md + multi-tenant-readiness.md

Update this file's references to the apex domain (Layer 6 grep should catch most of them, but double-check section headings, code comments, and example URLs).

If the migration is part of a broader product change, update the in-scope audit doc (e.g. `outputs/multi-tenant-readiness.md`) to reflect the new apex.

### Sequencing

Layers 1–4 are prep work and can land independently in any order. Layer 5 (cookie domain) is the load-bearing code change — ship it AS the cutover commit, with the corresponding `NEXTAUTH_URL` flip in the same Vercel deploy. Layers 6–9 are cleanup and can land before, during, or after the cutover.

The cutover sequence that minimizes downtime:
1. Layers 1–2 (DNS + Vercel domain attached, both old and new active).
2. Layer 4 (LINE OAuth callback added; old callback retained).
3. Layer 6 (code references updated, but Layer 5 cookie domain still on the old domain — deploy this).
4. Layer 5 + Layer 3 in the same commit + Vercel env update — this is the cutover.
5. Layer 8 — operator action: communicate re-auth, flush caches if desired.
6. Layer 4 — remove old LINE OAuth callback.
7. Layer 2 — remove old domain from Vercel.

## Sheets→DB migration

Multi-PR cutover replacing Google Sheets with Neon Postgres as the source of truth for the public site. Plan: `/tmp/sheets-to-db-migration-plan.md` (v2, post-review).

Status:

- **PR 1 — Schema additions** ✅ shipped (`87cc64f`, 2026-04-27). Strictly additive: `Player.position`, `Team.shortName/color`, `Venue.url/courtSize`, `Venue.name @unique`, `Match @@unique`, `Availability` model + enums, `Setting` model. Public site behavior unchanged.
- **PR 1.5 — Testing + autonomy + runbook** ✅ shipped (`7f32896`, 2026-04-27). Vitest, Playwright config, GitHub Actions CI, `.claude/settings.json` autonomy rules, runbook.
- **PR 2 — Backfill script + DB→public adapter** ✅ shipped (`6648654`, 2026-04-27). Live backfill ran clean against prod Neon: 4 teams + 53 players (41 with positions) + 8 game weeks + 24 matches + 67 availability rows. Goals preserved per `--no-overwrite-goals` default. Re-runs are idempotent (verified). Default `dataSource='sheets'` → public site behavior byte-equivalent to PR 1.5.
- **PR 3 — Toggle UI + RSVP dual-write** ✅ shipped (`e80cf44`, 2026-04-27). Re-enables Settings tab, adds Data source / Write mode radios + `setDataSource`/`setWriteMode` server actions. RSVP route rewritten per C4 (DB-first dual-write, fail-fast on DB error, log-and-continue on Sheets error in dual mode). `revalidatePublicData()` wired into all 21 admin server actions. `Setting` rows seeded.
- **PR 4 — Operational toggle flip** ✅ executed 2026-04-27 16:48 UTC. Operator drove the admin Settings UI on prod, flipped `dataSource` from `sheets` to `db`. Verified: Setting row updated (`dataSource=db`, `updatedAt: 2026-04-27T16:48:55.064Z`), apex began reading from DB within ~30s SWR cycle. **MD9 expanded smoke** ran end-to-end: created MD9 (`gw-minato-2025-9`, date 2026-08-01) + 2 matches (Mariners 2-1 Fenix completed; Hygge vs Torpedo scheduled) + 1 goal (Ian Noseda, assist Vernieri Luca) + 1 Availability row (Ian Noseda RSVP=GOING). Apex correctly rendered the new MD9 entry with score, goal mapping (scorer/assister names + scoring/conceding teams), JST kickoff/fullTime formatting (`19:05`/`19:40`), and availability status. Test data cleaned up post-verification; apex returned to MD1–MD8 only. **Cutover stayed in place — `dataSource='db'`**, `writeMode='dual'` (Sheets continues receiving RSVP writes as redundant store). Caveat: dual-write code path was unit-tested in PR 3 but not exercised end-to-end (no public RSVP submission via LINE OAuth in this run); first real RSVP post-flip is the live test.
- **PR 5 — Saving-stuck fix + APP_VERSION in LINE-user dropdown** ✅ shipped (`d02a2ef`, 2026-04-28). Patch release; no schema change. Two small public-site UI fixes bundled.
- **PR 6 — Admin assign-player Flow B + B1 Redis→Prisma migration + LineLogin model** ✅ shipped (`12f5cbf`, 2026-04-28). Adds `LineLogin` Prisma model populated from `lib/auth.ts` JWT callback. Public self-assign route (`api/assign-player/route.ts`) writes `Player.lineId` (atomic transaction with @unique-collision clear); legacy Redis `line-player-map` writes removed. `lib/auth.ts#getPlayerMapping` now reads Prisma first, falls back to Redis with a `[auth] DEPRECATED Redis hit` warn (deprecation window — remove in PR 7+ after soak with zero hits). New admin server action `adminLinkLineToPlayer` + `AssignLineDialog.tsx` modal in PlayersTab. `scripts/backfillRedisLineMap.ts` reads the legacy hash and upserts `Player.lineId` + `LineLogin`; idempotent, skips conflicts. Post-merge live backfill against prod: 34 scanned / 31 linked / 1 already / 1 conflict / 1 missing / 34 LineLogin rows.
- **PR 7 — Saving-stuck UX fix v2** ✅ shipped (`f50328b`, 2026-04-28). PR #50 (v1.1.2) added `router.refresh()` after `router.push()` but only addressed RSC cache staleness, not the perceived hang. Real root cause: the `submitting` flag spanned API write + next-auth `update()` + `router.push` + destination RSC re-render — under the post-cutover Prisma-on-every-JWT auth path that's 5–7 seconds. Fix: extract pure state-machine helpers in `src/lib/assignButtonLabel.ts`, introduce a separate `redirecting` flag that takes precedence; flip `submitting → redirecting` the moment the API write resolves. Button leaves "Saving…" within ~1s of API success regardless of how slow navigation is. Vitest pins the precedence rules; Playwright spec documents the local-dev manual repro.
- **PR 8 — Prisma-on-every-JWT perf fix** ✅ shipped (`96d4605`, 2026-04-28). New `src/lib/playerMappingCache.ts` (Upstash, 60s TTL, `t9l:auth:map:` namespace, null sentinel for unmapped IDs) wraps `lib/auth.ts#getPlayerMapping`. Cache is busted at every Prisma `Player.lineId` write site: `api/assign-player` POST + DELETE, `admin/actions.ts#updatePlayer` (invalidates both old and new), `admin/actions.ts#createPlayer`, `admin/leagues/actions.ts#adminLinkLineToPlayer`. Local A/B against the dev preview Neon branch (Tokyo→Singapore network, real Upstash, line-mock session): `/api/auth/session` median 264ms → 108ms, max 1369ms → 379ms — ~60% reduction at p50, ~72% at tail. Cold-Vercel-lambda magnitude (1–3s pre-fix) not reproducible locally; relative improvement is the directional signal. Vitest covers cache-hit, cache-miss, null sentinel, invalidate, Redis-unavailable, and Redis-error fall-through paths. **Caveat addressed by PR 9:** the cache was busted on every write, so the read inside `await update()` *immediately following* a write was unconditionally cold — i.e. exactly the post-assign latency users complained about post-v1.2.3.
- **PR 9 — Post-write pre-warm (closes the invalidate-then-cold hole)** ✅ shipped (`f9f2db3`, prod `https://t9l-website-q01pe7pnv-t9l-app.vercel.app`, 2026-04-28). Replaces `invalidate(lineId)` with `setCached(lineId, freshMapping)` at every `Player.lineId` write site: `api/assign-player` POST sets the post-write `{ playerId, playerName, teamId }` (slug-only, no `p-`/`t-` prefix); DELETE sets the null sentinel; `admin/leagues/actions.ts#adminLinkLineToPlayer` and `admin/actions.ts#createPlayer` fetch the post-write shape via the now-exported `lib/auth.ts#getPlayerMappingFromDb` helper for shape parity with the JWT callback; `admin/actions.ts#updatePlayer` keeps `invalidate` for the OLD lineId (deliberate — that user's mapping is now `null`-on-this-player and the conservative fall-through to Prisma is fine) and pre-warms the NEW lineId. The post-assign `await update()` on the client now hits cache and returns within the v1.2.3 warm-cache envelope (median 108ms / max 379ms in the v1.2.3 A/B) instead of cold-pathing to 1–3s. New regression-prevention tests in `tests/unit/assignPlayerCachePrewarm.test.ts` (POST → setCached with slug-only mapping; DELETE → setCached with null; neither calls invalidate) and a "post-write pre-warm contract" suite added to `tests/unit/playerMappingCache.test.ts`. Auth/perf section in CLAUDE.md updated with a "writes pre-warm, do NOT invalidate" sticky note.
- **PR 10 — Drop redundant `router.refresh()` + wrap navigation in `startTransition`** ✅ shipped (`9f063af`, prod `https://t9l-website-rm9wtk2pd-t9l-app.vercel.app`, 2026-04-28). First in a multi-PR push targeting cold-lambda perceived latency on assign-player. Removes the second RSC fetch that was firing after every assign/unassign because the API route already calls `revalidatePath('/') + revalidateTag('public-data', { expire: 0 })` server-side; Next propagates that to the client router cache on next navigation, making `router.refresh()` strictly redundant. Under cold-lambda steady-state that redundant fetch was a 1–3s critical-path round-trip. Navigation extracted to `src/lib/postAssignNavigate.ts`; Vitest pins the call shape (push exactly once with `'/'`, `refresh` never, both inside the transition callback) in `tests/unit/postAssignNavigate.test.ts`. Vercel preview build hit the documented Neon-Vercel race (`P1012` / `DATABASE_URL_UNPOOLED`); admin-merged per runbook because Unit + type-check was green. Prod deploy clean.
- **PR 11 — Drop awaited `update()` — fire-and-forget session refresh** ✅ shipped (`6d37ca1`, prod `https://t9l-website-36ub5hp2d-t9l-app.vercel.app`, 2026-04-28). Replaces `await update()` between API success and `postAssignNavigate` with a fire-and-forget call via the new `kickOffSessionRefresh` helper. Pre-fix the user's critical path serialized API write → `/api/auth/session` round-trip → navigation; under cold-lambda steady-state the `update()` request itself can spin up its own cold lambda for 1–3s, on top of the API write's cold start. Now the refresh runs in parallel with navigation. Brief stale-flash on slow refetches accepted (next-auth client-cache catches up within ~1s — affects `Dashboard` "Playing as" badge, RSVP bar, etc.). Helper at `src/lib/kickOffSessionRefresh.ts`; Vitest in `tests/unit/kickOffSessionRefresh.test.ts` pins three contracts: update called exactly once, helper returns synchronously without awaiting (regression target — re-introducing `await` fails the test), rejections swallowed via console.warn. Playwright timing tightened from 1000ms to 200ms (Definition of Done). Minor bump (1.2.7 → 1.3.0) — auth-flow semantics change. Vercel preview hit Neon-Vercel race; admin-merged per runbook (Unit + type-check green).
- **PR 12 — Move Vercel Blob upload off API critical path** ✅ shipped (`9d51ed9`, prod `https://t9l-website-co1k0pqzm-t9l-app.vercel.app`, 2026-04-28). Schedules the LINE-profile-picture mirror (LINE-CDN fetch + Blob `put` + Redis SET + `Player.pictureUrl` update) as background work via `waitUntil` from `@vercel/functions`. Pre-fix the entire chain ran serially in the route handler before responding — 200–500ms warm and meaningfully more cold per assign with a LINE picture. Now only the Prisma transaction (lineId) + cache pre-warm + revalidate are on the response path; pictures land out of band, with `revalidateTag('public-data', { expire: 0 })` inside the background task so the new URL appears on the next render instead of waiting up to 30s for `unstable_cache` to expire. Destination uses `PlayerAvatar`'s fallback chain (LINE CDN URL → static `/player_pics/{name}.png` → `default.png`) for the brief gap. Vitest in `tests/unit/assignPlayerBackgroundPic.test.ts` pins five contracts including a hang-test (response returns even when `put` never resolves — proves no `await`). New dep: `@vercel/functions ^3.4.4`. Patch bump (1.3.0 → 1.3.1) — perf optimization, no semantic change. Vercel preview hit Neon-Vercel race; admin-merged per runbook (Unit + type-check green).
- **PR 12.5 — Ledger backfill + cold/warm timing capture** ✅ shipped (TBD merge SHA, 2026-04-28). Docs-only follow-up. Backfills PR 12's merge SHA + prod URL. Captures unauthenticated cold/warm timings on apex (post-PR-12) for the rough cold-lambda budget — `/api/auth/session` 1.37s cold / 0.52s warm, `/` 1.82s cold / 0.99s warm, `/api/assign-player POST` (401) 1.89s cold / 0.51s warm. Each cold lambda spin-up is roughly a second of fixed cost; the perceived "5–7s" the user reported was the sum of multiple cold round-trips on the assign-player flow (API write → `update()` → push → refresh = 4 round-trips × ~1.5s cold). PRs 10/11/12 collectively remove two of those round-trips (refresh, awaited update) and 200–500ms of inline blob work, so the post-PR critical path under cold-most-of-the-time should be ~2–3s instead of ~5–7s. Patch bump (1.3.1 → 1.3.2).
- **PR 13 — Optimistic UI rewrite of assign-player** ✅ shipped (`29c0f55`, prod `https://t9l-website-7968i3pbl-t9l-app.vercel.app`, 2026-04-28). Replaces the auto-navigate-on-success pattern with `useOptimistic` + an inline success view rendered on `/assign-player`. The moment the user clicks Confirm, the form is replaced by "✓ You're linked to {Player Name}" with the team's color badge and a "Go to home →" button — *before* the API write resolves, fitting the <50ms perceived-instant DoD. Auto `router.push('/')` removed: the user pays the navigation cost on their schedule. The Go-home button awaits the in-flight API + next-auth `update()` if pressed before they settle (briefly shows "Finalizing…"), guaranteeing the destination renders with a fresh JWT — never with stale linkage data. On API failure, `useOptimistic` reverts the optimistic value to the committed value (`null`) at end-of-transition, and the error is surfaced with a "Wrong player? Undo" affordance on the success view; the user stays on `/assign-player` to retry. New helper `src/lib/optimisticLink.ts` owns the I/O boundary as the rollback gate (pure `attemptLink` / `attemptUnlink` returning `{ ok: true, ... } | { ok: false, error }`); component owns the optimistic state. Helpers `lib/postAssignNavigate.ts` and `lib/kickOffSessionRefresh.ts` (PRs 10/11) and their tests are deleted — the new flow no longer auto-navigates and the next-auth refresh is captured into a ref for Go-home to await rather than fire-and-forget. New unit tests in `tests/unit/optimisticLink.test.ts` (200 + 4xx-with-body + 4xx-no-body + network-throw + non-Error throw paths for both link/unlink). `tests/unit/assignButtonLabel.test.ts` updated for the simplified state machine (no `redirecting` state). Playwright spec replaced: success-view-visible-within-50ms-of-click DoD assertion (CI budget 150ms), plus a 2s-stall test that verifies Go-home awaits the pipeline before navigating. Minor bump (1.3.2 → 1.4.0) — UX behavior change (auto-redirect → inline success view).
- **PR 13.5 — Ledger backfill for PR 13** ✅ shipped (TBD merge SHA, 2026-04-28). Docs-only follow-up. Backfills PR 13's merge SHA (`29c0f55`) and prod URL (`https://t9l-website-7968i3pbl-t9l-app.vercel.app`) into the per-PR ledger and the PR 13 status entry. Patch bump (1.4.0 → 1.4.1).
- **PR 14 — Filter already-linked players from /assign-player picker** ✅ shipped (TBD merge SHA, 2026-04-28). Closes the false-success footgun introduced (well, exposed) by v1.4.0: pre-fix the picker rendered every roster row regardless of whether another LINE user already held that `Player.lineId`, so a user could pick a claimed player, the optimistic UI would flash success, then the API would 409 and the rollback path would fire. Unpleasant. Now `/assign-player` (server component) reads `Player.lineId IS NOT NULL` from Prisma at SSR time — `prisma.player.findMany({ where: { lineId: { not: null }, NOT: { lineId: viewerLineId } } })` — strips the `p-` prefix from each row's `id` to recover the public-side slug, and feeds the resulting `Set<string>` to a pure annotator (`annotatePlayersWithLinkedStatus`). The annotator returns the same group/team structure with each `Player` carrying a `linked: boolean` flag. The client renders linked rows as a non-clickable `<div>` (not a `<button>`) with a strikethrough name, "Already linked" tag, and 50% opacity — visible for roster transparency, but not selectable. The viewer's own slug is excluded from `linkedIds` server-side (the `NOT { lineId: viewerLineId }` clause), so the existing `isAlreadyAssigned` re-confirm/unassign UX still works. New helper `src/lib/linkedPlayers.ts` owns both the pure annotator (no I/O) and the Prisma fetch (returns empty set on Prisma failure — a stale "everyone selectable" picker is strictly less harmful than a 500). One extra Prisma query at SSR per `/assign-player` render, parallelized with `getPublicLeagueData()` and the session read via `Promise.all` — the page is `force-dynamic` and not on a hot path. Vitest in `tests/unit/linkedPlayers.test.ts` pins the annotator across seven cases (in-set, not-in-set, empty set, group/order preservation, full-field passthrough, immutability of input, viewer-exclusion seam — i.e. the helper itself does not know about viewers; that filtering is upstream in `getLinkedPlayerIds`). Playwright e2e (gated to localhost dev-login like the v1.4.0 specs) opens two browser contexts: A links a real player via the API; B (fresh cookie jar, distinct dev playerId seed → distinct lineId) opens `/assign-player` and asserts the linked row carries `data-linked="true"`, `aria-disabled="true"`, contains `Already linked`, and is rendered as a `<div>` not a `<button>`. Cleanup DELETEs A's link in `finally` so the dev DB returns to its prior state regardless of pass/fail. Source of truth = Prisma `Player.lineId` (the canonical post-PR-6 store; matches the API write site in `api/assign-player/route.ts`). Patch bump (1.4.1 → 1.4.2) — UX polish that closes a false-success path without changing the link contract or any persisted state.
- **PR 15 — Fix Illegal-invocation on link/unlink + hide linked players entirely** ✅ shipped (TBD merge SHA, 2026-04-28). Two user reports, both real, fixed in one PR.
   - **(1) `Failed to execute 'fetch' on 'Window': Illegal invocation`** on every link AND unassign click in the public site. Diagnosis: `AssignPlayerClient.tsx` was calling `attemptLink(id, { fetch })` and `attemptUnlink({ fetch })`, and the helpers in `src/lib/optimisticLink.ts` invoked `deps.fetch(...)` internally. That calls fetch as a *method of the plain `deps` object*. Browser fetch's WebIDL receiver brand check rejects any `this` that isn't a Window/Worker → "Illegal invocation". Vitest `vi.fn()` mocks have no brand check, so the existing 12-test optimisticLink suite passed cleanly while every real link/unlink in production threw. The user saw the v1.4.0 optimistic flip flash, then revert (because `attemptLink` returned `{ ok: false, error: "Illegal invocation" }` from the catch block). Fix: `deps` is now optional on both helpers; the no-deps path routes through a module-scope free-function wrapper `(input, init) => fetch(input, init)` which calls fetch as a global (the WebIDL realm-bound dispatch for the global call form — no `this` issues). Production callers in `AssignPlayerClient.tsx` drop `{ fetch }` from both call sites; the `{ fetch: spy }` injection seam stays for tests. New regression tests in `tests/unit/optimisticLink.test.ts` (3 cases) pin the no-deps→global-fetch contract via `vi.stubGlobal('fetch', ...)`. Caveat: vitest can't reproduce the brand-check throw (jsdom doesn't enforce it), so the unit test pins call SHAPE (where the call originates — global, not deps-property); the real-browser regression is caught by the Playwright spec.
   - **(2) Hide linked players entirely** instead of greying them out. PR 14 rendered linked rows as a non-clickable `<div>` with "Already linked" tag at 50% opacity for roster transparency; user prefers a clean picker. Filter moved from the client to the page in `src/app/assign-player/page.tsx`: `data.players.filter((p) => p.teamId === team.id && !linkedIds.has(p.id))`. The `annotatePlayersWithLinkedStatus` helper and `tests/unit/linkedPlayers.test.ts` (the PR 14 annotator suite) are deleted — `getLinkedPlayerIds` is the only export `linkedPlayers.ts` keeps. The client-side linked-row branch in `AssignPlayerClient.tsx` is deleted. Playwright spec tightened: instead of asserting `data-linked="true"` + `aria-disabled="true"` + "Already linked" tag, now asserts `getByTestId(linkedSlugRow).toHaveCount(0)` — i.e. the linked player is absent from the DOM. The viewer's own slug is still excluded from `linkedIds` server-side via `NOT { lineId: viewerLineId }` so they can re-confirm or unassign their own player.
   - Patch bump (1.4.2 → 1.4.3) — bug fixes, no contract change. Source of truth still Prisma `Player.lineId`.
- **PR 15.5 — Ledger backfill for PR 14 + PR 15** — Pending; will fill in both rows' merge SHA + prod URL post-merge in a single docs-only PR (PR 14's row was left TBD because the original PR 14.5 was closed in favor of folding the ledger work into PR 15.5 — see closed PR 65).
- **PR 16 — Redis-primary auth lookup (architectural inversion)** ✅ shipped (TBD merge SHA, 2026-04-28). Inverts the lineId→Player auth-path canonical store from Prisma to Redis. Pre-fix: every JWT callback that missed the 60s Upstash cache fell through to a Prisma `findUnique` with relation-include — under cold-Neon serverless that's a 1–3s round-trip on the request critical path. PRs 8/9/10/11/12 chipped at this incrementally (cache, post-write pre-warm, etc.); PR 16 just removes the fallback. Read path is now: store hit → return value, store miss → return null (orphan; pre-v1.5.0 fell through to Prisma, no more), store error → fall through to Prisma defensively (Upstash transient outage must NOT null every authenticated session for the duration of the blip; the fallback also pre-warms the store on success so the next request resolves directly). The `getMapping` return shape is a discriminated union `{ status: 'hit'|'miss'|'error' }` so the auth callback can distinguish the branches — pre-v1.5.0 collapsed miss/error into a single `undefined` return and the caller couldn't apply different policies. File renamed: `src/lib/playerMappingCache.ts` → `src/lib/playerMappingStore.ts`. Exports renamed: `getCached/setCached/invalidate` → `getMapping/setMapping/deleteMapping`. TTL extended from 60s to **24h sliding** — every read hit fires a fire-and-forget `expire(key, 24h)` so active users effectively never expire; long-inactive users (no auth refresh in 24h) → key expires → next access → orphan. The 24h window doubles as a self-healing safety net for write-path bugs (a forgotten `setMapping` decays within 24h instead of persisting indefinitely). Write sites keep their existing Prisma-first-then-Redis-pre-warm order — the framing changes (Redis canonical, Prisma durable backup) but the dual-write itself doesn't. Legacy `getPlayerMappingFromRedis` (line-player-map hash, PR 6 deprecation window) removed entirely — every LINE user was migrated to `Player.lineId` by the PR 6 backfill, the v1.5.0 store reads from a different namespace, and the fallback served no remaining purpose. The defensive `legacyRedisCleanup` HDEL calls in `api/assign-player` are kept so any residual entries decay to empty. New script `scripts/backfillRedisFromPrisma.ts` is the recovery procedure: bulk-reads `Player.lineId` rows, computes the canonical mapping via the same slug-stripping helper as the JWT path, and SETs each entry into Redis with the 24h TTL. Per-row decisions: CREATE (Redis missing) / MATCH (Redis = Prisma) / DRIFT-OVERWRITE (Redis ≠ Prisma; Prisma wins). `--dry-run` reports without writing; `--apply` actually writes. Pure decision helper `decideBackfillAction` unit-tested in `tests/unit/backfillRedisFromPrisma.test.ts` (8 cases: missing/match/drift/auto-parsed/null-sentinel/malformed-string/malformed-object/single-field-diff). The dry-run was run against prod Upstash BEFORE the code merged so the store is already populated when the no-fallback code lands — see operational events below for the count and any drift detected. Tests rewritten: `playerMappingCache.test.ts` → `playerMappingStore.test.ts` (24 tests covering tri-state get, sliding TTL fire-and-forget refresh, set/delete semantics, namespace isolation, Redis-not-configured fallthrough). New `getPlayerMapping.test.ts` (6 tests pinning the auth-side miss-vs-error policy via `__getPlayerMapping_for_testing` exported test seam). All write-site tests updated for the renamed exports. The `__getPlayerMapping_for_testing` export is unused in production — it's the test seam for `getPlayerMapping` (which is otherwise private). Minor bump (1.4.3 → 1.5.0) — architectural change to the auth path. User-facing behavior identical to v1.4.3 in steady state; the operational story (which store is canonical, what the recovery procedure is) is the substantive shift.
- **PR 17 — Auto-navigate + Sonner toast on /assign-player success** ✅ shipped (TBD merge SHA, 2026-04-28). Reverses the v1.4.0 inline-success-view UX: the user reported the explicit Go-home click as friction, not feedback. The new flow on success: API write resolves → `notifyLinkOutcome(result, toast)` → `router.push('/')`. The toast lives at the root layout (Sonner `<Toaster position="top-center" duration={4500} />` inside `app/layout.tsx`), persists across the route navigation, and auto-dismisses after ~4.5s. Error path: stay on `/assign-player`, fire `toast.error(...)` for retry — the inline `error` paragraph below the Confirm button is also kept for redundancy. New helper `src/lib/assignToast.ts` (pure, no I/O) is the toast-dispatch boundary — `notifyLinkOutcome` and `notifyUnlinkOutcome` take a discriminated-union result and a `ToastApi` shape (`{ success, error }`) and route to the right side with the right message; vitest in `tests/unit/assignToast.test.ts` pins 6 cases (success/error-with-message/error-empty-fallback for both link and unlink). Component changes in `src/components/AssignPlayerClient.tsx`: removed the inline success view entirely (the success branch + the `linkedView` JSX block); removed `useOptimistic` (no consumer left); removed `apiPromiseRef` / `updatePromiseRef` / `finalizing` state (the PR 13 await-the-pipeline machinery); removed the `LinkedState` type export from `optimisticLink.ts` (no consumers); removed `LinkAttemptResult` from the AssignPlayerClient imports (only the helpers need it now). The `submitting` flag still gates the Confirm button label via `assignButtonLabel` ("Saving…" between click and resolved API). Playwright spec rewritten: case 1 — click Confirm, assert URL is `/` within 5s + Sonner toast `role="status"` containing `Linked to {Player Name}` is visible within 2s + auto-dismisses within 8s; case 2 — stall the POST by 2s, assert the user stays on `/assign-player` with the Confirm button showing "Saving…" until the API resolves, then lands on `/` and the toast still fires post-navigation. The 50ms perceived-instant DoD from v1.4.0 is gone with the inline view — there's no more pre-API state to assert; the new latency story is "navigation completes when the API resolves, with the toast covering the gap." New dep: `sonner ^2.0.7` (installed via `npm install sonner`). Minor bump (1.5.0 → 1.6.0) — UX behavior change.
- **PR 18 — Fix v1.6.0 submit-stuck-on-saving + nav-tied-to-toast** ✅ shipped (TBD merge SHA, 2026-04-28). Two user-reported bugs in v1.6.0 (PR 17), both real, fixed together. **The bug:** v1.6.0's `handleConfirm` awaited `attemptLink(selectedPlayerId)` BEFORE firing `router.push('/')`. On a cold Vercel lambda the API write is 3–5s, so the user clicked Confirm, watched the button stuck on "Saving…" for 3–5s, and only saw the toast appear when the route finally changed — which the user described as "navigation tied to toast dismissal" because nothing visible happened until the toast did, leading them to dismiss it manually before realizing the page had already changed. **The fix:** new pure helper `src/lib/assignSubmit.ts` (`performAssignSubmit`) inverts the order — step 1 `pushHome()` SYNCHRONOUSLY (before any await), step 2 `await link(playerId)` runs in the background (the user has already navigated), step 3 `notifyLinkOutcome(result, toast)` (toast renders on the destination because Sonner's `<Toaster />` is mounted at the root layout), step 4 fire-and-forget `refreshSession()` on success (next-auth `update()`, swallows rejection with a console warn), step 5 `onError(err)` on failure (the component uses this to set the inline error text for the rare case where the user navigates back to `/assign-player`). The component (`AssignPlayerClient.tsx`) wraps `pushHome` in `startTransition(() => router.push('/'))` and passes `update` as `refreshSession`. **Error UX tradeoff:** the user is on `/` by the time a 5xx surfaces — they see the error toast and can navigate back to retry. PR 15 already filtered linked players server-side so 4xx (already-linked) is no longer a realistic path; the only failure is a server outage, which is rare. The brief stale-flash on `/` between optimistic-nav and `update()` resolution is the same accepted tradeoff as PR 11 / v1.3.0. **Tests:** new `tests/unit/assignSubmit.test.ts` (6 cases) is the regression target — the load-bearing case "calls pushHome BEFORE the link API resolves" uses a deferred-promise harness that drains microtasks between push and link-resolve, capturing call order in a string array; a regression to v1.6.0's await-then-push order would fail this test. Other cases pin: stalled-API-with-immediate-push, fire-and-forget-refreshSession (submit resolves while refreshSession is pending), refreshSession rejection swallowed with console.warn, onError fires on failure (with the right error string) and NOT on success. **Playwright tightened:** case 1's click→nav budget went from 5s to 1.5s (v1.6.0's 5s budget was too lax — it would have passed even on cold lambdas, which is exactly why this regression shipped); case 2 INVERTED — the 2s API stall now asserts the user lands on `/` BEFORE the stall ends (`waitForURL` with 1.5s timeout) and the toast appears post-navigation, vs. v1.6.0 which (incorrectly) asserted the user STAYED on `/assign-player` until the API resolved. Patch bump (1.6.0 → 1.6.1) — bug fix, no contract change. The `submitting` flag is still set on click, but it only gates the button label briefly until `startTransition` re-renders the new route; on the cold-lambda path the user is already on `/` while the await is in flight, so the label is invisible.
- **PR 19 — RSVP-on-Redis architectural inversion** ✅ shipped (`1dd31ed`, prod `https://t9l-website-lebtlidz2-t9l-app.vercel.app`, 2026-04-28). Inverts the RSVP read path from Prisma-via-`unstable_cache` to Redis-canonical. Pre-fix: `dbToPublicLeagueData` derived `availability`, `availabilityStatuses`, `played` from `Availability` rows included in the gameWeeks fetch; the whole LeagueData blob was wrapped in a 30s `unstable_cache`; every RSVP write had to bust `revalidateTag('public-data', { expire: 0 })` to surface, costing a full re-derivation per submission. v1.7.0 splits the read path: cached static reads keep the existing wrapper, live RSVP signals come from Redis at dispatch via `lib/publicData.ts#getRsvpData`, merged into the same `LeagueData` shape consumers expect. New file `src/lib/rsvpStore.ts` mirrors `playerMappingStore.ts` from v1.5.0: tri-state read result (`hit`/`miss`/`error`), per-write `setRsvp`/`setParticipated`, `seedGameWeek` for createGameWeek pre-warm, `deleteGameWeek` for delete cleanup, `RedisLike` injection seam for tests. Key shape `t9l:rsvp:gw:<gameWeekId>` — Redis HASH with `__seeded=1` sentinel + `<playerSlug>:rsvp` + `<playerSlug>:p` fields. Absolute TTL (EXPIREAT) at `max(gw.startDate, now()) + 90 days` — never sliding, since RSVP data has a natural lifetime tied to the matchday. Miss policy: fall through to Prisma + write back to Redis (cold-fill). Error policy: fall through to Prisma WITHOUT write-back (don't amplify Upstash blips into a write storm). New helper `src/lib/rsvpMerge.ts` owns the pure merge: `mapAvailability` (RsvpEntry → AvStatus, with v1.6.x precedence rules — PLAYED wins, NOT_GOING/empty drop) and `mergeRsvpData` (per-GW Redis maps → team-keyed availability/availabilityStatuses/played triplet). RSVP route `api/rsvp/route.ts` now writes Prisma + Redis in the same try block (failure of either propagates as 500 — partial-write states must not survive); drops `revalidateTag('public-data', { expire: 0 })` and `revalidatePath('/')` calls (RSVP no longer flows through the static cache). `dbToPublicLeagueData` no longer derives availability — drops `availability: true` from the gameWeeks include and returns empty objects for the three RSVP-derived fields. Sheets path (`getFromSheets`) is unchanged — still parses RSVP from RosterRaw cells, since the dataSource setting on prod is `'db'` and the Sheets path is legacy. Admin GameWeek lifecycle (`admin/leagues/actions.ts`): `createGameWeek` calls `seedGameWeek` after the Prisma create so future reads return hit-with-empty instead of miss-then-Prisma-fallthrough; `deleteGameWeek` calls `deleteGameWeekFromRedis` for cleanup. New script `scripts/backfillRedisRsvpFromPrisma.ts` is the recovery procedure: per-GameWeek CREATE/MATCH/DRIFT-OVERWRITE decisions with `--dry-run` mode; pure `decideBackfillAction` + `buildTargetFields` + `computeExpireAt` exported for unit testing. Cutover protocol: run `--dry-run` against prod Upstash BEFORE merging, surface output, run `--apply`, then merge. Tests: `tests/unit/rsvpStore.test.ts` (26 cases — tri-state read/seeded sentinel/TTL math/namespace isolation/RedisLike injection), `tests/unit/rsvpMerge.test.ts` (15 cases — mapAvailability precedence + merge correctness + defensive drops), `tests/unit/rsvpRouteIntegration.test.ts` (5 cases — Prisma + Redis dual-write contract, slug-not-prefixed-id passed to setRsvp, no `revalidateTag`, 500 on Prisma failure with no Redis side-effect), `tests/unit/backfillRedisRsvpFromPrisma.test.ts` (15 cases — buildTargetFields shape + decideBackfillAction CREATE/MATCH/DRIFT branches + computeExpireAt math). Existing `tests/unit/dbAdapterHelpers.test.ts` lost the 6 `mapAvailability` cases (relocated to `rsvpMerge.test.ts`). New Playwright spec `tests/e2e/rsvp.spec.ts` (gated to localhost + a pre-linked `E2E_LINE_ID` env) submits an RSVP via the API and asserts the new status renders within the architectural-payoff budget. Out of scope for v1.7.0: Sheets dual-write retirement (still fires Sheets writes in `dual` mode); admin-write of `participated` (no admin endpoint writes it today). Minor bump (1.6.1 → 1.7.0) — architectural change to the RSVP read path.
- **PR 20 — Redis-canonical write path (architectural inversion)** ✅ shipped (`42c6e75`, prod `https://t9l-website-e14dgxslu-t9l-app.vercel.app`, 2026-04-28). Inverts the public-write hot paths so Redis writes block the response and Prisma writes are deferred via `waitUntil`. Pre-fix: assign-player POST/DELETE awaited `prisma.$transaction` (~1–3s on cold Neon plus cold-lambda overhead) before responding; RSVP POST awaited `prisma.availability.upsert` similarly — that was the bulk of the 5s post-link / RSVP delay the user reported. v1.8.0 inverts: the canonical Redis write blocks the response (typically <100ms); Prisma transaction runs in `waitUntil` after the response returns. Affected sites: `src/app/api/assign-player/route.ts` POST + DELETE (Prisma transaction + legacyRedisCleanup deferred via `persistAssignmentToPrisma` / `persistUnassignmentToPrisma`), `src/app/api/rsvp/route.ts` POST (Prisma upsert + Sheets dual-write deferred via `persistRsvpToPrisma`). Skip-list (deliberate): admin write sites stay Prisma-first because admin pages re-read Prisma directly via `revalidatePath('/admin/...')` — deferring there would surface stale state on the admin's own next render. Hot-path savings are public-only. **Throwing-variant adds:** `src/lib/playerMappingStore.ts#setMappingOrThrow` and `src/lib/rsvpStore.ts#setRsvpOrThrow`. Identical write shape to the silent variants but propagate Redis errors instead of swallowing — required on v1.8.0 hot paths because a silent Redis failure with deferred Prisma would 200-OK with no durable write landing anywhere. No-client (KV env unset) stays silent in both variants — that's a dev/test condition, not a prod failure mode. **Race-window analysis (the load-bearing correctness check):** PR 15's `linkedPlayers` picker filter reads `Player.lineId` from Prisma. During the deferred-write window (~1–2s waitUntil settle) a second user can see a just-claimed player as available, click Confirm, and end up with a phantom Redis mapping that gets overwritten when their own deferred Prisma write lands. Their session keeps showing them as the wrong player until the 24h sliding TTL expires or they re-link. This race already existed pre-v1.8.0 (Prisma transaction window was ~50ms but non-zero); the window just widens. PR 15's filter has always been best-effort UX, not a correctness gate. Acceptable. **Drift recovery story:** two layers. (1) Inline structured logs `[v1.8.0 DRIFT] kind=playerMapping op=link lineId=%s ...` and `[v1.8.0 DRIFT] kind=rsvp gw=%s ...` emit per deferred-Prisma-failure; operators grep Vercel logs and replay manually. (2) New script `scripts/auditRedisVsPrisma.ts` is the inverse direction of the existing `backfillRedis<X>FromPrisma` scripts — scans Redis namespaces and reports state present in Redis but missing-or-differing in Prisma. `--dry-run` (default) reports a punch list across both domains; `--repair-prisma` writes the missing rows back to Prisma using Redis as truth. Two domains in one script (`--domain=playerMapping|rsvp|both`). Pure decision helpers `decidePlayerMappingAudit` and `decideRsvpAudit` are exported and unit-tested in `tests/unit/auditRedisVsPrisma.test.ts` (18 cases — match/redis-only/prisma-only/differing/malformed branches across both domains). Categories: MATCH, REDIS-ONLY (v1.8.0 drift; repaired), PRISMA-ONLY (read-side; Layer 5/5b territory, NOT repaired here), DIFFERING (Redis canonical wins on repair), MALFORMED (admin garbage, reported only). **Tests:** `tests/unit/assignPlayerWriteInversion.test.ts` (7 cases — call ordering via deferred-promise harness, response-before-Prisma timing, DRIFT log on Prisma rejection, 500 on Redis throw); `tests/unit/rsvpRouteWriteInversion.test.ts` (6 cases — same shape plus sheets-only mode keeps the synchronous Sheets-canonical path); `tests/unit/auditRedisVsPrisma.test.ts` (18 cases). Existing tests updated for the rename setMapping → setMappingOrThrow at the route layer: `tests/unit/assignPlayerCachePrewarm.test.ts`, `tests/unit/assignPlayerBackgroundPic.test.ts` (asserts waitUntil called twice — Prisma defer + pic mirror), `tests/unit/rsvpRouteIntegration.test.ts` (rewritten — Prisma upsert is now INSIDE the captured-and-replayed waitUntil callback, not awaited inline). Existing `tests/unit/playerMappingStore.test.ts` and `tests/unit/rsvpStore.test.ts` gain 4 cases each pinning the throwing-variant contract (writes succeed silently on no-client; throw on Redis errors). Playwright: `tests/e2e/assign-player.spec.ts` and `tests/e2e/rsvp.spec.ts` each gain a v1.8.0-specific direct-API timing test (warm POST budget <600ms — was 3–5s cold pre-v1.8.0). Minor bump (1.7.1 → 1.8.0) — architectural change to the write paths, parallel to v1.5.0 (auth) and v1.7.0 (RSVP) read-path inversions. Out of scope: admin actions stay Prisma-first; SETNX-style atomic claim for the link race is not added (existing race already accepted).
- **PR 21 — Drop public-data revalidation from `/api/assign-player` POST/DELETE + lighter `getPlayerByPublicId` validation read (v1.8.2)** ✅ shipped (TBD merge SHA, 2026-04-29). Two perf wins on the assign-player synchronous critical path. **(1) Public-data revalidation drop:** the v1.8.0 route called `revalidatePath('/') + revalidateTag('public-data', { expire: 0 })` on every link / unlink, which forced the next `/` render to re-derive the entire `LeagueData` blob from Prisma + the RSVP fanout. v1.8.1 perf measurement on a dev preview (line-mock auth, 5 fresh users) confirmed the bust is wasted work: API alone p50=897ms / p95=1039ms; full click→toast E2E p50=1900ms / p95=4911ms; **GET `/` immediately after a link was 1068ms vs 488ms baseline (~580ms penalty per link warm; multi-second cold)**. Audit confirmed `lineId`-derived data is NOT in the static cache: `dbToPublicLeagueData.ts` doesn't read `lineId`; `linkedPlayers.ts#getLinkedPlayerIds` is uncached and called directly from `/assign-player/page.tsx` (not through any `unstable_cache`); `data.ts`/`sheets.ts`/`stats.ts`/`publicData.ts` don't reference `lineId`. The link state lives in the JWT (refreshed via `next-auth#update()` on the client) and Redis (`playerMappingStore`, the canonical store consulted by the JWT callback's `getPlayerMapping`). Mirror of v1.7.0's same drop on `/api/rsvp` for the same reason. Picture-mirror `revalidateTag('public-data', { expire: 0 })` kept inline in `uploadAndPersistLinePic` because `Player.pictureUrl` IS in the static cache, but that runs in the deferred waitUntil callback (already off the response critical path; conditional on `linePictureUrl + BLOB_READ_WRITE_TOKEN`). **(2) Lighter player-validation read:** the v1.8.0 route called `await getPublicLeagueData()` to do `data.players.find((p) => p.id === playerId)`. `getPublicLeagueData` always runs `getRsvpData()` on the DB path — uncached, fans out 12+ parallel Upstash HGETALLs across all default-league GameWeeks. Load-bearing for dashboard renders; pure overhead for write-path validation. v1.8.2 routes the validation through `lib/publicData.ts#getPlayerByPublicId(publicPlayerId)` that calls the cached `getFromDb()` / `getFromSheets()` directly and returns `{ id, name, teamId } | null` from the in-memory `players` array — no RSVP fanout. **CLAUDE.md addition:** new principle 11 in the State-based-data-on-Redis pattern: writes to Redis-canonical state should NOT invalidate the static `public-data` cache; cache invalidation is for static-data writes only (Team/Player/Match/Goal/Venue admin actions, picture-mirror Blob URL updates). Audit before adding `revalidateTag('public-data')` to any new write site: if the field being written is reachable from `dbToPublicLeagueData` / the `getFromDb` Prisma include, the bust is correct; if not, drop it. **Tests:** 4 new cases in `tests/unit/assignPlayerWriteInversion.test.ts` (POST does not call `revalidatePath`; POST does not call `revalidateTag` on the synchronous response path — picture-mirror revalidate is gated by `linePictureUrl + BLOB_READ_WRITE_TOKEN` which the default fixture omits; DELETE does not call either; route uses `getPlayerByPublicId('test-player')`, not `getPublicLeagueData`). `tests/unit/assignPlayerCachePrewarm.test.ts` and `tests/unit/assignPlayerBackgroundPic.test.ts` updated for the renamed mock (`getPublicLeagueData` → `getPlayerByPublicId`). Patch bump (1.8.1 → 1.8.2) — perf optimization on existing contracts; no new feature, no breaking change.

- **PR 37 — Match time picker is time-only + new-match defaults stagger (v1.21.1)** ✅ shipped (TBD merge SHA, 2026-04-30). Patch follow-up to v1.21.0 — closes the v1.20 audit's two bigger-lift items on the "Add Match" affordance: (1) `playedAt` defaulted to GW.startDate at midnight forcing admins to edit time on every add; (2) the kickoff editor was a `datetime-local` picker even though the date is implicit from the parent matchday. v1.21.1 swaps the match-row pill to `variant="time"`, threads `gwStartDate: Date` into MatchCardRow, and constructs the full datetime by combining the picked HH:MM with the matchday's date via `${fmtDate(gwStartDate)}T${val}` — server-side `parseJstDateTimeLocal` then handles the JST-instant interpretation per the v1.9.0 helpers. New helper `src/lib/scheduleStagger.ts#defaultMatchKickoffTime(idx)` returns the JST stagger time for the Nth match of a matchday (idx 0 → 19:05, idx 1 → 19:40, idx 2 → 20:15; clamps to last value beyond standard 3-match T9L matchday format). - **PR 38 — Multi-tenant prep α (RSVP route league context fix)** ✅ shipped (TBD merge SHA, 2026-04-30). First in a three-PR multi-tenant readiness chain (α/β/γ). Pre-fix the RSVP route hardcoded `LEAGUE_ID = 'l-minato-2025'`, mis-routing any subdomain RSVP to the default league's GameWeeks. v1.22.0 introduces `src/lib/getLeagueFromHost.ts#getLeagueIdFromRequest()` which reads the Host header and resolves to a `League.id` via `unstable_cache`-wrapped Prisma reads (60s TTL, `leagues` tag). Three branches: subdomain matches → that League's id; apex / dev base / localhost / Vercel preview → default league id; subdomain present but unknown → null. RSVP route POST awaits the helper, returns 404 on null, threads the resolved id into `gameWeek.findUnique`. - **PR 39 — Multi-tenant prep β (parameterize public data fetcher)** ✅ shipped (TBD merge SHA, 2026-04-30). Second in the multi-tenant readiness chain. Pre-v1.23.0 every public read path was implicitly default-league-only via `prisma.league.findFirst({ where: { isDefault: true } })` inside `dbToPublicLeagueData()`. v1.23.0 parameterizes the entire stack: `dbToPublicLeagueData(leagueId?)` flips its where-clause based on whether the arg is supplied; `getPublicLeagueData(leagueId?)` and `getPlayerByPublicId(slug, leagueId?)` thread through; `getFromDb` (the `unstable_cache`-wrapped function) accepts `leagueId?: string` so per-league entries are isolated by Next's parameter-based cache key. All four public read consumers (`app/page.tsx`, `app/schedule/page.tsx`, `app/stats/page.tsx`, `app/assign-player/page.tsx`) and the `/api/assign-player` POST route now resolve leagueId via the v1.22.0 `getLeagueIdFromRequest()` helper and pass it through. Subdomain hosts now render their league's data, not the default league's. Out of scope: `LeaguePublicView` (already league-scoped via `getLeagueBySubdomain`); per-league cache-bust tags (deferred — `unstable_cache` requires static tags). **Tests:** new `tests/unit/publicDataLeagueScope.test.ts` (9 cases pinning the where-clause flip, the no-silent-fallback contract for explicit-but-missing leagueIds, and the dispatcher pass-through at all three function layers). Existing `assignPlayerWriteInversion.test.ts` gains 2 cases for the route's leagueId thread-through and 404-on-null path. 465 passed | 2 skipped. Type-check clean. Minor bump (1.22.0 → 1.23.0) — backwards-compatible parameterization (omitted arg preserves prior behavior).
- **PR 40 — Multi-tenant prep γ (cross-subdomain JWT cookie + Domain migration runbook)** ✅ shipped (TBD merge SHA, 2026-04-30). Third and final in the multi-tenant readiness chain (α/β/γ). Pre-fix the NextAuth session cookie was host-only — a JWT issued at apex would not be sent to `*.t9l.me` subdomains. v1.24.0 adds `getAuthCookieDomain()` which parses `NEXTAUTH_URL` and returns `.t9l.me` for any t9l.me-family host (apex, prod sub, dev base, nested dev sub), `undefined` for localhost / Vercel preview / missing-or-malformed env. The `authOptions.cookies` config sets the `domain` attribute on `sessionToken` and `callbackUrl`; `csrfToken` keeps its host-only `__Host-` prefix per spec. No user-visible behavior change on the current single-domain deploy — cookie scope is a strict superset of host-only. New top-level CLAUDE.md section "Domain migration runbook" documents the 9 layers an apex-domain migration would touch (DNS, Vercel, NEXTAUTH_URL, LINE OAuth callback, cookie scope code, hardcoded URLs, NEXT_PUBLIC envs, cache/session invalidation, doc updates) plus a recommended sequencing. The `outputs/multi-tenant-readiness.md` audit doc updated to reference the new section. **Tests:** new `tests/unit/authCookieDomain.test.ts` (11 cases — all branches plus two security-defensive cases pinning suffix-vs-substring distinction). 476 passed | 2 skipped (465 baseline + 11 new). Type-check clean. Minor bump (1.23.0 → 1.24.0). **Closes the multi-tenant readiness chain.**
- **PR 41 — Renderer convergence: apex + subdomain merged onto unified `Dashboard` (v1.25.0)** ✅ shipped (`29b562e`, 2026-04-30). First of two multi-tenant launch PRs (α / β). Pre-v1.25.0 the public landing path branched at `app/page.tsx`: apex (`t9l.me`) → `Dashboard`, subdomain (`tamachi.t9l.me` etc.) → `LeaguePublicView` — a stripped-down 3-tab schedule/standings/teams view with no RSVP, no next-matchday banner, no logged-in-user affordances. v1.25.0 deletes [`src/components/LeaguePublicView.tsx`](src/components/LeaguePublicView.tsx) and routes both apex and subdomain through `Dashboard`, fed by the v1.23.0 parameterized `getPublicLeagueData(leagueId?)`. Routing delegated to `getLeagueIdFromRequest()`: apex / dev base / localhost / Vercel preview → default league id; known subdomain → that league's id; unknown subdomain → `null` → renders an explicit "League not found" surface. Subdomain users now get NextMatchdayBanner + MatchdayAvailability + RsvpBar + UserTeamBadge + GuestLoginBanner on the home tab; their `/schedule` and `/stats` sub-routes were already subdomain-aware as of v1.23.0. **Cleanup:** deleted `getLeagueBySubdomain` in [`src/lib/admin-data.ts`](src/lib/admin-data.ts) (zero remaining callers) and the legacy `getLeagueFromHost` function in [`src/lib/getLeagueFromHost.ts`](src/lib/getLeagueFromHost.ts) (full-League fetch — only caller was the page-level subdomain branch; the file keeps its name and still hosts `getLeagueIdFromRequest` + `extractSubdomain`). **Cross-league session safety:** existing render-null branches in `Dashboard` already handle a session whose `teamId` references a team not in the rendered league's roster — `pickUserTeam` returns `null` → UserTeamBadge hides; `userTeamIsPlaying` flips false → RsvpBar hides; the `availabilityStatuses?.[md.id]?.[userTeamId]?.[userPlayerId]` lookup with a stale teamId returns undefined → no spurious wrong-league badge. v1.26.0 (PR β) makes the JWT league-aware so the per-league teamId is deterministic when a player belongs to multiple leagues simultaneously. **Tests:** new `tests/unit/rendererConvergence.test.ts` (13 cases pinning import shape, deletion, leagueId thread-through, and the unknown-subdomain branch). 490 passed | 2 skipped. Type-check clean. Minor bump (1.24.0 → 1.25.0).
- **PR 42 — JWT league context: per-league `playerId`/`teamId` resolution + per-league Redis keys (v1.26.0)** ✅ shipped (TBD merge SHA, 2026-05-01). Second of two multi-tenant launch PRs (α / β). Pre-v1.26.0 the JWT was league-blind: a single LINE user mapped to a single `{ playerId, teamId }` regardless of host, and the Redis cache used a single key per LINE user (`t9l:auth:map:<lineId>`). With multi-tenant a player can be assigned to different teams in different leagues; v1.26.0 makes the resolution deterministic per host. **Resolution path:** the JWT `jwt()` callback in [`src/lib/auth.ts`](src/lib/auth.ts) lazy-imports `getLeagueIdFromRequest()` (v1.22.0) on every callback and threads the resolved leagueId into `getPlayerMapping(lineId, leagueId)`. Recomputes on every callback (regression target — pre-v1.26.0 a one-shot resolution at sign-in would persist the wrong league across subdomain navigation). **Per-league Redis keys:** [`src/lib/playerMappingStore.ts`](src/lib/playerMappingStore.ts) namespace flips from `t9l:auth:map:<lineId>` to `t9l:auth:map:<leagueId>:<lineId>`. The `getMapping`/`setMapping`/`setMappingOrThrow` signatures gain a required `leagueId` parameter. `deleteMapping` is overloaded: `(lineId, leagueId)` DELs the single per-league key; `(lineId)` SCANs the namespace and DELs every match (used by admin paths that don't operate within a single league). **Miss policy flip:** with per-league keys a miss is ambiguous (cold cache vs genuine orphan), so the read path falls through to Prisma + writes back. Mirror of v1.7.0's RSVP store policy. Error policy unchanged: Prisma fallback without write-back. **`getPlayerMappingFromDb(lineId, leagueId?)`** picks the per-league assignment when leagueId is supplied; falls back to teamId="" when the player is global but has no roster slot in this league. **Public hot path writes** (`/api/assign-player` POST/DELETE) thread leagueId into `setMappingOrThrow`. **Admin write paths**: `adminLinkLineToPlayer` (single league context) does per-league pre-warm; `adminClearLineLink` does per-league DEL; `updatePlayer`/`createPlayer` (no single league) do invalidate-all via SCAN-and-DEL and rely on lazy-fill on next read. **session.leagueId / token.leagueId** added to next-auth type augmentation. **Tests:** rewritten `tests/unit/playerMappingStore.test.ts` (35 cases) + `tests/unit/getPlayerMapping.test.ts` (10 cases) + new `tests/unit/getPlayerMappingFromDb.test.ts` (8 cases) + new `tests/unit/jwtLeagueContext.test.ts` (9 cases) + rewritten `tests/unit/adminWriteInversion.test.ts` (6 cases) + updates to `adminLineActions` / `assignPlayerCachePrewarm` / `assignPlayerWriteInversion` for the new signatures. 520 passed | 2 skipped. Type-check clean. **Old `t9l:auth:map:<lineId>` keys decay over the 24h sliding TTL post-deploy** — no migration required. Minor bump (1.25.0 → 1.26.0). **Closes the multi-tenant launch chain.** What's left for the actual multi-tenant launch is operator-side: (1) admin UX for attaching subdomains to leagues, (2) per-subdomain DNS provisioning runbook, (3) production cutover runbook for the first non-default-league subdomain.
- **PR 41+ — Retire Sheets path + write-mode flip** — Pending; only after weeks of confidence operating on `dataSource='db'`. Will switch `writeMode` to `'db-only'` and delete the legacy Sheets reads. (PR 16 already retired the legacy Redis line-player-map fallback; PR 19 made Redis canonical for RSVP reads; PR 20 made Redis canonical for public writes too. The remaining Sheets dependency is the legacy parser path used when `dataSource='sheets'`.)

### How to run the backfill

\`\`\`bash
# Pull production env (or per-branch preview env via vercel env pull)
vercel env pull .env.production --environment=production --yes

# Source DB connection vars
grep -E '^(DATABASE_URL|DATABASE_URL_UNPOOLED|GOOGLE_)' .env.production > /tmp/bf.env
set -a; source /tmp/bf.env; set +a; rm /tmp/bf.env

# Always preview first
npx ts-node --project tsconfig.scripts.json scripts/sheetsToDbBackfill.ts --dry-run --verbose-diff

# Then run for real (defaults are safe: no goal overwrites, availability merge mode optional)
npx ts-node --project tsconfig.scripts.json scripts/sheetsToDbBackfill.ts

# To recreate goals (destructive — only if Sheets is the trusted source AND you've staged a Neon snapshot):
npx ts-node --project tsconfig.scripts.json scripts/sheetsToDbBackfill.ts --allow-overwrite-goals

# To preserve in-flight RSVPs during the dual-write window (PR 3+):
npx ts-node --project tsconfig.scripts.json scripts/sheetsToDbBackfill.ts --availability-merge
\`\`\`

### Redis → Prisma backfill (PR 6, archived in v1.12)

The PR 6 one-shot migration that populated `Player.lineId` and `LineLogin` from the legacy Redis `line-player-map` hash completed successfully on 2026-04-28 (34 scanned / 31 linked / 1 conflict / 1 missing / 34 LineLogin rows). The script was archived to [`scripts/_archive/backfillRedisLineMap.ts`](scripts/_archive/backfillRedisLineMap.ts) in v1.12 because the legacy hash is no longer read anywhere — the v1.5.0 (PR 16) inversion routes auth lookups through a different namespace (`t9l:auth:map:`). The archived copy stays in-tree as historical record only; the unit test that pinned `decideLink` is preserved at [`tests/_archive/backfillRedisLineMap.test.ts`](tests/_archive/backfillRedisLineMap.test.ts) but excluded from the Vitest run.

## Known infra issues

### Neon-Vercel preview env race

**Symptom:** Vercel preview build fails on the first deploy of a new PR branch with:

\`\`\`
Error code: P1012
error: Environment variable not found: DATABASE_URL_UNPOOLED.
prisma/schema.prisma:8 — directUrl = env("DATABASE_URL_UNPOOLED")
\`\`\`

The Vercel build runs `prisma migrate deploy` immediately on push, but the Neon-Vercel marketplace integration's per-branch DB provisioning (which injects `DATABASE_URL` + `DATABASE_URL_UNPOOLED` for the new git branch) hasn't completed yet. Build dies in ~6 seconds.

**Hit on PRs 43, 47, 48** so far. Pattern: small change → fast push → first build wins the race against the integration. Larger PRs (PR 44, 45, 46) provisioned in time and built clean.

**Workaround in use:** if `Unit + type-check` is green on the PR (i.e. the change itself isn't broken — only the env wiring is missing), admin-merge via `gh pr merge <num> --admin --merge`. The merge to main triggers a prod deploy that uses the production Neon env (always provisioned), so prod always builds clean. We've done this on PR 47 and 48; the autonomy rule is otherwise strict on Vercel green.

**Proposed fix (future session):**
1. Investigate the Neon-Vercel integration provisioning latency. The integration may have a "pre-provision on PR open" setting we're missing.
2. Alternative: set `DATABASE_URL_UNPOOLED` as a non-Neon-managed branch-scoped env var (mirror prod's value) so new branches inherit it from a project-default instead of waiting on the integration. This re-introduces the prod-creds-on-preview risk we removed earlier — would need careful scoping (e.g. only point at a shadow/dev Neon DB, not prod).
3. Alternative: drop `prisma migrate deploy` from `npm run build` and run it as a separate Vercel build step gated on env-var presence. Decouples the build from migrations for branches that don't need DB access.

Tracked as a chore for the next session; not load-bearing on the migration work shipped through v1.1.1.

### Neon free-tier branch limit

Project `young-lake-57212861` is capped at **10 concurrent Neon branches** (free-tier limit). When `neonctl branches create` returns `branches limit exceeded`, the active session is blocked from cutting a new pre-PR snapshot.

**When this hits:**
- **Additive-only PRs** (e.g. PR 6's new `LineLogin` table — no alters to existing rows/columns) **may proceed without a Layer-3 snapshot**, with an explicit "Snapshot not taken" note in the ledger row including the rollback recipe (typically `DROP TABLE "X"` + code revert). Layers 1–2 (git tag + Vercel deploy promotion) still apply.
- **Non-additive PRs** (column drops, type changes, data migrations, anything that mutates existing rows) **must wait for cleanup** before merging — invoke the Neon branch hygiene rule above to retire an older snapshot, then cut the pre-PR branch normally.

Hit on PR 6 (auto session — couldn't prune because `Bash(neonctl branches delete*)` is denied in `.claude/settings.json` and the user wasn't at the terminal). PR 6 was additive-only so it proceeded without the snapshot; pre-pr-2-backfill is queued for retirement next session.
